Vandalieu had deliberately created a hole in the barrier for his diversion tactic, and prepared traps behind that hole. There was no way he would leave a city that was so important to him behind those traps.

He was capable of moving the mountain range, so it was certainly possible that he was capable of moving a city. There was nothing that Vandalieu deemed worth protecting at the end of this road.

And so, Heinz continued waiting for Vandalieu’s arrival.

+++

## **390 : The countless hands that pray because of a shortage of hands**

“Hmm? I’m in… the sky?” a certain god murmured in confusion as he suddenly regained consciousness, noticing that there were clouds floating below him.

The last thing he remembered was being on the ground, so why was he now so high up that he could look down upon a sea of clouds? He couldn’t remember at all.

He was Wisewarn, the God of Concealment. He was a subordinate god of Zuruwarn, the God of Space and Creation, and he ruled over concealment… places that were concealed.

He possessed the head of a cat, the wings of an owl, the torso of a gecko and a long tail like that of a snake. It was a bizarre form befitting a subordinate god of Zuruwarn, who took the form of a four-headed lion.

But he was unmistakably a god of Lambda, and he had joined Vida’s faction as Zuruwarn had instructed him to before Zuruwarn entered his long slumber.

During the battle against the Demon King’s army, he aided the champions’ army greatly by allowing them to use his concealed chambers and passageways. However, in the battle against Alda that followed, the enemy knew his methods. Light-attribute gods saw through his concealment and sealed him away when he tried to flee.

“That’s right, I should be sealed away. So why am I in the sky? Why has my seal been undone?”

If he had been rescued from his seal, then why was he so far from the ground, where he had been sealed away? And where was the one who had removed the seal? He couldn’t think of any possible answers to these questions. However, he couldn’t afford to take his time to ponder them, either.

Despite the altitude, Wisewarn was in a state where he had descended upon the mortal world. Even now, he was expending energy just to exist here.

But where was he supposed to go?

Based on the last events I remember, I must have been imprisoned by Alda or his servants. So I must be here because my seal was undone for some reason. With that being the case, it would be suicide to return to the Divine Realm of the one who was in possession of my seal… Alda’s forces.

But on the ground, I can feel Guduranis’s presence in several places for some reason… Could it be that the seals on Guduranis were removed as well, rather than just ours?

Wisewarn and the other gods did not possess a radar that allowed them to sense the accurate locations of other gods or evil gods belonging to the Demon King’s army. Thus, it was impossible to learn the location of a hiding god who had erased their presence without finding them. That was why Zakkart and the other creation-oriented champions had failed to notice Guduranis himself being present among the monsters approaching them when they were killed a hundred thousand years ago.

That was also the reason the remnants of the Demon King’s army had managed to remain in hiding until Alda and Bellwood found them.

But the senses of gods were not so dull that they could not notice the flow of large quantities of Mana.

Alda had embedded fragments of Guduranis’s soul in gods of Vida’s faction and evil gods from the Demon King’s army, then forced them to descend upon the mortal world. They were expending tremendous quantities of energy, and they were also in a berserk state, screaming and rampaging.

Since they were making such a conspicuous uproar, it was impossible for a god to not notice their presence unless they were in a similar state of madness themselves.

“This presence is… The presence of Zantark-sama and some others has vanished. Farmaun’s presence has vanished too… Did Lafaz defeat him? Vida-sama’s presence is… It feels like it is coming through a person, but I can still feel it. It’s also far away from the great presence that is similar to Guduranis’s. I suppose I will head there first to gain an understanding of the situation.”

Wisewarn decided to distance himself from the great Guduranis-like presence (Vandalieu) and hurried towards Vida’s presence – unaware that someone had removed the fragment of Guduranis’s soul from him.

In Nineland, the capital of the Hartner Duchy, a fierce three-way battle between gods was taking place.

Six years ago, Nineland had suffered a tragedy with the castle tipping on an angle and treasures being taken from its treasure chambers, but in more recent years, it had been recovering.

However, when they saw an enormous being that transcended human knowledge appear in the sky, many instinctively sensed that even that was coming to an end.

It was Gidragdra, the Evil God of Mad Slaughter, one of the commanders of the Demon King’s army. He had the form of a crustacean with countless legs that had pincers or claws at their tips.

He let out a maddened roar. “A nest of inferior life forms! First, I shall slaughter every living thing in this area! And I shall begin with you!”

He attacked the bizarre-looking god that had appeared next to him – one that, upon first glance, appeared to be an ordinary cloud other than its sinister shape. But as Gidragdra’s attacks struck him, he let out strange, ghost-like noises and revealed his true form.

He changed his entire shape other than his enormous mouth so that the rest of his body was nothing but countless tentacles, and he was still made entirely of gray, nearly-black clouds. This was Basbalulu, the Evil God of Abandoned Clouds and Demon Rain. He seemed to be criticizing Gidragdra for attacking him despite them both belonging to the Demon King’s army.

“What?! Do you really think I need a reason to kill you?! Am I not allowed to kill my allies without a reason?! The Demon King’s army needs no such weak fools! So I am not even killing an ally!” Gidragdra screamed.

Unfortunately for Basbalulu, Gidragdra was the Evil God of Mad Slaughter. He was a mad god who gained strength not from the prayers of his worshipers, but from the screams of those he killed and those who feared being killed by him.

Although he was a commander of the Demon King’s army, his madness had been a source of trouble even for Guduranis, and this madness had been accelerated by the fragment of Guduranis’s soul that had been embedded in him.

Basbalulu screamed as he flew around to avoid Gidragdra’s attacks, but perhaps deciding that his situation would only worsen, he attempted to go on the offensive. In order to regain some stability, he produced rain from his body that was made of clouds and attempted to put some distance between them.

However–

“Shut up, you wretched remnants of the Demon King’s army!” shouted a Colossus as she sent Basbalulu flying before his rain could reach the ground.

She was beautiful and imposing, wearing an armor of crystal that reflected the sunlight. The people on the ground looked up, hoping that Alda had sent this god to save them. But naturally, they were wrong.

“I will never forgive you vermin or myself. Nor will I forgive Alda, Bellwood, Nineroad, Farmaun, or anyone who worships them! I will crush you!” she declared, her voice filled with rage and hatred, making the people realize that they were mistaken.

She was Nadia, the Crystal Colossus. She was a Colossus of Vida’s faction who had been defeated and sealed away during the battle between Vida and Alda.

“I remember that crystal!” said Gidragdra. “It was probably me who killed the Crystal Colossus before you! Now allow me to test whether you are worthy of killing as well!”

Basbalulu roared fiercely.

“I shall avenge my ancestor! DIIIE!” shouted Nadia.

The impacts of the clash between the three gods were felt on the ground. People took cover to avoid being knocked off their feet, and stained-glass windows in Churches shattered.

Bugs, rats, snakes, and lizards crawled from back alleys and hidden corners, and a countless number of crows took flight into the sky, causing the people to scream.

These small animals… were Demon King Familiars disguised as such.

“So, this is the next location,” one of them sighed.

“I never thought I would ever come here again,” murmured another in exasperation.

They joined to become an enormous swarm… and then fused, twisting their countless small limbs together to form a sphere.

And then Vandalieu appeared in the middle of that sphere.

“People will suspect me of having political motives, so let’s make this quick. According to Ricklent, I still have a lot more places I need to be, after all,” he said.

But like the demigods, Vandalieu was hundreds of meters up in the air, higher than the tips of the castle’s spires. Nobody on the ground could notice that he was there.

“I-it’s over… We’re all going to die…”

“Why! Why did four of them have to appear above us?!”

The answer to that was that Alda had set his eyes on this city because Vandalieu had a history here, and because it was in a duchy adjacent to the Boundary Mountain Range… but the city’s inhabitants had no way of knowing that.

I’m explaining things to Katie and Lucas’s representatives right now. I’m sure they’ll manage, Vandalieu thought.

Although he held no animosity for the people of Nineland, he felt no affection for them either, so he didn’t intend to do them any courtesy beyond that.

The two evil gods, who had been sealed away when Guduranis was still alive, froze in confusion as they sensed Vandalieu’s presence that resembled his.

“This presence is Guduranis-sama?! No, it’s different?!” exclaimed Gidragdra.

Basbalulu made a similarly shocked noise.

“‘World-piercing Destructive Hollow Cannon.’”

Basbalulu, the Evil God of Abandoned Clouds and Demon Rain, let out a dying noise as Vandalieu took this opportunity to fire a black beam of light that pierced him.

Although his body was made of clouds, making him resistant to physical attacks, he stood no chance against Vandalieu devouring his soul.

“Alright, I’ve successfully achieved one of the goals I came here for,” Vandalieu said.

One of the reasons he had come to the Hartner duchy after rescuing Luzemazera, the Goddess of Regeneration, was to destroy Basbalulu.

In the Demon King’s army, Basbalulu had been one of the subordinates of the Evil God of Cursed Poison. He was a fearsome god who robbed people of land to live on by condensing corrupted mana into a liquid that rained onto the ground, causing Devil’s Nests to spread in the blink of an eye.

If Vandalieu had left Basbalulu alone, Nineland would have quickly been turned into a Devil’s Nest, rendering it very difficult for ordinary humans to live there.

《You have acquired the Demon King’s Appetite!》

It seemed that Alda had embedded Basbalulu with Guduranis’s ‘Appetite.’ Why had he given ‘Appetite’ to an evil god whose body was made of clouds? Rather than making him stronger, Vandalieu suspected that it had made Basbalulu’s original instincts clash with the fragment, rendering both ineffective.

No, maybe he deliberately embedded an incompatible fragment in Basbalulu because he would be just as troubled if Basbalulu actually became stronger and spread more Devil’s Nests in a short period of time? Whatever, it doesn’t matter.

With that, Vandalieu pushed the thought from his mind and directed his attention towards Gidragdra and Nadia.

Both remaining gods attacked him.

“You bastard! How dare you kill Basbalulu! He was my prey! How dare you defeat him without even tormenting him!” Gidragdra screamed.

“Hmm, having murderous intent directed towards me for a reason I can’t really understand makes me feel calmer,” Vandalieu said.

“Die, you poor imitation of Guduranis!” yelled Nadia.

“No, I’m going to live. And so are you.”

Vandalieu deflected Gidragdra’s pincers with his arms, wrapped himself around the evil god’s joints in an attempt to destroy them, and counter-attacked with a punch.

He stopped Nadia’s sword, stretched out his other arm to fire ‘Barrier bullets,’ then attempted to tie her down by wrapping himself around her limbs.

And with his arms, he also blocked falling fragments of crystal and the spells that Gidragdra was firing, which occasionally were aimed towards the city.

“To think that I would be literally short on hands,” Vandalieu said to himself.

The other reason he had come here was to save Nadia, who was currently swinging her crystal sword in a frenzy.

Nadia was a Colossus, and unlike Luzemazera, she did not expend tremendous quantities of magic just to exist in the mortal world.

But as Vandalieu watched through the eyes of his Demon King Familiars, Nadia had started fighting the evil gods who had fragments of Guduranis’s soul embedded in them like her.

At this rate, Nadia would be defeated. She was just a single Colossus, but her foe was the Evil God of Mad Slaughter, a commander of the Demon King’s army. It was impossible for her to be victorious in that battle.

And another large factor was that Vandalieu had not positioned any fighting forces in Nineland other than his Demon King Familiars.

After all, I never imagined that Alda would unleash three gods here, with one of them being a commander of the Demon King’s army.

The Hartner Duchy was adjacent to the Boundary Mountain Range, but there was no way to directly cross the barrier, and Vandalieu and his allies were already aware of the locations of tunnels passing through.

And there was only one person Vandalieu was only just barely friendly with in Nineland – the reincarnated individual Katie.

Vandalieu had not expected that Alda would deploy so many forces here.

Gidragdra shouted in exertion as he fought, then chuckled. “It seems that you have started to understand the joy of taking lives, too!”

Using his pincers, he deflected, pierced, and severed the countless Demon King arms that Vandalieu was extending. But Vandalieu created thorns before the pincers impacted his arms, produced Jaws of the Demon King in the wounds where they were stabbed, and detonated severed arms using ‘Flaming Prison Death.’

At the same time, he used other Demon King arms to fire ‘Death Cannon’ and ‘Hollow Cannon,’ creating several holes in Gidragdra’s body.

“Well, I’ve grown stronger by feeding on the enemies I defeated, so I can’t say I don’t know what you mean,” Vandalieu said.

But it wasn’t that he was toying with Gidragdra.

He couldn’t commit to any large attacks because Nadia was resisting him more fiercely than he had expected.

“Why!” Nadia demanded. “Why won’t you attack me, imitation of Guduranis! Are you trying to say that I am not your enemy?!”

Nadia, the Crystal Colossus, was significantly weaker than the Colossus of Roaring Thunder Brateo, whom Vandalieu had fought against in the past. She was perhaps a little stronger than his son Radatel, the Colossus of Lightning.

But the way she struggled was troublesome. If Vandalieu used his arms to grab her arms or legs, she screamed as she attempted to tear off her own limbs to free herself without any hesitation.

“It’s precisely because you’re not my enemy that I’m struggling so much here,” Vandalieu said.

Having no choice, he hastily let her go.

If she were his enemy, he could just wait for her to destroy herself, but since he was trying to save her, he couldn’t allow that to happen. This made it very difficult to apprehend her.

And Gidragdra seemed to have noticed this; he was directing his attacks not only at Vandalieu, but at Nadia as well, only making the situation even more troublesome. “Then I can kill her, right?! I can kill her?!” he said gleefully.

… On top of all this, Vandalieu had to ensure that no harm came to the people of Nineland. And even at this very moment, his other Demon King Familiars – his split entities – were fighting against the other gods released by Alda.

Vandalieu had regained some of his Mana from devouring Basbalulu’s soul, which had dissolved quickly and tasted sweet like cotton candy, but it wouldn’t be long before he spent it all again.

If he was honest, he was short on hands. He wanted reinforcements, but Fidirg, Zozogante, Randolf, and Meorilith had already gone to where Pauvina was.

And to make things even worse, the knights’ order and adventurers of Nineland were attacking the three gods in the sky in order to protect their city… in other words, they were attacking Vandalieu as well – though Katie and the civil officials in her castle who had been informed about the situation were desperately trying to stop them.

Gidragdra cackled in joy. “I’m going to kill you both!”

“How much must you make a mockery of me before you are satisfied! I will sacrifice my pride and my life to defeat both of you!” Nadia declared.

“… Let’s stop caring about appearances,” Vandalieu decided, deciding that he was at his limit.

He unleashed the Demons waiting inside one of his ‘Inner Worlds.’

“Hahah! We have our orders from the great Vandalieu-sama! Defend them with your lives!”

“Protect the humans that crawl about on the ground!”

Vandalieu had kept these Demons waiting in the ‘Inner World,’ as they lacked the skills to serve as main fighting forces. But they were over a thousand in number.

Fragments of crystal and carapace the size of carriages were falling from the sky, and the Demons were capable enough to stop them from landing on the city. Vandalieu had refrained from releasing them due to the risk of causing more panic among the people on the ground, but he was no longer in a situation where he could afford to care about that.

“W-what?! Where did all these Demons come from?!” shouted a bewildered adventurer who had flown into the sky, prepared to give his life in order to stop the ‘three evil gods.’

“A human who is not crawling on the ground! What shall we do?!” one Demon said.

“Let us have him protect the other humans, too! Come, human!” another Demon shouted.

The adventurer shouted in panic as he was dragged off by the flock of Demons.

“Are you short on hands? Then shall I bring you the hand of a land-dwelling beast known as a cat?!” snarled Gidragdra, swinging a particularly large pincer downwards like a hammer.

TLN: This comes from the Japanese phrase “猫の手も借りたい” which literally means “to want to borrow a cat’s hand.” It is an expression to say that one is so short on hands, they would even accept the help of a cat.

“No thank you, I have plenty,” said Vandalieu, stopping the attack by raising one of his arms.

The pincer bounced off it spectacularly, and Gidragdra lost his balance as he was pulled along with its weight.

“W-what?!” he exclaimed.

Vandalieu had produced a paw pad of the Demon King on the arm, using its elasticity to bounce the pincer off it.

“Now is my chance!” shouted Nadia.

She attempted to skewer both Vandalieu and Gidragdra upon her crystal sword. Vandalieu deliberately let her. The crystal sword buried itself deep in him, and dark blood gushed out.

But it was Nadia who screamed. It was no ordinary blood that was splashing onto her. It was the slippery and highly viscous Demon King mucus, stained by the Demon King’s ink sacs.

And a new shadow appeared, causing the people of Nineland to feel true despair.

“Lafaz, you came to help,” Vandalieu said.

A fierce crow echoed across the sky.

It was Lafaz, the Bird Beast-king. Although he looked sinister because he had fused with an evil god, he still belonged to Vida’s faction.

With another loud crow, Lafaz beat his wings to hold Gidragdra back with shockwaves and blades of wind while tossing the orb in his beak to Vandalieu.

“Nice pass. Well then, there’s no need to wait, so I’ll undo this seal right now,” Vandalieu said.

He opened the Orb… the seal that Farmaun Gold had placed upon himself and Darmatark, the God of Purifying Flames. He then bit into and broke the fragment of Guduranis’s soul embedded in Darmatark.

《You have acquired the Demon King’s Malice!》

With that, Vandalieu swallowed Darmatark into one of his ‘Inner Worlds,’ forcefully sealing him away once more. Unlike the Demon King’s continent, there were no pseudo-Divine Realms near Nineland, so he had no other choice.

“W-what happened to me? Where am IIIII?” Darmatark shouted as he vanished.

“You bastard! Farmaun, I will kill you this time for sure!” snarled Gidragdra.

“I don’t need to hold anything back against you!” said Farmaun, grasping the situation as soon as he was freed and flying forward towards the remaining evil god.

In the meantime, Vandalieu dealt with Nadia as he had done with Darmatark.

《You have acquired the Demon King’s Vengefulness!》

It seemed that Nadia had been attacking gods embedded with fragments of Guduranis’s soul, including herself, because the ‘Vengefulness’ embedded within her had combined with her own desire for vengeance.

Nadia coughed weakly and went limp, still covered in mucus, no longer having the strength to move.

Still holding her with Demon King arms, Vandalieu turned to face the last remaining enemy. “Now then, let me give you a hand.”

He tore off one of his Demon King arms and hurled it at Gidragdra.

Gidragdra clicked his tongue. “Another exploding arm!”

Without even looking at it, he cut off one of his own pincers and sent it flying to block the Demon King arm which exploded as he had expected, but… it was not flames that emerged from within, but a black-red mist.

“What?!” Gidragdra exclaimed in confusion. But a moment later, he began screaming in pain.

Vandalieu had transformed the Demon King arm into ‘Bloodlust,’ flesh-eating microbes that even devoured gods. They entered Gidragdra through the many wounds all over his body, tormenting him as he had demanded of Vandalieu, slowly but surely feasting on him.

Realizing what it was, Farmaun and Lafaz raised their guard, believing that they would be devoured as well, but… they felt no pain.

“…? I thought ‘Bloodlust’ was an attack that doesn’t discriminate between its targets?” Farmaun murmured.

The black-red mist ignored Farmaun and swarmed around Gidragdra.

“I’ve become able to control it,” Vandalieu said.

The flesh-eating bacteria that Vandalieu had transformed his blood into was still a part of him. In other words, the ‘Bloodlust’ was Vandalieu, and Vandalieu was the ‘Bloodlust.’

With the power of things like the ‘Pale Rider’ Job, named after a being that spread contagious diseases, Vandalieu had succeeded in becoming able to control ‘Bloodlust.’

As Gidragdra was slowly devoured, Vandalieu dealt the finishing blow by impaling him with Demon King horns to save Mana.

“Thank you for the help, Farmaun, Lafaz,” Vandalieu said. “You two take Darmatark somewhere safe. Or are you still able to keep going?”

“… I might be able to manage one more location, but I think my strength is less of a problem than the fact that it makes no sense for me to be fighting on Vida’s side,” said Farmaun.

He was considered a god of Alda’s forces in human society; if he fought on Vida’s side now, it might come back to haunt him. He spoke frankly, hoping for Vandalieu’s understanding.

“Then please be on standby in Borgadon’s Divine Realm. I think someone somewhere will call for you when they’re short on hands,” said Vandalieu, rejecting Farmaun’s concerns because he could even use a cat’s help right now.

“Wait, but…” Farmaun began to protest.

“Lafaz seems to want you to do your part. Or to be more precise, he seems to want to say, ‘If you’ve got time to think about things that are going to happen much later, get moving already. This is a time of emergency.’”

“Ugh, he’s right, but…”

“Most of your worshipers are adventurers, and almost none of them are the kind of worshipers who engage in harsh training to increase their devotion, or the kind who worship you because they believe you’re an ally of Alda or Bellwood. They understand that they can’t hear your thoughts through Divine Messages,” Vandalieu continued in order to persuade Farmaun.

With human society believing that Farmaun was a god of Alda’s forces, in order to inform them that he had joined Vida’s side, he would have needed to send them Divine Messages.

But the majority of his worshipers only prayed to him lightly and carried his holy symbol for good luck. There had never been anyone with the devotion necessary to hear his Divine Messages even if he sent them.

And Farmaun was hesitant to actively spread the word that he had joined Vida’s side. How was he supposed to hold his head high and proudly declare that, after all that he’d done?

“But my request is that you put your shame aside and lend me your strength,” Vandalieu said.

He understood what Farmaun felt, but even so, he pressed the palms of every Demon King arm that was free together to form pairs of praying hands, praying to Farmaun.

“… If you’re praying that hard, I don’t have a choice, do I? Alright, I’ll be on standby in the Divine Realm of the God of Mountains,” Farmaun said.

As an unimportant god, if prayers were offered to him, Farmaun had no choice but to answer.

Lafaz gave a quiet crow, as if to say, “Finally.”

“Now then, I’m headed off somewhere else,” Vandalieu said.

He stored Nadia, who was still in a daze and covered in mucus, safely inside one of his ‘Inner Worlds.’ The Demons and the countless Demon King Familiars around also returned to him, and then he vanished.

《You have acquired the Demon King’s Murderous Intent!》

+++

## **391 : The bloated soul**

The Birgitt Duchy’s army and the Farzon Duchy’s second army were facing off at the border between the two duchies. But before the battle could tr uly begin, two intruders appeared, turning the situation into chaos.

On one side was Lezafortes, the Lion Beast-King, who let out a ferocious roar. He was emanating a presence and Mana that was somehow both divine and sinister.

On the other was the ‘All Bone Palace’ and ‘Concert Venue’ Knochen, who let out a deafening groan. He had been sent from the Demon Empire of Vidal to reinforce the Birgitt Duchy’s army.

A beast-king with a body length of a hundred meters and a mass of bone with more than ten times that body volume. The clash between these two forces was not something that any ordinary person could interfere with.

“I am telling you to kill me! Why can’t you understand?!”  Lezafortes said angrily, bringing his front legs down to smash the bone arms that Knochen had raised to defend himself. With the same momentum, his paws crashed into the dirt, creating enormous holes.

Knochen groaned once more. Even as fragments of his bones scattered into the air, he swiftly attempted to pin Lezafortes’s front paws to the ground. His movements were so quick that it made one wonder if he had even taken damage at all.

But with a growl, Lezafortes managed to protect his front paws with his head. The bones that Knochen rained down upon him were deflected by his sturdy mane.

However, Knochen was far from being on the back foot. Vandalieu had given Knochen his own bones, and Knochen fired them at Lezafortes now as projectiles. The bones pierced his tough fur and skin, though they were stopped by his muscles before they could reach his organs. With a howl of pain, Lezafortes leapt backwards in an attempt to put some distance between himself and his foe.

Knochen showed no mercy. He unleashed the ‘Elder Dragon Poison Breath,’ causing the demigod to howl again before coughing and choking.

With a powerful poison enveloping him, Lezafortes heaved in suffering, blood-tinged saliva spewing from his mouth. The grass and trees around him withered and turned brown.

The soldiers of the Farzon Duchy’s army were hit by the shockwaves of this attack, causing them to drop dead, one after another.

One of them screamed in agony.

“M-my body’s melting…” one said weakly before collapsing.

Watching this unfold from his stronghold, Duke Gerald Birgitt, who was commanding the Birgitt Duchy’s army, gave a dry laugh. “… I sure am glad that we built friendly relations with the Demon Empire of Vidal.”

When Lezafortes appeared in the sky, Gerald had felt an instinctual fear and prepared for his own death. But when he saw Knochen fly at Lezafortes and even inflict damage upon the Farzon Duchy’s army at the same time, that fear had vanished… though he was instead filled with a sense of powerlessness.

“Bombarde, hypothetically speaking… is it even possible to assist Knochen-dono?” Gerald asked his close aide.

“… We have already sent messengers offering a temporary truce and telling them to surrender, haven’t we?” said Bombarde, a bear-type Beast-kin who was one of the Birgitt Duchy’s most elite soldiers.

“That isn’t what I mean. I’m talking about a more direct kind of assistance. Ah, it’s just for future reference, of course. I don’t intend to actually give the order.”

Bombarde stared at the battle between Lezafortes and Knochen, who had finally assumed a form that was a combination of an Elder Dragon and a Colossus. “Even if an average soldier used all of their strength as if their life depended on it, they would still be crushed like a fly if they even went anywhere close to that battle. Even an above-average soldier would almost certainly die in vain, achieving nothing. It would be wise to avoid attacking, even if only to target the Farzon Duchy’s army.”

“Yes, you’re right. Thank you. That puts my mind at ease,” Gerald said.

The reason Gerard was here right now despite the fact that he was the duke was because he believed he would be safest right here on the battlefield, where the reinforcements he had requested from the Demon Empire of Vidal were.

This was true in a way, and because Lezafortes had fallen from the sky before the battle against the Farzon Duchy’s army had even started, not a single person from the Birgitt Duchy’s army or the reinforcements deployed from the other duchies had even been injured.

Even now, because the armies had been pulled back to keep their distance from Knochen and Lezafortes, nobody had a scratch on them other than those who had fallen over from the constant trembling of the earth.

Meanwhile, the state of the Farzon Duchy’s army could be summed up in a single word: wretched.

The Farzon Duchy’s army had been divided in two, as they had attacked here and the Hartner Duchy at the same time so that they could choose between the best duchy to cross the Boundary Mountain Range from. After halving their forces, they had bolstered them with adventurers and the order of priest-warriors of the Church of Alda before embarking on this war. Like the army deployed on the border with the Hartner Duchy, the unexpected circumstances had thrown their chain of command into chaos, which was why they were stuck in place, unable to establish a truce with the enemy army or retreat.

And although Gerald initially thought that the Farzon Duchy’s army might look for an opportunity to interfere in the battle between Knochen and Lezafortes, they were actually going the long way around to try and attack the Birgitt Duchy’s army, so they couldn’t let their guards down – though that was precisely why Knochen wasn’t holding back from getting the Farzon Duchy’s army caught up in his attacks, causing great damage to them.

“But all that we are doing is keeping our distance, keeping our defenses up, and watching the battle from afar… Given that, it is not so strange for me to question why I am even here, is it?” Gerald said.

“The same is true for us. Or so I would like to say, but… if we were to get caught up in that, we would die,” said Bombarde.

As he watched, a silhouette that was apparently a hero candidate activated ‘Familiar Spirit Descent’ and charged at Knochen and Lezafortes, only to vanish into a torrent of bones a moment later.

“I suppose it is only to be expected that even Knochen-dono is struggling against a Beast-king. I do think that it is troublesome, but as a Beast-kin, I cannot deny that I feel proud,” Bombarde said.

A Demon King Familiar that had remained silent up until now suddenly spoke up. “Actually, Lezafortes currently has a fragment of Guduranis’s soul embedded in him, preventing him from using his full strength.”

“Is that true? I thought that having a fragment of the Demon King’s soul embedded in him would make him stronger,” said Gerald.

“It is true that fragments generally make the host stronger. But that is only true if the host actively makes use of them, like Rikudou… Dark Avalon,” explained the Demon King Familiar.

Those who had fragments of the Demon King’s soul embedded in them generally gained more Mana and became more aggressive, though the degree of each effect varied depending on which fragment it was. There were also other effects, such as the host becoming able to use the fragments’ original powers… For example, the ‘Instinct’ would make the host’s instincts for survival and combat sharper, while the ‘Memories’ would allow the host to replicate spells and combat techniques from Guduranis’s memories.

“But as you can see, Lezafortes is resisting the fragment. He is only on a rampage right now because he’s unable to completely suppress it, so I don’t think he’s able to use his full strength right now,” the Demon King Familiar said. “Even now, he’s trying to move in a way that avoids damage to the nature and humans around him.”

Indeed, it was a different story if the host was resisting the fragment infesting them. Even though the host would still gain increased Mana, neither the host nor the soul fragment would be able to use it properly if they were clashing against one another.

There is a saying: ‘You are your own worst enemy.’ And that could not be more true for Lezafortez right now.

“Considering that, isn’t he being quite merciless to Knochen-dono?” said Gerald.

Just as he said that, Lezafortes swung his front paws, shattering the Elder-Dragon-Colossus-form Knochen’s legs. The resulting snapping noise was so loud that it was difficult to believe that it was the sound of bones being broken.

“That’s because Knochen is Undead, which means Lezafortes doesn’t consider him to be someone who needs to be protected, and because Knochen is actively getting the humans of the Farzon Duchy caught up in the battle,” the Demon King Familiar explained. “After all, Lezafortes has essentially been teleported from a hundred thousand years ago to the present day.”

“I-I see,” said Gerald.

“But that ends here,” the Demon King Familiar said, leaping forward.

It was joined by a swarm of Demon King Familiars that appeared out of nowhere. There were so many of them that one had to wonder, where had they all been hiding?

“This Undead, it has the presence of Marduke, Zerno, and Ganpaplio?!” Lezafortes exclaimed, sensing the presence of the great gods in Knochen’s bones.

Knochen roared as he coordinated his movements with the Demon King Familiars and caught Lezafortes by surprise to bind his limbs.

“C-curses!”

“I’m sorry to keep you waiting,” said Vandalieu’s main body as it appeared among the Demon King Familiars. “I’ll be taking that fragment of the Demon King now.”

With the soul fragment removed, Lezafortes regained his sanity. “Agh, where in the world am I?!”

“I’ll be taking him away to explain the situation, so I’ll leave the rest to you,” Vandalieu said.

And with that, he put Lezafortes in one of his inner worlds and disappeared back into the sea of countless Demon King Familiars.

Knochen still remained on the battlefield. And now that he had one less enemy to worry about, he began scattering the potential heroes and the warriors of the Church of Alda as they attacked him recklessly, groaning fiercely as he ripped the bones out of their bodies while they were still alive to add them to his own body.

“Once that battle settles down, let’s send another messenger to offer a ceasefire,” said Gerald.

“Indeed, I expect that the more fanatical ones will have had their bones pulled out of them by then,” said Bombarde.

And so, the battle on the holy war’s Birgitt Duchy front came to an end.

《You have acquired the Demon King’s Pride!》

While on the move, Vandalieu checked his current status.

“Hmm, I’ve taken quite a beating.”

There was no problem with his physical body, but his soul had become quite distorted, due to having devoured so many fragments of Guduranis’s soul in such a short period of time.

“To think that my soul would get bloated as well, not just my stomach… At this rate, everyone will be shocked when I go to visit their Divine Realms.”

Vandalieu remained unaware that his soul had been more sinister in appearance than the average evil god, even before he began devouring fragments of Guduranis’s soul. He started twisting and stretching himself, trying to force it into a more organized shape.

《The acquired Demon King soul fragments have fused to become ‘True Demon King!’》

“This should do. Now then, let’s absorb all of the other fragments of Guduranis’s soul that are elsewhere, before Heinz and his party reach Talosheim.”

Vandalieu had deliberately created an entrance by which Heinz and his companions could infiltrate the region inside the Boundary Mountain Range in the form of a valley, and he had prepared fighting forces and multiple fake Talosheims to slow them down.

Vandalieu didn’t know whether Heinz was really capable of cutting through the Boundary Mountain Range, whose mountains were several thousand meters tall, but creating a straightforward path for Heinz had seemed wiser than finding out. This way, he didn’t have to worry about which part of the mountain range would be cut through, and it had allowed him to decide Heinz’s path of infiltration.

Of course, allowing Heinz and his companions into the region within the Boundary Mountain Range meant exposing Talosheim and the other nations to danger. Thus, Vandalieu had moved Talosheim.

Along the path used in the Mirg shield-nation’s invasion about two hundred years ago, he had placed Golems and forts to slow Heinz and his companions down, and beyond those was a replica of Talosheim whose buildings looked just like the real thing. And beyond that replica were even more replicas of Talosheim.

As for the real Talosheim, Vandalieu had turned the entire city into a golem and moved it… placing it inside one of the floors of a specially-made Dungeon. He had then moved the Dungeon’s entrance, so Heinz and his companions would never reach it.

On top of that, he had returned Mei and Mari to Origin for now, just in case. Both of them had wanted to remain here, but Lambda was currently more dangerous than Origin was… There were several Demon King Familiars with them, and Vandalieu had trained the Ghosts of the former presidents and such as much as possible, so they should be fine.

_With that said, the fact that death-attribute mages other than me exist probably doesn’t matter much to Heinz right now._

The Five-colored Blades had learned of Mei and Mari’s existence from the reincarnated individual Asagi, but circumstances had changed since then.

Right now, Heinz was trying to kill Vandalieu because the final words of the imperfectly resurrected Guduranis had convinced him that it was possible for Vandalieu to one day be taken over by the fragments of Guduranis’s soul that he had absorbed.

There was no way of knowing if that would happen in five seconds, in a year, or a hundred years, but as long as Heinz believed that there was a chance that it could happen, he would likely never change his mind on his belief that Vandalieu needed to be killed.

However, just because Mei and Mari could use death-attribute magic didn’t mean that they were capable of absorbing fragments of Guduranis’s soul. Thus, no matter what Heinz was thinking, he wouldn’t prioritize going after their lives before Vandalieu’s.

_At the very least, he shouldn’t be trying to find them at the risk of exhausting himself before killing me… Considering that, the current situation might be the most convenient thing for him. After all, he’s just fighting Golems that aren’t very strong while pretending to be headed in Talosheim’s direction until I come to him._

It occurred to Vandalieu that the fact that Heinz and his companions were moving so slowly might be because he was waiting for Vandalieu to come out rather than trying to make it to Talosheim, where real traps and preparations to repel them might have been made.

… If that was the case, Vandalieu felt like a fool for putting so much effort into making all kinds of preparations, but it was better than suffering as a result of not preparing enough.

And although he knew what Heinz was thinking, that was not true for Bellwood and Alda, so he decided not to let his guard down until they were dead.

“Ah, the Golems have been wiped out.”

While Vandalieu was doing this, the Golems that were slowing down Heinz and his companions had run out more quickly than anticipated.

“… They’re currently headed towards a fake Talosheim, so I suppose I can just leave them. The fake Talosheim has _that_, too, though I would have liked to settle things without showing it to anyone if possible.”

In order to make the fake Talosheims as close replicas of the real one as possible, they had required replicas of a particular structure… the enormous statue of Vandalieu. They had been turned into Golems and their interiors had been filled with Demon King Familiars – and there were multiple of them. These would likely keep Heinz and his companions stalled for a while longer.

“The next location is where Mom is.”

And with that, Vandalieu headed to the Jahan Duchy, where Darcia was fighting.

Alda, the God of Law and Fate, had unsealed and unleashed numerous gods all over the world, but he had not done so in the Holy Nation of Amid, its vassal states, or the Farzon Duchy.

Vandalieu was unlikely to have positioned any of his fighting forces there, and even though Alda was willing to allow the population of humanity to drop to several thousand during this war, he had believed that there was no use in meaninglessly reducing the number of his own worshipers.

However, Alda had unleashed multiple gods in the Jahan Duchy. It was a region with many devout worshipers of Alda, but it had already been exposed to Vandalieu’s influence. It was only a matter of time before its people were corrupted (converted to worshiping Vida’s faction) and, as much as Alda pitied them, he had decided that it was best to reduce his numbers while he still could.

And most importantly, he had done so because Darcia, the ‘Incarnation of Vida,’ was there.

“Vida-sama!” roared a Beast-king with three eyes, enormous tusks, and wings on its back. It breathed heavily through its nose as it approached Darcia. “Come, Vida-sama! Let us create children! I, Vafovald, have prepared myself to become father to a new Beast-kin race!”

This was Vafovald, the Evil Demon Elephant Beast-king. Although he fell in the battle against the Demon King, as an evil god attempted to devour him, he survived by instead fusing with his would-be devourer and taking over him. Now, he was obsessed with Vida in a bad way.

“I’m sorry! You’ll have to discuss that with Vida herself later!” said Darcia.

Having used ‘Goddess Descent,’ Vafovald had mistaken her for Vida. She was currently using a Magic Item to fly, doing her utmost to run away while fighting in order to draw him and the others away from the Jahan Duchy’s cities.

This was also to protect these gods.

Another was Byazekbyoct, the Evil God of Impure Light. He looked like nothing more than a group of human-child-sized disco balls, but he screeched as he fired beams of light containing poison – something that should be impossible, according to this world’s laws of physics – in Darcia’s direction.

“‘Radiance Bending Wall!’” shouted Zadiris, creating a barrier that bent light in order to refract Byazekbyoct’s beams. “Curse you, you big oaf! Will you not think of those who have to defend against these attacks!”

“Mother, he has lost his sanity because of the fragment of the Demon King’s soul. He can’t hear anything you’re saying,” said Basdia as she bisected one of the shining spheres that made up the evil god’s body.

“I understand that, but I cannot help but say it. These lust-blinded fools,” Zadiris sighed in exasperation.

Indeed, it was not just Vafovald who had mistaken Darcia for Vida.

“I shall be the first to create children with Vida-sama! The sea needs Sea-Beast-kin, not just Merfolk!” snarled Toothwald, the Walrus Beast-king, as he bared his tusks to intimidate Vafovald.

“What?! You would dare interfere with my relations with Vida-sama?! Unforgiveable!”

“Let us settle this like men!”

The two Beast-kings glared at each other, baring their fangs and readying themselves to fight over Vida, who had descended upon Darcia’s body.

“Stop it! Don’t fight here!” Darcia said hastily, trying to stop them.

The city was still too close, after all.

Darcia thought of undoing ‘Goddess Descent,’ but Vida’s anger was too fierce for her to suppress – Vida was likely furious at Alda for what he had done to these two gods who adored her.

By summoning Vida, she had been able to quickly defeat and seal away one of the evil gods of the Demon King’s army that had appeared at the same time as Byazekbyoct.

But the appearance of Vafovald and Toothwald had complicated the situation and started a peculiar three-way battle.

And then, the countless Demon King Familiars gathered… and Vandalieu appeared.

“I cannot pretend I didn’t hear all that,” he said.

· **Name:** Knochen

· **Titles**: All Bone Palace, Concert Venue, Flesh and Bone Colossus

· **Rank:** 16

## **392 : The gluttonous Elder Dragon who even drinks evil poison**

The hundred-meter-tall walrus collided head-on with the enormous body that Vandalieu had created with a countless number of Demon King arms, legs, and jointed legs.

Toothwald, the Walrus Beast-king, grunted as he was stopped in his tracks. “I am the one being overpowered?!”

“There’s a big difference in the number of legs we have, after all,” said Vandalieu.

By absorbing the fragments he had received from the dukes of the Orbaume Kingdom, he had become able to produce legs of the Demon King.

“And you lose points for lacking strength in your charge,” Vandalieu said.

By moving those countless legs and jointed legs, he pushed Toothwald back, away from the Jahan Duchy’s capital.

“W-where are you taking me?!” Toothwald demanded.

“I was thinking that we should get further away from the city, just in case,” Vandalieu replied.

“Are you that intent on separating me from Vida-sama?!”

“You’re not worthy of me calling you stepfather.”

Vandalieu’s main body was tiny from Toothwald’s perspective, but at that moment, he felt a powerful pressure emanating from it. Despite being in a state of madness induced by the Demon King soul fragment embedded in him, Toothwald could not help but flinch.

“This should do,” said Vandalieu, deciding that they were far away enough from the city. “Now then, I will remove the fragment of the Demon King’s soul.”

In order to remove the fragment of Guduranis’s soul from Toothwald, whose movements were dulled after flinching in fear, Vandalieu produced tentacles with suction cups. His target this time was an enormous male walrus rather than a goddess or a female Colossus, so he felt very at ease.

However, before Vandalieu could complete this task, Vafovald, the Evil Demon Elephant Beast-king, raised his trunk and charged at Vandalieu. “Get back, Toothwald!”

But Vandalieu remained calm and cast ‘Impact-Negating Barrier,’ which removed all kinetic energy from Vafovald’s mass.

“Y-You stopped this attack from my trunk, which is praised to be powerful enough to break mountains?!” Vafovald exclaimed.

With its kinetic energy sapped from it, Vafovald’s trunk drooped lifelessly. As the Beast-king stood there in astonishment, a thick tentacle… or rather, a trunk of the Demon King wrapped around him.

“Yes, yes, I’ll be with you shortly,” Vandalieu said. “And you lose points for that. The owner of a trunk that can only attack like _that_ isn’t qualified to become my stepfather, either.”

“Y-you bastard! You intend to tear apart the bonds between myself and Vida-sama?!” Vafovald roared.

“No, you can talk about those bonds with Vida herself later. But please stop chasing my mother around,” said Vandalieu, attempting to stop Vafovald’s movements so that he could remove the soul fragment embedded within him.

Vafovald was only chasing Darcia around because the fragment of Guduranis’s soul infesting him had caused him to lose his sanity. In other words, this was the fault of Alda, the God of Law and Fate. Vafovald was not at fault here.

With a high-pitched, piercing screech, Byazekbyoct, the Evil God of Impure Light, rained beams of light down in Vandalieu’s direction – not caring about whether Toothwald or Vafovald were hit, of course.

“‘Great Radiance Bending Wall!’ ‘Lightning Cannon!’” shouted Zadiris.

“I won’t let you interfere!” declared Basdia. “‘Divine Severing!’”

Zadiris’s Light Princess Magic refracted the corrupted light once more, while Basdia’s axe cleaved the spheres that made up Byazekbyoct’s body, one after another.

“I won’t let you do as you please anymore!” said Darcia.

She had used ‘Chaos’ to transform her legs and produce talons, and she was now using them to shred the spheres.

Zadiris, Basdia, and Darcia’s role was to hold Byazekbyoct back while Vandalieu absorbed the Demon King soul fragments from the two Beast-kings.

Byazekbyoct let out a noise that could be described as a scream, or perhaps a dull, piercing cry. But as one might expect of an evil god, he was not merely wailing in pain.

Blades of light appeared from the countless spheres that he was made of, and began attacking Basdia, Darcia and Zadiris. He had switched to melee combat, having seemed to have decided that attacking mainly with beams of light was disadvantageous for him.

“‘Rapid Reaction!’ Those crude movements won’t work on us!” said Darcia.

Byazekbyoct’s movements were too slow for Darcia and Basdia. Darcia beat him with her transformation staff, while Basdia crushed the blades of light with her boots.

“They _will_ work on you, Mother, so fall back to where Van is!” Basdia warned Zadiris.

“Indeed. I will take you up on your offer and fall back!” said Zadiris.

Zadiris was not as proficient in melee combat; it would be difficult for her to evade all of the spheres with blades of light attached to them flying around at high speed while casting her spells. Thus, she fell back to where Vandalieu was as quickly as she could.

It wouldn’t have been a problem if Darcia and Basdia were able to completely stop Byazekbyoct, but there were simply too many spheres. No matter how strong they were, they simply couldn’t deal with all of them. And no matter how many spheres they broke, pierced, or cut apart, no matter how much Byazekbyoct screamed, the evil god showed no signs of weakening.

“Can you not see if he has a weak spot?” Basdia asked the split entity of Vandalieu that had descended upon her body.

She wanted to know if Byazekbyoct had a main body or core of some kind.

“I don’t know. My main body is searching the Demon King’s Memories, but… Guduranis didn’t really manage his subordinates that closely,” the split entity replied.

Vandalieu had absorbed the Demon King’s Memories, but it was made of the memories of a life-form from another world, who possessed different values and a different mind structure, recorded by sensory organs whose number, structure, and type were also different from those of humans.

It wasn’t a document that was organized for others to easily understand, and Guduranis had not possessed the ‘Perfect Record’ Skill that Vandalieu possessed now, so there were also things that Guduranis had forgotten. And it was Guduranis’s personal memories; he had not even bothered to remember things that were of no interest to him.

And it seemed that Guduranis did not have a detailed understanding of his subordinates’ abilities or biology. He did remember details about his close aides that served as commanders, whose names were spoken of in legends. But he only remembered the names and a few characteristics of the more insignificant evil gods.

Of course, it was this structure of the Demon King’s army that had allowed the champion Zakkart to successfully convince Gufadgarn and Fidirg to change sides.

“I see. What about you, Darcia?” Basdia asked.

“I don’t know, either. All of the balls look the same,” Darcia replied. Even with Vida descended upon her, her eyes could not tell the spheres apart. “Every sphere has the same quantity of Vitality, and it doesn’t look like they’re trying to protect one in particular. Each ball might be part of a group that is known as Byazekbyoct… I think that’s the kind of being that he is.”

There wasn’t one sphere in particular that was controlling the others; they were moving as if they were a countless number of individual sphere-shaped organisms that made up a group known as Byazekbyoct. The evil god was originally from a race that was built like this.

Basdia frowned upon hearing Darcia’s explanation. “I see, so he’s the same as Van is now, then. It’s troublesome to have an enemy that can do the same thing.”

“No, he’s completely different from me. I have a main body, after all,” said the split entity of Vandalieu in disagreement.

Meanwhile, behind Basdia, Vafovald unleashed a shockwave with his trunk as he resisted Vandalieu’s attempt to restrain him. The shockwave struck Vandalieu’s main body, causing it to go flying as it fell to pieces.

“B-boy?!” Zadiris shouted in despair.

But a moment later, a part of a nearby Demon King arm transformed into a new Vandalieu.

“I’m over here, Zadiris. That was a Demon King Familiar that was my main body until just a second ago,” the newly-formed Vandalieu said.

Up until recently, he had been doing much trial-and-error to try and increase the number of main bodies he possessed, but this had ultimately been unsuccessful. Instead, he had become able to make his main body switch places with any of his split entities – his Demon King Familiars or body parts made with Demon King fragments.

Vandalieu’s Demon King Familiars and his split entities were him. With that being the case, Vandalieu had believed that it would be possible to turn a Demon King Familiar into his main body.

With further trial-and-error, he had succeeded in becoming able to switch places with parts made from Demon King fragments or his Demon King Familiars.

Naturally, he was able to do this with main-body-type Demon King Familiars, but even in cases where the Demon King Familiars had different forms or lacked the variety of fragments to create a human body, he was still able to transform them into a new main body.

If he wanted to, he could, at a moment’s notice, switch places with any of the small-animal-type Demon King Familiars in the cities, the Demon King Familiars guarding Hadros in the Jahan Duchy’s castle, the Demon King Familiars deployed in the Hartner Duchy, or the horse-type Demon King Familiar that Juliana was riding while fighting against Zobuberogia, the Evil God of Ruinous Greed.

Vandalieu had used this method – the method of having his main body switch places with Demon King Familiars all over the world – to move between locations as if teleporting.

And just now, he had switched his main body’s position with a body part made of Demon King fragments in order to evade Byazekbyoct’s beams of light… Strictly speaking, the evil god’s attacks had struck their target, but the amount of damage Vandalieu received from one of his countless arms being attacked was far, far less than the damage he would receive if his main body was attacked.

“I-I see. But is it alright for you to be here? Is there not another place where our allies are struggling?” asked Zadiris.

“There is, but things have worked out so that I don’t need to go there for now,” Vandalieu replied.

Rewinding time a little…

Dobopezepaluo, the Evil God of Cursed Poison, appeared in the skies over the Sauron Duchy’s capital. This event was sudden and unexpected, both to the people in the city and to Dobopezepaluo himself.

_Where am I? Who undid my seal? Was it Guduranis-sama? But the world is still so unsightly,_ he thought.

The air was neither hot nor cold, and it lacked the stench of mold and fungus spores. The sky was not dark, but neither was it bright enough to burn flesh.

It was like a breeding farm created to allow weak, inferior organisms to live. And yet, these inferior organisms did not obediently allow themselves to be devoured. They formed groups and used tools to resist. It was truly repulsive and unsightly.

_Unsightly… Unsightly! Unsightly! Unsightly! It is far too unsightly and corrupted to become our new beautiful home! I must purify it as quickly as possible!_

Under ordinary circumstances, it was likely that Dobopezepaluo would have fled this place and looked for somewhere to hide, prioritizing understanding the circumstances he found himself in and ensuring his own safety first.

He had already been sealed away once before. In other words, he had been defeated by the champions’ army. Even if his seal had been undone, if he were to stay here, it was possible that the champions would notice that he had been released and gather to seal him away again.

And yet, he was prioritizing contaminating the world with his own cursed poison. It was because of the sheer revulsion he felt towards the natural environment of the world of Lambda and how different it was from his ideal pleasant environment. And it was because of the fragment of Guduranis’s soul that had infested him, causing him to gradually lose his sanity.

If he were to proceed and spread his poison into his surroundings, the people of the Sauron Duchy at ground level would likely die helplessly.

But before Dobopezepaluo could begin doing so, a bizarre Elder Dragon appeared at the edge of his vision.

“…? Who are you?” Dobopezepaluo asked.

Strangely, the Elder Dragon asked the same thing. “What are you?”

This Elder Dragon was Bakunawa, Vandalieu’s first-born child and son of Tiamat, the Mountain Queen Elder Dragon God. Upon smelling an unfamiliar, dangerous scent, he had flown over here from beyond the Ark Mountain Range.

The evil god resembled an upside-down octopus, with a head covered in barnacle-like shells and protuberances, and tentacles that possessed numerous eyes and mouths with irregular spacing between them. As Bakunawa looked at him, he instinctively sensed that this was a dangerous being.

He felt anger at the danger that this being’s presence imposed upon his beloved elder sister, and he was filled with an overwhelming hunger.

“Are you a monster who has increased its Rank? Or are you an Elder Dragon who mutated after joining our side? No, it matters not. Help me purify this world,” Dobopezepaluo ordered.

“I’m _definitely_ going to devour you!” Bakunawa declared.

Dobopezepaluo made an astonished noise as Bakunawa closed the distance between them in an instant, as if he had teleported. Bakunawa twisted his body in mid-air to unleash a powerful attack with his tail.

At that moment, cracks appeared in the evil god’s barnacle-like protuberances, spraying purple, venomous-looking blood into the air from his entire body surface. As his title suggested, Dobopezepaluo’s entire body was made of malicious poison and curses.

But before any of his blood or shell fragments could fall upon the ground, Bakunawa inhaled through the enormous mouth on his torso, consuming it all.

“As I thought, delicious!” he said.

Dobopezepaluo’s countless eyes opened wide in astonishment.

_Impossible! He is devouring me?! Is this the power of the ‘Skills’ that the Demon King spoke of?!_

Even in the world that Dobopezepaluo had originally come from, there had not been a single living creature who could remain unharmed after consuming a part of him. Guduranis, with his overwhelming power, had been Dobopezepaluo’s only natural enemy. And yet, in this hideous world, he had found a new natural enemy.

The moment he came to this realization, his mind was taken over by an unnatural anger. “Curse you! Devour me, you say?!”

Bakunawa’s tail attack had sent the evil god flying away from the city towards the Ark Mountain Range, but Dobopezepaluo forcibly stopped his body mid-air and secreted more cursed poison.

“Don’t underestimate me! I am Dobopezepaluo, the Evil God of Cursed Poison! I am the evil god who rules over curses and poison! I do not know who you are, but if your confidence is based on a mere resistance Skill, you would be a fool to think that would be enough to resist my cursed poison!”

The barnacle-like protuberances produced a waterfall of poison so deadly that a single whiff would cause an ordinary person’s nasal tract and brain to rot away. It was a cursed poison designed to kill foes – far more vicious than the poison he released to ‘purify’ this world.

Even if someone possessed the ‘Status Effect Immunity’ Skill, they would still die in an instant as the curse poisoned their body and mind. Even Bellwood and the other champions who had sealed Dobopezepaluo away had not come up with any strategy beyond using sheer power in order to purify the cursed poison with light and fire-attribute magic while fighting. And although they had succeeded in sealing away the evil god before they succumbed to the poison, they had not actually overcome the cursed poison itself.

But Dobopezepaluo was still oblivious.

“This juice is delicioooous!” Bakunawa exclaimed as he chased after Dobopezepaluo, away from the skies above the Sauron Duchy’s capital.

With his mouth wide open, he continued sucking in and swallowing the cursed poison.

It had a rich, lung-burning, sickly-sweet aroma; a tongue-numbing fizziness that was stronger than Cola, and the texture of a rich smoothie.

“Papa’s more delicious, though,” Bakunawa added.

He was the first death-attribute Elder Dragon to be born in this world. He was the first child of the Demon King that was born in this world, the one who ruled over all causes of death – curses, poison, and disease.

Attempting to kill him with curses and poison was more foolish than trying to burn a Fire Dragon to death with flames.

“Impossible… even the champions could not remain unharmed after coming into contact with my cursed poison, but this Elder Dragon is swallowing it and calling it delicious?! S-such power and beauty…!” Dobopezepaluo exclaimed.

Bakunawa was nullifying the cursed poison and continuously swallowing it, Dobopezepaluo’s chest (or rather, the part of his body that was equivalent to his chest) burned with respect for him. But that was quickly erased by a fierce anger.

“Unacceptable! I will not accept it! A being more powerful and beautiful than myself, more powerful and beautiful than Guduranis-sama, must not exist in this unsightly world!”

With that anger burning in him so that the ‘Narcissism’ within him would not be denied, the evil god produced more cursed poison just to keep Bakunawa’s mouth occupied while spewing additional, different kinds of poison from his heads that resembled octopus tentacles.

Venom Gusts and Venom Slimes, which were poison and curses that had turned into monsters, began appearing one after another. Of course, Dobopezepaluo did not expect these to defeat Bakunawa. However, judging from the fact that Bakunawa was trying to protect this land, he expected that creating monsters and making them cause damage would distract him and create an opening to make his counter-attack.

However, although the champions that Dobopezepaluo feared were not present in this land, there were numerous heroes.
