The number of my wives is already set in stone, and if Akitsushima Island calms down due to the marriages, Roderich will be relieved, too.

Because of that, I’d like to postpone dealing with Philine for a bit longer, if possible.

The other nobles? I don’t care! Don’t push any more girls on me!

“How is the ruling of Akitsushima Island actually going?”

“At present, everything is proceeding well, I’d say.”

Since they’re basically Mizuho people──though it’d be bad not to call them Akitsushima people since the islanders would get angry if you call them Mizuho people──they have been cautious for militaristic reasons, but it seemed to have been a great idea to show them my magic.

There were almost no casualties during the conquest, and the few that got injured or killed simply had ignored the rules of battle. The development of the island is advancing under the lead of the Margrave Baumeister House, and once the population grows, it will also become possible for them to migrate to other places. We’re forcing the hot-blooded folks to earn money in monster domains. All that’s left now is to stabilize our family’s rule until I die.

“That’s great to hear. At any rate, the negotiations between the Kingdom and the demons are completely stuck.”

With the Empire having joined as well, there are various influential people and groups with various interests among the three parties. You can say it’s only natural that a solution will take time.

“Recently, it looks like they’re trying to use excavated items for technological development.”

“They built a device to prevent theft.”

“I want that by all means.”

In reality, that alone won’t be sufficient. We have been buying various magic tools for cheap from the demon queen’s company. We managed to obtain a large number of magic tools, which are regarded as trash in the demon country, in this way, allowing us to use them in the development of the Baumeister territory, including Akitsushima Island.

The purchase itself is illegal, or rather, very dodgy in regard to the law, but if we didn’t do this, I wouldn’t be able to handle all of the territory myself since it’s simply too big. If we don’t automate it through magic tools, the development won’t proceed. Of course, one could say we should buy the necessary tools at the Kingdom’s magic tool guild, but magic railroad cars, magic farm machinery, and magic desalination facilities didn’t exist in the Kingdom because of the lack of technological level of the magic tool guild.

Moreover, because the production output of other magic tools that actually exist in the Kingdom is low as well, the prices are abnormally high. Even then, it’d be all well if only we could procure the tools, but the shortage of stock meant that you had to reserve and wait for them.

Usually, this situation is so bad that anyone would consider importing magic tools from elsewhere, but the magic tool guild will definitely go out of business if highly efficient, moderately priced magic tools are imported from the demon country.

Our magic tool guild has linked up with the Empire’s magic tool guild, lobbying for a ban on magic tool imports. Given that the chief executive of the magic tool guild passed away in this situation, things became unnecessarily more complicated and confusing.

If the negotiations are concluded because of this death, the people would suspect that the Kingdom had signed an unfavorable treaty after being tricked.

“Having said that, it’s not like the situation has changed in any way. The Kingdom is plunging ahead with its development. Meanwhile, the recent civil war has strengthened the power of the central government in the Empire. This is allowing the Emperor to push the development of magic tools while also using it as a means of post-war recovery.”

This might be another reason why the negotiations aren’t going anywhere. Moreover, because of the recent change in governments in the demon country, no experienced politicians are taking part in the negotiations on their side.

“There is no need to fret.”

“I think so as well.”

Like this, the party came to an end without a hitch. Once again, it hit me that I had become a Margrave, but as expected, it didn’t change anything about my everyday life.

“Milord, today’s schedule is full. After all, you have managed to become a Margrave. It’s a peerage equal in rank to a Marquis. Milord’s responsibilities are going to become bigger. I shall work even harder than before to match this heavy responsibility.”

“…”

“(Wend, didn’t your treatment actually became worse after you were assigned as Margrave?)”

“(I have been feeling something like that as well…)”

Erw’s merciless remark stabbed my delicate heart. Roderich is the sort of person who sees his work as his purpose in life, but I’m not like that. Maybe it’d have been better if I hadn’t become a Margrave?

Still, seeing how I couldn’t have declined it anyway, it’s pointless to think about such hypothetical scenarios. Thus, I started my public works with magic.

---

“Huh? Your Majesty, do you have school today?”

“Yep. Today is the anniversary of the school’s establishment.”

“You sure have a lot of vacations. I’m envious…”

“The time for a demon student at school is long. The curriculum is kept very lax. Lyra has been calling it the Adverse Effect of a Pressure-free Education System.”

“I see…(humans and demons sure come up with the same terminology…)”

A lot of heavy machinery, farm tractors, and railroad cars were busily moving around on Akitsushima Island. The ones operating them were young employees of the demon queen’s company and islanders, as well as my retainers who were currently learning the ropes from the employees.

As expected, the benefits of automation are enormous. The development work here is carried out much more efficiently than on the mainland, where we are using all the magic tools excavated from ancient ruins.

“After all, half of the graduates will be unemployed after going through this long educational period. It might actually be a rather problematic system.”

“Ugh!”

“President, we’re working right now!”

“We’re going to get married soon as well.”

Mall and his friends reacted to the term ‘unemployed’. They have been teaching young islanders how to handle the heavy machinery. They have been acting as if it doesn’t matter to them, but it looks like they actually minded being unemployed for an extended period of time.

Anyway, these guys are genuinely excellent, given that they’ve quickly reached a point where they can teach others to operate the machines. Regardless of Arnest’s usual behavior, he does hate idiots, so Mall’s group wouldn’t have been able to join the seminar if they didn’t have some brains.

“We have been hiring many of the young employees at my company. After teaching them for a short time, we’re putting them to use as magic tool operators, repair crews, and trainers.”

The magic tools used by them have been entirely procured by Lyra-san. Many of them are trash that they repaired and items that were sold to her dirt cheap because they’re old models. Since they are usually easy to use, they have been very popular over here.

“I have various questions about this…”

“I’ll answer whatever I can answer myself.”

“Okay, so why do you have so many magic tools leftover?”

“Simply put, we’re overproducing them.”

All the magic tools moving over here have been dubbed “old models.” And yet you can still use them perfectly fine. Quite a few were inferior in performance to the magic tools from underground ruins, but usually, there was no problem using them. At least, magic tools are definitely faster than using standard tools like pickaxes.

Besides, they’re items we can’t build on the Lingaia Continent right now.

“If you maintain a magic tool properly, it can keep going for several hundred, or even several thousand years, depending on the type.”

“This is nice, I think.”

“Yes.”

A spell called Preservation exists. If you remove the core from magic tools, they are easier to build than the industrial goods and electrical appliances of modern Japan, so you can learn maintenance and repairs quickly if you get a bit of training.

If the core part is broken, it’s busted, but even then, the demon country achieved it through increased productivity and tighter quality control.

“Magic tools that are hard to break…new products which are being produced one after the other. Every year, several new items are presented, but I cannot erase the question of how the current items differ from last year’s competition. I won’t claim that the performance hasn’t improved, but to be honest, the difference is quite small. If the number of demons buying new magic tools decreases, the company will have to lay off people and eventually shut down itself. Of course, the government is troubled by that, so they prohibited the use of older magic tools.”

Officially, they claim they’re doing it because magic tools are dangerous beyond their service lifetime.

In reality, they enforced a replacement of magic tools by law and tried to prevent an increase in unemployment or the collapse of the company itself.

“They keep the economy running by having the people buy magic tools frequently.”

Because of that, a tremendous amount of magic tools becomes garbage, and it takes a large sum to dispose of them while keeping environmental protection in mind.

“The illegal dumping of garbage has turned into a social problem. Even when we pick up the garbage, we won’t earn any complaints; rather, we’ll get thanks. Volunteers at our company are cleaning up trash every day.”

At a glance, they’re doing public service for free, but the demon queen’s company repairs the old tools and sells them to us for a profit.

“Also, we have started to collect waste for free as well.”

This seems to be Lyra-san’s idea. They pick up magic tools, which have exceeded their lifetime, from normal citizens to dispose of them for a small fee. Then they repair those as well, before selling them to us.

“However, Layla mentioned it as well, but it seems like the number of rivals has recently been growing.”

“Eh!? Really?”

So we aren’t the only ones handling things like this. Considering it calmly, it makes a lot of sense, but I was still surprised by this. Still, it’s only logical for people with some wit and the ability to get things done to start this sort of business in the demon country.

“Especially since the Empire got involved. According to rumors, the imperial government has founded dummy companies, using those to do trade with garbage dealers in our country.”

This is something Peter would definitely pull off. While officially getting worn out from fighting with the magic tool guild, he’s buying up secondhand magic tools to use them for development purposes. If he feels like it, he can also lend them out to other nobles, which allows the imperial government to become even more powerful.

“They sure are lucky that the magic tool guild isn’t getting angry.”

“It’s the same for you as well, isn’t it, Margrave Baumeister?”

At first, I only used the magic tools I bought from the demon country on Akitsushima Island, but since we have been lacking magic tools on the mainland, we used some tricks to use those demon magic tools there as well.

Sooner or later, the magic tool guild will probably catch wind of this, but even if they complain about it, I intend to insist that we’re just buying trash from the demons and magic tools that we cannot obtain at the Kingdom’s magic tool guild.

Even Roderich is going along with this bullish position of arguing that they shouldn’t complain if they can’t provide magic tools with the same functions in the first place.

Because we have been burdened with Akitsushima Island in a situation where the development of the Baumeister mainland hasn’t even finished yet, it’s only natural that we lack manpower. Hence, it’s of utmost importance for us to automate as much as possible. Seeing how the magic tool guild cannot provide what we need, we have no choice but to import the tools from elsewhere.

“The Kingdom’s government was the last to pick up on this, but they apparently made their move now as well. It seems like a merchant is gathering oversized garbage as their representative.”

No one is explicitly talking about it, but everyone is thinking the same. Given that the negotiations aren’t going well, thanks to the magic tool guild’s pressure, we have no option but to obtain the demons’ magic tools unofficially.

“It’s illegal, though.”

To be precise, the Helmut Kingdom and Sacred Urquhart Empire have extremely loose laws. Even someone like me can easily find loopholes.

Because there had been just one foreign country thus far, I’d be punished if I selfishly traded with the Empire’s government or nobles, but trading with the demons, who didn’t enter the quotation so far, wasn’t against the law.

The trade negotiations were blocked by the magic tool guilds of both countries, so you couldn’t call it illegal if someone bought magic tools from the demons on their own accord. The magic tool guilds might protest against this, but it’s not like it violates the laws of both countries.

However, I have been buying magic tools at the magic tool guild as long as they had what I was looking for. I was doing that in preparation for the guild’s protests. Though it doesn’t look like it’s been found out yet, seeing how no one has told me.

“I don’t know about the official negotiations, but the number of demons dealing with humans behind the scenes will likely keep growing.”

I have been using my Teleport to meet with the demon queen and Mall’s group, who put the goods into their magic bag. The other merchants can’t use that method, but all of the demons are outstanding magicians. They can put the goods in a magic bag and transfer them all the way to the Lingaia Continent.

Any demon wanting to make a profit should be doing at least that much, the demon queen explained.

“It was a good thing that Lyra and I got to know Margrave Baumeister. Otherwise, Mall and his friends would be forced to fly with magic.”

“Eh? Us?”

“Please let us use a ship at least!”

“No, since it’s likely going to sink, that would be a bit too much…”

As might be expected, even Mall’s group wasn’t intent on traveling to both countries by ship, risking an accident and getting stranded. They learned from their own experience, since we rescued them when they were stranded at sea on a self-built raft.

But these days, they shouldn’t do anything like that, given that they’re going to get married.

“I heard some people even bought old magic airships. Individuals and small companies are likely scheming to do trade with the Lingaia Continent.”

The number of demons and humans moving on their own accord was increasing. I made my move first, then the Kingdom and Empire, and now even nobles of both countries, who are quick on the uptake, are making their moves. Because of that, some people, who were trying to achieve success, were eagerly collecting all the junk.

“Can they buy boats?”

“Wooden boats are cheap, after all.”

Currently, the defense forces seem to rely mainly on metallic magic airships in the demon country. It takes a lot of money and effort to maintain the old wooden airships, and because their magic tools have reached the end of their service lives, it’s impossible to operate them, leading to many ships being abandoned, the demon queen explained.

“Do you want them, Margrave Baumeister?”

“I’ll gladly take all you can get.”

Magic airships are hard to come by over here, so I obviously want as many of them as I can get.

“Well, we’re talking about Lyra here, so I think she’s already gathering them, but I’ll tell her just in case.”

After checking the state of Mall’s group and the dispatched young instructors, the demon queen returned to her farm village with my Teleport.

---

And then, one week later, several hundred medium and small magic airships were lined up on a great field in the Baumeister Margraviate’s mainland.

“What an amazing amount…”

“This is just a part of the total. Our company has secured ten times as much.”

“It’s because of Lyra’s excellence.”

“I see…”

Because of today’s big sale, Lyra-san showed up as well.

“The only regrettable thing about this is that quite a few of the large airships were snatched away by other traders. Even so, I managed to obtain a certain number of them…”

“I won’t buy any large airships. I can introduce you to customers, though.”

The demon queen looked at me, clearly not understanding why I didn’t want to buy the large airships.

“Only the Kingdom’s government is allowed to own large magic airships. The ones who likely snatched the other large airships…”

“Dummy company set up by the Kingdom and Empire, huh…?”

Roderich answered in my stead.

According to the information he gathered, Peter and the Kingdom’s crown prince have been buying special magic tools and such from the demons.

Even though they’re using dummy companies as countermeasures against the magic tool guilds, it’s an open secret at this point, so it won’t be weird for the guilds to complain about this anytime soon.

Since the magic tool guild has been quarreling ever since the guildmaster’s death, that might not be happening anytime soon, though.

“The law forbidding nobles to possess large airships has been around for a long time now, so I cannot afford to break it. I will buy the small and medium airships. But, quite a few of them seem to be rather dangerous to use…”

Many of the ships have deteriorated significantly because they were treated as oversized garbage. Around half of the ships here looked like they’d break apart if you tried to fly with them.

“They’ve been accordingly cheap in return.”

“Well, okay. That’s fair.”

The old airships of the demon country are made of wood and use a design similar to that of the airships on Lingaia. They were likely treated as trash because they’re outdated, but it should be fairly possible for human craftsmen to fix their hulls.

We’re going to build several repair workshops and airship hangars in the margraviate, and then we’ll put the ships in service after repairing and training sailors.

It’s been judged difficult to completely eradicate the serpents on the southern route, which also includes Akitsushima Island. As such, it has become necessary to increase the number of airships. We can also use them to travel and transport goods within our vast territory. And on top of that, they can be used for trade, and people traffic with other noble territories. No matter how many airships there are, it won’t be an issue to put them to work.

“I will try contacting a person who is buying the large airships.”

I took out my MHCD and contacted the crown prince.

『Ooohh! How nice to hear from you, my friend Wendelin!』

“Why is he deliberately stressing the part of him being your friend, Margrave Baumeister?”

Demon Queen, please don’t point that out.

『So, are you going to invite me to some event? I can open up my schedule for you at any time!』

“So desperate…”

Demon Queen, any more…and I’ll start crying because it’s so pathetic (even if the crown prince cannot hear her).

“Actually, there’s something I’d like to discuss with you…”

I brought up the story about the large, magic airships with the crown prince. Thereupon, his tone became very serious.

『The people, whom I asked, reported that they were able to secure quite a few of them, but for Peter-dono to have also moved in addition to you, Wendelin, was unexpected』

As far as the Kingdom was concerned, they had known for a long time that I was making deals with the demons in secret. I’d have been punished if I had procured weapons or dangerous drugs, but when it came to magic tools, which our country doesn’t possess, they’ve been doing the same. It’s a fact that I moved first, but nowadays others are in on this as well. There would be no point in blaming me for this.

“The merchant we asked didn’t know about the law that nobles aren’t allowed to possess large magic airships. Thus, I wanted to introduce her to Your Highness.”

The Margrave Baumeister House has no intention to go against the law. I had to make sure that the crown prince fully understood this part.

『I’ll buy all of them. Regardless of their state. We must get a lead on Peter-dono in this matter. I got scolded by Father about it』

Because they can be used for transport and travel, both countries have been tenacious about securing large airships. It’s something like a competition over the number of battleships by the countries on Earth in the past.

Until just recently, the Kingdom had an overwhelming advantage in this area, but the Empire has caught up by buying old airships from the demons. Nothing less of the guy who won the struggle for the throne in the civil war. Peter’s decision-making speed is astonishing.

Still, for him to move behind the scenes despite them looking troubled by the messy state of the negotiations…

His Majesty and the crown prince cannot fall behind.

“I don’t need an agency fee either.”

『That is very welcome』

Since I’d hate being blamed for having started to trade with the demons before anyone else, I should get the crown prince indebted to me here.

Having such thoughts…does that mean I’ve improved? Or did I go out for wool here, just to come back shorn? It’s hard to tell.

『Let us talk about the details later then』

“I understand.”

After ending the call with the crown prince, I told Lyra-san that he wants to buy the large airships.

“Thank you.”

No, no, it’s enough if I get her to feel indebted to me with this.

“Given that no official trade agreement between the two governments exists, this can be counted as a sort of smuggling. It’s not illegal, but the government won’t back you if things go wrong. The number of humans entering that market will probably increase from now on, but at the same time, swindlers will pop up as well.”

Some people might already have been scammed. It’s not just the humans who deceive others. Swindlers also exist among the demons. Of course, once the trade of weapons, illegal drugs, and slaves starts, the governments of both countries won’t be able to stay silent any longer. Freedom necessitates self-discipline.

“You are quite special in this regard, Margrave Baumeister-dono. I hope His Highness is the same,” Lyra-san said while smiling coolly.

If the monarchy had continued in the demon country, she might have been its prime minister. She’s demonstrating her excellence in the management of their company. But, it looks like she’s deeply worried about being unable to find herself a good man.

At first, Mall and his friends tried to make a pass at her, but once they realized they had no chance, they set their sights on young female demons working at the company. Since they can marry them now, they might actually be quite skilled at communication.

“Lyra.”

“Yes, Your Majesty. Is there anything worrying you?”

“Is our company going to dwindle, seeing how we just trade in second-hand magic tools?”

She has a point. If all the old magic tools are gone, they won’t have much of a choice but to gather magic tools that stop being used every year and sell those. If the number of merchants entering this market increases, it’s possible that Lyra-san will be unable to secure the purchases.

“Accordingly, there’s something I wish to buy from the Baumeister Margraviate.”

“Is there anything among our goods you could sell in the demon country?”

I can only think of metals and food. But it’d be best to wait for the official trade agreement to deal with these.

“Of course there is. The monster domains in my country are all on one island, so the variety of monster types is low. Even if we buy their raw materials, you can hardly make anything out of them.”

For example, the demon clothes use processed fibers and fur produced on large-scale farms. There also exist clothes made from monster materials, but they are expensive and rare.

“The labor costs in our country are higher than in human countries. It’s expensive to deliberately make clothes out of materials obtained through hunting. Since they’re luxury items on top of being high-class, the number of people capable of buying them is low.”

“Won’t that be the same with the monster materials we can get over here?”

“No. You have an extremely large number of monsters that don’t exist in the demon country. If it’s accessories and clothes made out of those, it should meet a demand among a fixed number of rich people.”

“What about the processing techniques?”

“The demon country has become proficient at technology that produces large amounts of clothes with a certain level of quality, but the sewing techniques of professional tailors aren’t that different from those in the human countries. The labor costs in the Kingdom are low, so it will be possible to lower the price a bit and have people from the middle class also buy the products.”

“In this case… It’s going to be that man, huh…?”

“You sure have a lot of acquaintances, Margrave Baumeister-sama.”

Thinking of a person who could be entrusted with that new project, I immediately contacted him.

---

“Heeeeey, how have you guys been doing?”

“…”

“Huh? Ron-chan, you’re here as well? You don’t really have that much interest in fashion, do you? Your fashion sense during our time as newcomer adventurers was so bad that I had to buy things for you to wear. How nostalgic.”

“I was very grateful to you back then…”

That person, although it might be inconvenient for Doushi, was no one other than Candy-san. Be it fashion design, sewing, business, or sales, this man can handle all of it. He should fit Lyra-san’s criteria pretty neatly.

As far as Doushi is concerned, he probably isn’t overly happy with this choice of personnel because Candy-san knows all his past weaknesses and blunders, but…it looks like fixing Doushi’s fashion sense proved to be difficult even for Candy-san.

“Let’s produce a small amount first, and if it’s popular, we can add people. I have the necessary connections.”

Despite his odd appearance for the Kingdom’s standards, Candy-san is acquainted with a lot of people, so he’d order the production of clothes for us.

“Hey, what kind of fashion do demons like?”

“This here is the fashion magazine with the most popular clothes in our country.”

“For you guys to have something like that…the demon country sure is convenient.”

Candy-san flipped through the magazine while looking very interested.

“But, it’s not that different from human fashion. Though it seems like a lot of your clothes are leaning more towards being functional…”

I think the demons’ fashion resembles that of modern Japan. Every year a fashionable color is designated and there exist smaller, seasonal fads. But, there are unexpectedly many people who don’t spend much time on their fashion. Quite a few also wear casual wear or fake jumpsuits like Lumi. Those are regarded as work clothes that are common among working people. Troublesome folks have been misappropriating them as plain clothes. Of course, office workers wear suits, but many also wear them during their days off, albeit without neckties.

“Even though they work in offices, many of them earn a meager salary. I have previously worked in an office as well. The pay was rather bad.”

Lyra-san explained the fashion situation in the demon country.

“Because of that, many people buy cheap clothes. Those are clothes mass-produced by big corporations. The high-class brands are catered towards wealthy people and those who see fashion as a hobby.”

“That’s why we’re going to make clothes with materials you can’t get in the demon country at the same level of quality and sell them at a slightly lower price than the high-class brands. We also have the advantage of tailoring them by hand. People who have settled for having one set of high-quality clothes thus far might be able to buy two or three sets with the same amount of money.”

“It’s going to be second-hand, but we can also provide sewing machines for cheap.”

“Hmm, the magic tool guild will make a fuss about that, so we should refrain from using those for now.”

Actually, sewing machines exist on the Lingaia Continent as well. Their performance is poor, but they’re much faster than sewing by hand. Candy-san himself possesses several of those machines. He told the magic tool guild that he wants a lot more, but he was apparently turned down because their production can’t keep up with the demand.

“They’re trying to block the import from the demon country, despite being unable to sell it themselves…what a truly detestable bunch of people.”

It sounds as though Candy-san doesn’t like the magic tool guild all that much.

“It’s because they’d all become unemployed if magic tools from the demon country were to regularly enter the Kingdom’s market.”

“You have a point there.”

Price, efficiency, and failure rate; there are a few aspects where Lingaia’s magic tools can win against the demon country’s magic tools. At this point, the only thing holding everything back is the magic tool guild’s political power.

“Right now they’re at a dead end, though. After all, their guildmaster, who held a lot of political clout, died the other day.”

“I went to the funeral service, but are they still fighting over the succession to his post?”

“Yep. It seems like a quite stupid thing to do at a time like this, doesn’t it?”

With this ongoing struggle over the succession, they shouldn’t be able to negotiate anything, but since they aren’t that stupid either, they have been continuing to apply pressure on the Kingdom’s government to not import magic tools from the demons.

As a side effect of their internal problems, the production rate has dropped. This shutdown of the magic tool guild is becoming a problem, even for the capital.

“We’re just importing junk, though.”

“It seems like they’re adopting vehicles called Magic Four-Wheelers, which can move without horses, for the army. Those have been imported from the demon country, haven’t they?”

Not only our family, but other nobles and the governments of both countries are actually importing magic tools. All of them are decommissioned vehicles or vehicles planned to soon be decommissioned in the demon country, but it’s inevitable because the magic tool guilds can’t make these.

“Margrave Baumeister-sama, I heard you sold a considerable number of items, which have been excavated from ancient ruins, to the magic tool guild.”

“You sure have good ears, Candy-san.”

“I’m a former adventurer, after all.”

Heavy machinery and vehicles were included as well. They probably bought them from me as research material so they’d be able to make those themselves, but I haven’t heard anything about them having succeeded in building a prototype yet. It’s probably impossible to predict when they might reach such a point.

“That’s why. They’ll be troubled if people tell them to make things themselves if they’re unhappy about the import, so they’ve been tacitly tolerating the import of magic tools they can’t build themselves.”

The highly prideful top brass of the magic tool guild likely can’t admit that they can’t build something.

The same applies to the Empire magic tool guild as well. They should have obtained many of the items Duke Nürnberg excavated during the Civil War, but they haven’t been able to reproduce them thus far. This is the reason why they’re strongly opposing the import of magic tools from the demon country, together with the Kingdom’s magic tool guild.

“You can’t fill your stomach with pride.”

“I agree with Candy-san’s opinion on this.”

Lyra-san doesn’t seem to have any issues with Candy-san, who’s a girl at heart. Maybe it’s not that unusual in the demon country? They might be recognizing the right of such people over there, just like they do in modern Japan.

“If it’s luxury items, it’s better to produce them in small batches. It bears no meaning to mass-produce them.”

“It is a pleasure to see that our thinking aligns.”

Lyra-san appears to consider Candy-san a good trading partner.

“I’ll leave my store in the capital to the daughter of my acquaintance and make the clothes at the tailor workshop in Baulburg.”

---

Candy-san and I decided to build a workshop for order-made clothes, with each of us funding half of the costs. We gathered craftsmen who seemed capable of making goods that would sell in the demon country and added more workshops. This didn’t include just clothes, but also handicrafts, art pieces, accessories, and more.

The scale was small, and the production capacity was low, but those weren’t products destined to compete with mass-produced items in the first place.

I think it’s going to be more than plenty with this much.

---

“Selling those items in the demon country falls into our sphere of action. Given that they will very likely sell since they’re unusual and rare, we will keep searching for other products we can exploit in the same way.”

Just like this, small-scale foreign trade was added to the company of the demon queen and Lyra-san. Keeping the scale small was a measure to prevent the government from taking action against them.

“As we have been doing so far, we will keep collecting magic tools as well. There are many magic tools which have been discarded as it was too much of a hassle for their owners to take them to rubbish dumps, so as long as we sell those after repairing and cleaning them…hehehe…”

“You’re going to make quite a profit, eh?”

Candy-san remained calm, even after watching Lyra-san smiling in an eerie manner.

“The scale of the company with His Majesty at the top keeps growing bigger, and we’re also saving up money. Being able to have a positive outlook for the future is a good thing.”

Their methods are somewhat fishy, but I’m using them as well, and if you apply extreme logic here, you could argue that they’re simply selling junk. Besides, there are many demons who are planning to do the same as Lyra-san, and there are also many humans who desire to do business with them.

This nice opportunity to make a profit will disappear once the governments conclude a trade agreement, so it’s necessary for me to move quickly as Margrave Baumeister. Lyra-san probably also believes that it’s a good chance to gather personnel and assets for the demon queen.

“Once the goods are finished, I will come here to purchase them.”

“We will keep making them. Should I try to call out to other acquaintances?”

Thus, Candy-san became the manager of the tailoring workshop and the other workshops that produced items for the demon country’s market in Baulburg.

I wonder how the relationship with the demons is going to develop from now on? There are many parts we don’t know yet, but even though the top remains still, those at the bottom adopt countermeasures and take byways.

---

“Ron-chan, you should wear different clothes every once in a while. You’re already past forty, aren’t you? I think a calm outfit like this would suit you as well. I’m sure your wives would fall in love with you again.”

“You have my gratitude…”

“Oh my, this does look nice.”

Once the contracts were all signed, Candy-san recommended calm clothes like those worn by adult men to Doushi and forced him to try them on. Maybe they were new products, or maybe Candy-san prepared them for Doushi. Either way…usually Doushi wouldn’t comply with trying on clothes, but Candy-san might be someone akin to a natural enemy for him. He meekly tried on the clothes like a lamb.

“If you had gone on that date with the dancer Sasha-san while wearing such fashionable clothes, she wouldn’t have dumped you back when you were eighteen years old.”

“Telling that story in front of everyone…”

“Also, there was that poster girl from the coffee shop in the southern district. I met her there the other day. She has four children nowadays. Time sure flies. You went to that place every day, despite it being so far away.”

“Please give me a break…”

It looks like Candy-san has a lot of dirt on Doushi. I think I’ll have him tell me some of it in the near future.

+++

# **Chapter 9 – In the End It Seems I am Fated to Continue Getting more Wives**

“Good day. Thank you very much for the invitation. Even so, I must say, you’re quite amazing, Margrave Baumeister.”

“What’s so amazing about me?”

“You will find almost no demons who own a private beach.”

The number of deals between the Baumeister House and the company run by the demon queen continued to increase. Today, the demon queen, Lyra-san, Mall, and his friends followed my invitation and came to our usual private beach.

Elise and my wives were also present. We were swimming in the sea, doing barbecue, and playing beach volleyball.

The demon queen wore a pink swimsuit with the form of a dress. It looked very lovely on her. At the very least, it didn’t give one the impression of her being a demon queen.

Even so, she’s the person with the biggest mana capacity among those I met. However, I’ve never seen her use magic

Maybe she can’t use magic? No, that cannot be. She simply might have no opportunity to use her magic back in the demon country.

“Is something the matter, Margrave Baumeister?”

“Your Majesty, don’t you use magic?”

“I use it rarely, but usually I’ll depend on magic tools. There exists magic that has been passed down in the royal family. Every once in a while, I practice that magic with Lyra.”

“Even if you might have lost your power as a ruler, training the legendary magic of the royal family is indispensable.”

Wearing a violet bikini which emphasized her top-notch figure, Lyra-san explained the circumstances.

“Is that magic passed down through books or something like that?” Katharina asked Lyra-san, as someone possessing a lot of interest in the matter of magic.

“Yes, it’s one of the many heirlooms left behind by the royal family.”

“It must be quite valuable.”

“No, written copies were sold at bookshops. We own the real one, but leaving aside its cultural value, its monetary value isn’t…well, it’s treated more like an ancient document.”

Even books describing the treasured magic of the royal family don’t fetch much of a price in the demon country, huh? Somehow, it’s quite saddening.

“In the first place, only a few people can learn the royal family’s magic, and on top of that, there’s no one actively trying to learn it either. It’s simply of little use in today’s demon society. So, at most, unemployed people with lots of spare time might bother, I guess?”

“””_twitch_”””

Mall and his friends reacted to Lyra-san’s explanation. Have those three possibly learned the magic of the royal family during their period of unemployment?

“Margrave Baumeister, the royal family’s magic is impossible with our mana capacity!”

Mall and his friends’ mana capped out at the intermediate level, so it seems they cannot use the special royal magic.

“What sort of magic is it?”

“Since it’s something used by the demon king, it’s a spell allowing you to blast away an enemy army or something like that, I’d say.”

“It’s called royal magic, but it’s basically an area-affecting annihilation spell.”

Once I heard Ramul and Sylas’s explanation, I could see why it might have no use in today’s demon country. It’s pretty clear that using such a spell in an inhabited area would cause a lot of trouble. Or rather, it’d be still okay if it were just treated as trouble. In the worst case, it might be seen as a terrorist attack.

“The royal magic is something you use in critical situations. I’ve been training it on a regular basis and will use it without hesitation, if the need should ever arise.”

“What a wonderful resolve, Your Majesty.”

Lyra-san was the only one being deeply moved when the demon queen declared her determination while throwing out her very humble chest. Going by the standards of the Lingaia Continent, they make for a beautiful picture of a lord and her retainer, but the demons likely regard this as outdated thinking.

“Having said that, it’s unnecessary in the current era. It will likely end with me and my children merely memorizing the spell.”

“Well, you’d be arrested if you fired it off in the city.”

Yeah, she’d definitely be sent to jail for murder and damage to property if she did something like that. Even I can tell as much.

“I don’t think you need to learn it anyway, Margrave Baumeister.”

“You mean because I can already use magic with a lot of firepower?”

“Correct. Its incredible firepower is its sole feature. Therefore, it makes little to no difference to the big spell advanced magicians as you use.”

“I see. So, has your mana capacity already stopped growing, Your Majesty?”

Arnest, who was participating in our little outing, asked the demon queen. He wore a striped body-suit swimwear, covering his body from the neck to the knees and elbows.

“No, I’m still young. Besides, it seems like I have a relatively big mana pool among the many generations of demon kings. At present, I have already exceeded the average mana capacity of all past demon kings.”

“That is truly incredible.”

“Professor Arnest, you too possess a considerable mana capacity, don’t you?”

“It is not really that useful for my research. The only time when I felt thankful for having such a big mana pool was when I crossed over to this continent, I suppose.”

Considering all that, you cooperated with Duke Nürnberg quite a bit, didn’t you? You operated his device to obstruct magic.

Despite Arnest’s usual behavior, his mana capacity ranks among the top three in the demon country, so it’s kind of amazing that he seriously considers his own mana pool as ‘not really that useful.’

“But, it’s incredible that there are people with more mana than Wend.”

“It is!”

Luise and Doushi were surprised by Arnest’s mana capacity. Doushi’s mana pool was slightly smaller than mine. However, given that it was still growing despite him being beyond forty, you can definitely label Doushi as a special case.

“I just thought of this, but won’t you match your vessel with Arnest’s, Margrave Baumeister-sama?”

“I don’t want to do that with Arnest.”

If I had to answer why, it’s mostly an emotional issue. Besides, I’ll likely exceed Arnest’s mana in a few more years.

“I do not want to do it either!”

Even Doushi doesn’t want to match his vessel with Arnest either. Yep, this is no rational issue, but an emotional one.

“In that case, will you do it with me?”

“I’m not sure about it, to be honest.”

“Why? For the demons of old, mana was the source of power and riches. Ancient documents mention that they requested a vessel matching the demons, who possessed a bigger mana capacity than their own, even if they had to lower their head for it.”

Does that mean they even asked hostile demons? It sounds like they’ve been using vessel matching a lot more openly than humans.

“There’s a custom among humans…”

I explained to the demon queen that humans wouldn’t match vessels across genders unless they’re family or in a relationship.

“I think we should respect each other’s culture and customs. In that case, the vessel matching with Arnest…”

“No!”

“Absolutely not!”

Doushi and I strongly refused to match our vessels with Arnest.

“You certainly appear to be unpopular, Professor Arnest.”

“I have been merely walking the path of genuine research.”

Of course, it’s not only that. Another reason is that he also gave us a lot of trouble during the final stage of the civil war. Anyway, I hate the idea of matching my vessel with Arnest.

“No helping it, if you don’t want to. I’m going to play beach volleyball. Fujiko, Lulu, Philine!”

“Aye!”

“Coming!”

“Let’s decide on the teams.”

The three children were going to play beach volleyball with the demon queen.

“Wendelin-sama, thank you very much for the new swimsuit.”

“Sure, but don’t show it to Margrave Breithilde.”

“Okay.”

I gave Philine a light-green dress-type swimsuit, but even such a modest swimsuit goes way beyond this world’s strict dress code for women. Since I might be scolded if she showed it to her father, I asked her to wear it only when we were together at this private beach.

“Alriiiiight! Let’s go! Secret Skill: Demon Queen Serve!”

The four girls started playing with the demon queen, and Fujiko played against Lulu and Philine. The demon queen had the first serve. The name of her technique sounded a bit scary, but it was just a plain serve without any mana loaded into it. Lulu received it easily, and Philine returned it to the other side of the field. Fujiko received that ball in return, and so on.

It’s great that all four of them are quite athletic.

“It’s quite difficult to move on the sand. You don’t seem to have many problems with it, though, Lulu.”

“I’ve lived on a sand beach for a long time, after all. But, it’s my first time playing volleyball.”

Because the village where Lulu used to live was built on a sandy beach, she didn’t struggle to move in the sand. Given that she had to always rush over whenever a serpent appeared to repel it, her muscles naturally adapted.

Nothing less of a southern girl.

The swimsuit she was wearing today was one of Candy-san’s creations. It was a light-blue dress-type.

“Is that so? We have all sorts of sports games in our country.”

“Don’t you have any wars?”

“Fujiko, are you hailing from a belligerent country or something?”

“Since I heard that you’re demons, I thought that you were always fighting.”

The demons in the books, which Fujiko read at home, apparently constantly fought over who was going to rule their land.

“Fujiko, such demons only existed several ten thousand years ago.”

However, when the demon queen got appalled by Fujiko bringing up such an ancient story, the ball plopped down in her blind spot.

“Yay! Eat my feint toss!”

“Whaaa───! That’s unfair! Philine! Use the Date family’s hidden Save technique!”

“Eyy!”

“Not bad! Lulu, you too!”

The four girls had fun playing volleyball while chatting. Other than those four, Lyra-san was drinking a tropical juice while lying on a beach chair to heal her fatigue from everyday’s work, Arnest was writing a report on an underground ruin he had explored (yes, even at a time like this), and Mall’s group was watching the barbecue.

“Sensei, the meat is done.”

“The fish as well.”

“The shrimps and shells look so tasty.”

Agnest, Cindy, and Betty were actively offering me the grilled food while wearing swimsuits made for them by Candy-san.

![](file:////tmp/wps-alejandro/ksohtml/wpszEgW92.png) 

Being invited to this private beach and receiving exclusive swimsuits from the Margrave Baumeister House basically carried that sort of meaning. Roderich has also been pestering me because of their significant contributions to the development of my territory, and thus, it was decided that they’d officially marry into my family.

All of them, except Agnes, are adults, and since it’s already set in stone, their families have opened branch stores of their businesses in Baulburg. Moreover, it’s planned to open branch stores on Akitsushima Island as well. On top of that, the three girls will be responsible for this network of branch stores.

Of course, they won’t have the time to personally get involved with the management of the franchise, so they’ll be figureheads, just like Luise and Ina. Instead, their relatives and veteran employees, who have been working for their families for many years, will be handling the actual work.

“Sensei, it seems like the sunglasses are selling well to adventurers who are active in the Demon Forest. The sunlight over here is strong, after all. Some of the fishermen are buying them, too. But, it looks like glasses are unusual on Akitsushima Island.”

“Now that you mention it, I certainly didn’t see any glass-wearers on Akitsushima Island.”

It might be that glasses are simply unusual because the island was embroiled in many smaller skirmishes and wars for a long time.

“The flowers are selling well, I hear. The people of that island seem to do what’s called Flower Arrangement, just like the Mizuho people.”

Cindy’s flower store seemed quite promising. The Mizuho people were the same in this regard, but the islanders would buy unusual flowers from outside the island to use them for their flower arrangements. In reverse, the rare flowers growing in the Mizuho Dukedom and on the Akitsushima Island were selling well in the Kingdom.

The number of farms cultivating seeds and seedlings for export has recently grown. Many noble women liked gardening as a hobby, so their seeds and seedlings sold well, too.

“We have also increased the number of branch stores. Since it’d be prone to fail if onii-san were to be involved with it, Rosa-san is handling all of it.”

“That should be a relief, I guess.”

To begin with, restaurants are a business with lower expenses, depending on how you do things. The Akitsushima and Mizuho people──they are of the same ethnic group, but given their strained relationship, they will be offended if you lump them together──appear to be interested in foreign cooking, so Rosa-san had opened several branch stores in Mizuho and on Akitsushima Island.

Moreover, she only entrusted Betty’s big brother with the main restaurant in the capital and the development of new dishes. It’s because she suspected that adding him to the management wouldn’t lead to any decent results. Though I actually think so as well.

“Sensei, it must be hard for you as well with the upcoming wedding ceremonies.”

“Well, it’s mostly because we have to adhere to their customs.”

In addition to my three pupils, I’m also going to marry Ryouko, Yuki, and Yui for the sake of a stable rule of Akitsushima Island. I will have a child with Ryouko, the sole lady of the island’s most prominent Akitsushima family, and have that child become the next family head of the Akitsushimas. The same applies to Yuki, the head of the Hosogawa family, and to Yui, the only daughter of the Matsunaga family.

Roderich said that the same fate awaits Fujiko once she becomes an adult. When I asked him whether he couldn’t decrease the number a bit, he told me he’d rather increase the number of my wives.

『Almost all of the former lord families on Akitsushima Island have declared they would offer a wife to you, Milord. I somehow managed to contain the number of wives to this level. In return, Friedrich-sama and those coming after him will be forced to accept their demands to an extent…』

If the government of Akitsushima Island doesn’t stabilize, the Baumeister House might be crushed in the future. If I have to marry in order to prevent that, it cannot be helped.

Then again, we’re talking about Roderich here. He’s probably trying to establish our family’s dominance on the island by mediating preferential marriages with families that contribute to the land’s rule.

Most recently, Roderich has become so experienced that I sometimes think he’s some sort of prime minister of a major power.

『Anyway, we cannot exclude the three mentioned before. If things go badly, it could lead to a rebellion』

Basically, it means someone blood-related to the Margrave Baumeister, the overall ruler of the land, will be assigned as the top of the island for all coming generations. It’s a full-fledged, political marriage, but Roderich called this a duty of high-ranking nobles.

“Thou sure have it tough.”

“On the other hand, you have it good, don’t you?”

“Right? I told you, didn’t I, Wendelin? The status of royalty of higher nobility is nothing more than a bundle of duties and obligations. Some people go crazy from all those obligations, no matter how skilled they might be. Just like Max did. Wendelin, make sure not to get crushed by it.”

“Don’t worry. I’m not that ambitious anyway.”

I’d consider it odd to start a rebellion just to push my will through like Duke Nürnberg. After all, I believe it’s fine for me to be a stupid lord who only serves as a figurehead.

“Luckily, thou hast Roderich at thine side, Wendelin. Even in the Empire, that man would have been qualified for the post of prime minister. Thou hast not the qualities necessary to become a tyrant, so thou can adhere to calmly planning things.”

“If I don’t do that, I won’t be able to handle matters. At this point, the Baumeister Margraviate is like a small country.”

In the future, our territory should exceed the Breithilde, Browig, and Holmia Margravates. Our relationship with the Kingdom is also important. And our connections to the Empire and the Mizuho Dukedom will also play a role.

Then again, I don’t have much clue about diplomacy. I think I’ll keep outsourcing it to Roderich altogether.

“So, I heard thou won’t be inviting many people to the ceremonies.”

“It’s because the ceremonies won’t be held at a church.”

Although they have been declining in recent years, the Akitsushima family itself is a family of priests. Because of their Shinto-like religion, it’d cause a big backlash on the island if we held the ceremonies according to the Church’s customs. That’s why we plan to hold wedding ceremonies that fully comply with the rules of Akitsushima Island.

Currently, Matsunaga Hisahide is pooling his efforts into the preparations. The wedding ceremonies will be held on the island, and only a limited number of people will be invited.

“Given those circumstances, my uncle won’t be attending either.”

“I see. I guess it’d be asking too much for Cardinal Hohenheim to participate in the wedding ceremony of a different faith.”

“That is one part of it, but if he attended, he would also be put in a position where he would need to pressure them into converting to our religion.”

That would probably cause a backlash by the residents of Akitsushima Island. Knowing all that, the church won’t send any of its members.

“They’re using the excuse that it’s ultimately a family matter of the Baumeister House,” Elise explained.

“I suppose that would be the smartest way to go about it,” Therese commented.

“His Highness the Crown Princess will be present, though.”

“…That man has really taken a liking to thou, hasn’t he, Wendelin?”

I think it’s rare to find someone who has virtually no friends despite having no reason to be disliked.

I’ve explained to His Majesty and His Highness that this time’s marriage was aimed at securing a stable government of Akitsushima Island for the Baumeister House. As far as the royal family was concerned, they had no objections to this.

The reason is the discovery of an uninhabited continent around 300 kilometers south of Akitsushima Island. The Lingaia, which had been sent east to explore, also found many islands and land.

Many monster domains exist on the continent, and its full extent is unclear as of yet, but the Kingdom’s policy has been set. They’ll leave the troublesome ethnic groups to the Baumeister House, while they will concentrate on occupying and developing the new uncharted lands.

“Usually, His Highness the Crown Prince would be forced to rule the island after marrying Ryouko, Yuki, and Yui. But now Wendelin seems to be doing it in his stead. It’s only natural for him to be grateful.”

As far as the Kingdom is concerned, they can simply reap the benefits from the Akitsushima Island, which has been stabilized by the Baumeister House. I think it’s only logical for the crown prince to take part in the ceremony.

“Also, Margrave Breithilde-sama and Margrave Browig-sama will be present too.”

The Holmia House is currently busy because of the demons, and since we aren’t particularly close to them either, I didn’t invite them.

“It’s apparently going to be a wedding ceremony with an unusual format, so I should observe it in preparation for the future.”

Actually, the demon queen and Lyra-san plan to attend as well.

Seeing how a new continent has been discovered, the Kingdom’s expansion is going to continue for a good while. So far, the trade negotiations with the demons are at a standstill, but my trade of magic tools, which can’t be built by the magic tool artisans on the Lingaia continent, has become an open secret at this point.

The Kingdom apparently wants to obtain and study magic guns and cannons in the future, but they won’t be able to obtain such items through the trade routes used by Lyra-san and the other demons. Such weapons are being strictly managed in the demon country. And Lyra-san likely wouldn’t put herself in danger of getting arrested to smuggle weapons either. I mean, she can earn more than enough of a profit by simply selling repaired junk, and scrapped or second-hand vehicles, as well as ships.

“Three big nobles are aiming to obtain vehicles and ships, huh?”

“They can’t build them themselves, after all.”

I sold the vehicles I got from the underground warehouse to the magic tool guild, but it sounds like their research is somehow stuck. There’s no way technology will progress so easily, so it’s inevitable that something like this will happen.

Though I must admit I’d like them to at least produce some results, given that they have the actual goods as a reference on hand.

“I’m looking forward to the wedding ceremonies.”

Lyra-san’s eyes were filled with joy. I’m sure she’s expecting this to be a good opportunity to make some profit.

---

And then, one month after the beach party, the wedding ceremonies between me and Ryouko, Yuki, and Yui were held on Akitsushima Island. The ceremonies were performed in the renovated and expanded shrine of Otsu. The rituals were very similar to those in Japanese wedding ceremonies. Ryouko, Yuki, and Yui wore white kimonos and head-dresses.

“My dear husband, please take care of me for the rest of our lives.”

“Please take care of me as well. But, are you okay with this?”

“Yes. Back when I led my troops against Kanenaka, I was very worried and anxious. You saved me from this situation when you suddenly descended from the sky. I’m happy that I can now become your wife.”

Ryouko must have been very insecure and anxious as the family’s figurehead.

“I also felt very relieved at that time. After all, I cannot use any magic.”

The Hosokawa family, which has assisted the Akitsushima family for many generations, thrives on knowledge and education, but, in turn, it has had unusually few members capable of using magic.

I guess it means I came to their rescue just as they were worried they wouldn’t be able to repel Kanenaka, who excelled in the military arts.

“Then again, given my role, you were the only one treating me as a woman, Milord.”

With Ryouko being demanded to show generosity since she was a figurehead, Yuki had to occasionally steel her heart. Even now, she’s still respected by the retainers and residents, but they also fear her. This is probably also why you didn’t hear anything about a romantic relationship with Yuki.

“Therefore, I’m quite happy right now.”

“I see. So am I.”

In my eyes, Yuki is easy to talk to. She has been assisting me well.

“I’m just an extra to Ryouko-sama and Yuki-san.”

At some point, Yui had emerged as the third woman. But, I guess it’s no wonder, seeing how she’s the daughter of Matsunaga Hisahide, who not only is a magician and lord but also managed to survive the treacherous world of the central area.

“My father will be happy as long as Akitsushima Island becomes stable and continues to develop from now on. The child born to me is going to become the next head of the Matsunaga family, so he has been very strict in his demands to my future husband…”

Despite appearances, Hisahide is very doting on his daughter. Because of that, he set the bar very high for the husband of his darling daughter.

“At one point, Miyoshi Yoshitsugu-sama wished for me to become his wife, but Father turned him down.”

I wonder just how high his standards had been to reject a marriage with the child of his former lord.

“You being present at that time was a big help, Your Lordship. We are well aware of your circumstances that might make it hard for you to visit the island frequently. But, whenever you visit, the three of us will do our very best to welcome you warmly.”

I wonder whether there are many level-headed women like Yuki on Akitsushima Island.

“It’s not Earl Baumeister anymore, but Margrave Baumeister, huh? Oh well, whatever. One day I’ll overtake you and become the lord of this island!”

“Humph!”

“Master…that hurt.”

“We are in the middle of an important ceremonial occasion! Behave yourself!”

“Yes…”

Instead, there are many idiots among the men of this island?

That simpleton, Sou Yoshitoshi, showed up and got hit by Doushi’s fist for being rude. Behind him were the three delinquent girls.

“Having said that, I cannot win against my first obstacle, my master, at present!”

“Of course!”

I doubt a human capable of that has been born yet. I suppose Yoshitoshi and the three girls won’t think of anything stupid while Doushi is in good health.

“For now, you’ve been entrusted with the island, so we have splurged on the congratulatory gifts.”

That was no exaggeration either. Yoshitoshi and the three girls were carrying a huge load of gifts.

“Why are you guys so rich?”

“It’s because of the high demand for parrots!”

The former lords, whose only redeeming feature was their military arts, lost their purpose on Akitsushima Island after it became peaceful. Their talent as civil officials was unknown, so many of them moved over to the monster island, where Lulu used to live, trying to make a living like Yoshitoshi and the three delinquent girls. They were using their excess power to hunt monsters.

Nowadays, a new village has been built on the site where Lulu’s village stood. Yoshitoshi and the others spent their days there, training and going out on subjugations.

The feathers of the parrots, which inhabited the island in ridiculously large numbers, were so popular as material for making high-class clothes and beddings that even Lyra-san was buying them.

“You earned that much?”

“No matter how many we get, it’s never enough. And, no matter how many parrots we kill, they never run out!”

That monster domain is a paradise for parrots, after all. Since adventurers will have the tables turned on them if things go badly, Yoshitoshi’s group is probably valued highly for being able to hunt down many of those parrots.

“Okay, so you’ll be staying on that island for a while then?”

“Using the buildings of the old village is harsh. We’re going to build a new house since we have enough money.”

I’d say they’re doing pretty well to be able to build houses so suddenly.

“Well, the number of people living there has grown.”

“Hehehe, we’re going to accumulate riches on that island and use that to retake our home island one day.”

“I will raise plenty of children and then march on Akitsushima someday!”

“Be happy and spend your time peacefully while you still can!”

I understood everything from the statements of the three delinquent girls. At the same time, happiness welled up in me as well. I had never expected him to win over those three girls. Yoshitoshi is an idiot, but he might be an unexpectedly good guy.

“Wend, are you sure?”

“Isn’t it fine?”

Luise was worried, but as long as they say whatever they want to say like this, it’s going to be okay. If they really plan to start a rebellion, they wouldn’t be so open about it.

“His Highness is currently in the middle of business talks with Lyra-san?”

“So it seems.”

The three big shots, whom I introduced to Lyra-san, immediately went into action and are now talking about something with her while looking all serious.

At present, it’s popular to engage in private trade with the demons through independent routes in the Kingdom and Empire. Any high-ranking noble who didn’t get involved in this business at this point would be deemed a blockhead.

No matter how much the government struggled with the negotiations, noble territories are like independent countries. But the nobles belong to the Kingdom or Empire. Even if they do private trade with the demons, there are rules they must abide by.

It’s not like those rules are written down somewhere; if you import weapons, for example, you cannot complain if they’re interpreted as inciting insurrection. Actually, several noble houses requested weapons from demons, but it seems like the Kingdom immediately launched an investigation.

If they actually bought any, they’ll definitely lose their current peerage. Apparently, this happened to some noble families in the Empire, who tried to import weapons from the demons. Then again, it appears those nobles were tricked by the demons and only had their money stolen.

Lyra-san mentioned that, recently, shady demons had begun participating once the private trade with humans proved profitable.

Making a profit without being deceived is a part of your capability as a noble or royal.

“Wend, it’s about time.”

“Got it.”

At last, the Akitsushima-style wedding ceremony is going to start for real. Once the three brides and the groom showed up, a few dozen shrine maidens started to dance on the shrine’s ground to offer their respects to the gods.

“Ryouko, you’re not going to dance because you’re one of the brides?”

“I will show my dancing later, if you wish. It’s not like dancing is just a job to those shrine maidens.”

With the Akitsushima family serving as head priest, the shrines, which had been split up thus far, were reorganized under the Otsu shrine as the main shrine. The best shrine maidens gathered from all over the island, performing today’s dedication dance, but most of them were daughters of wealthy merchants, village chiefs, wealthy farmers, or former lords.

“Today, a festival is also being held in front of the shrine. Since the island has been unified, many people have gathered. It’s also an opportunity for the shrine maidens to show themselves off to the men.”

Shrines accept unmarried women as shrine maidens, and the women are taught many things while also being trained to become good wives. During festivals, those shrine maidens would be asked to dance. If a man saw one and took a liking to her, he could request a marriage interview with the shrine. If the woman agreed, they’d have a marriage interview, and if both gave their okay, it’d lead to a marriage.

“Even if the first wife is decided through political marriages, it often happens that men find a concubine or two in this setting.”

I guess that means it’s a chance for the women to become concubines to an influential lord. Many of the shrine maidens were pretty, and their dances were elegant and charming.

“Dear, do you see a girl who fancies you?”

“Hahaha, I just thought they’re pretty while watching them dance.”

![](file:////tmp/wps-alejandro/ksohtml/wpssXRyRP.png) 

Seriously…please spare me from getting any more wives.

Once the dedication dance ended, a priest offered a prayer and then had us do the three-times-three exchange of nuptial cups. This part closely resembled the ceremony between Erw and Haruka. But I guess that’s only natural since Haruka is from the same ethnic group.

“As of now, you four have become married in front of the gods.”

The wedding ceremonies held on Akitsushima Island, alongside the festival for the renovated shrine, were a huge success. The island’s residents rejoiced over the newfound peace and positively accepted their new ruler.

There is probably still a lot to do, but with this, the Baumeister Margraviate is fully set. I decided to do my best for a bit longer so I could quietly retire as soon as possible.

# **Extra – Maids are Immortal and Indestructible!**

I’m soon going to become an adult, and to match that, it’s planned for my wedding ceremony with Erwin-sama to be held. When it comes to marriages, the husband and wife are busy running around to prepare everything. But, Erwin-sama is a chief vassal of the Margrave Baumeister House and thus very busy with his duties. Hence, I must do my best to cover for him as his future wife. This is what you call a wife’s duty, according to Haruka-sama.

Dominique-nee-san and I took advantage of Master teleporting and headed to Candy-san’s tailor shop in the capital. I ordered a wedding dress for my wedding, so I had to come in to try it on.

As I watched the custom-made wedding directly in front of my eyes, it finally hit me that I’m going to be married soon.

“How beautiful…”

“It’s a big moment that only happens once in your life, Lea-chan. I sewed the dress for you while pouring my heart into it.”

“As expected of you, Candy-san. You’re a very skilled tailor. Ah, but there are also people who don’t keep it to once in their lives.”

“Humph!”

“Ouch, that hurts…Dominique-nee-san.”

“Don’t say such an ill omened thing!”

“Now, now, Dominique-chan, she does have a point. It’s true that some people end up marrying twice, thrice…or even more times in their lives. But…despite his outward appearance, Erwin-chan is a kind man.”

“True.”

“…Lea. Didn’t you just hint at the possibility that you won’t keep it to once in your life?”

“Ultimately, I just talked about society. I’m going to become a fine wife for Erwin-sama.”

“That’s the spirit! Lea-chan, I’m going to root for you as well.”

“Thank you, Candy-san.”

Once I put on Candy-san’s handmade wedding dress, I can also become a good wife.

“Okay, let’s put it on right away, and I’ll make the finer adjustments.”

“You two are really getting along well, don’t you…? By the way, haven’t you gained weight again, Lea?”

“It’s alright. I made a diet in preparation for the wedding ceremony.”

However, it wasn’t a half-assed diet like the ones Katharina-sama does, where she talks about sweets going into another stomach or postpones the actual dieting. I actually lost weight by working out. After all, I frequently took on work that requires a lot of stamina.

“…Working out, huh? What about your food?”

“Haha! Naturally I decreased my meal portions and I also lowered the amount of snacks…as much as possible.”

In the end, I lost weight, so isn’t it fine?

Candy-san went out of his way to sew a dress for me, so I got all motivated and went on a diet so that the dress wouldn’t be tight or unwearable.

“True. Lea-chan, you’ve become quite slender.”

“Please leave it to me. I’m a maid who will properly get things done when it counts.”

I’m different from Dominique-nee-san, who still hasn’t returned to her figure from before her pregnancy!

“Humph!”

“Ouch…”

“I can immediately tell what you’re thinking in that little bird brain of yours.”

Just because I thought about it to myself…why…?

Anyway, it’s going to be my once-in-a-lifetime moment, so the wedding dress has to be adjusted perfectly.

Hmm, it’s somewhat loose. I guess you can call my diet a wonderful success.

“You two sure are close. …Oh my, it looks very nice on you, doesn’t it, Lea-chan?”

“Nothing less of you, Candy-san. It’s a dreamy dress.”

A wedding dress is the dream of every woman. Next week I’m going to marry Erwin-sama while wearing this.

“You often hear that fine feathers make fine birds, and I must admit it suits you really nicely.”

“Dominique-nee-san, is that supposed to be praise?”

“Of course. Finally, you’re going to marry as well. It’s deeply moving.”

I feel like she’s toying with me, though…

“All that’s left are a few adjustments…okay, I used pins for the adjustment, so take it off carefully, okay?”

“Candy-san, you’re really a professional.”

I don’t think there are many people around who can sew wedding dresses. I hear he used to be an outstanding adventurer who exceeded Doushi-sama. I guess you could call him the living proof that talent isn’t distributed evenly.

“Thanks to that, my reputation is good, so I’ve been getting lots of orders lately. But, you know…”

“Is there any trouble, Candy-san?”

Did he get some sort of absurd demand from a noble customer? In that case, he could consult our Master and Doushi-sama about it. I’m sure they’d act on Candy-san’s behalf.

“It’s not that sort of trouble. Rather, I simply got too many orders and have to turn down some.”

“If that’s the case, what exactly is worrying you?”

Dominique-nee-san asked Candy-san.

“You see…I’ve become skilled enough to sew wedding dresses, but I won’t ever get the chance to wear one in my life, will I…? Life is really unfair.”

“”…””

Even Dominique-nee-san couldn’t be irresponsible here and promise him that he’d wear a wedding dress at some point. I think Candy-san is more suited to be a bride than anyone else, when it comes to his personality, but…life is truly unfair.

---

“Lea-san, this is the flower list. This time, we have gathered many special types. Quite a few flowers haven’t arrived at the store yet, but it’s planned for all of them to be here by the day before your wedding ceremony.”

“That’s an awfully big number of different flower types.”

“Just as it was with Anna-san’s wedding, the ceremony and banquet can’t be too flashy, so Haruka-sama asked us to prepare plenty of flowers.”

“As expected of Haruka-sama.”

“I’d like you to also prepare various types of flowers for when I marry Sensei.”

Given that Haruka-sama and Anna-san were very busy with the preparations for my wedding ceremony, Dominique-nee-san and I went out to the Baulburg branch of the flower shop run by Cindy-san’s family to check on the flowers that would be used for the ceremony and the banquet.

Since we informed them in advance of our visit, Cindy-san waited for us at the store and handled our business.

“Dominique-nee-san, is the work at the mansion okay?”

“Since it’s Erwin-sama’s wedding ceremony, Elise-sama told me to help you for a while.”

“Elise-sama sure is a kind person.”

“Yes, she is.”

Certainly, Elise-sama’s heart is as big as her chest. No wonder that she’s being hailed as a saint in the capital.

“If there are this many types of flowers, the ceremony is definitely going to become very gorgeous.”

I’m Erwin-sama’s concubine, so the wedding ceremony won’t be as extravagant as Haruka-sama’s wedding with Erwin-sama. Rather, it’s planned as a cosy celebration with Master and his wives at the mansion.

It would be great to have plenty of decorations and pretty flowers on the table.

“However, they do not have any Sparkle of Newlywed Wife!”

“””Whoa, you startled me!”””

Being suddenly addressed by Doushi-sama in this flower shop…might have been slightly bad for my heart.

“Doushi-sama, is Sparkle of Newlywed Wife a flower name?”

“It is an alias. The flower is said to glow golden when it blooms, and it is quite popular at wedding ceremonies!”

“You sure know a lot about flowers, Doushi-sama…”

Dominique-nee-san looked surprised, but Doushi-sama regularly gives flowers to his wives. So, even if it’s somewhat unexpected, it makes sense that he knows a bit about flowers.

“How do you know about this, Lea?”

“I met him several times at this store.”

He apparently comes here to buy unusual southern flowers you can only get at this branch store. I think Master would do well to follow Doushi-sama’s example. He’s kind and gives his wives all kinds of gifts, but for some reason, many of his presents are food. I think it would be better to give flowers to women!

Ah! Erwin-sama…will be okay since he’s going to start doing this from now on.

“The range of your connections surprises me each and every time…Cindy-san, the Sparkle of Newlywed Wife isn’t on this list, is it?”

“No, it’s not. It’s very popular, but it’s also extremely hard to obtain. In addition, Sparkle of Newlywed Wife is bad with warmer temperatures.”

“In other words, it’s near impossible to get your hands on it in Baulburg, huh?”

“That’s how it is. It’s unfortunate, but we couldn’t include it on the list.”

“I see…I guess that makes sense.”

I have never seen a Sparkle of Newlywed Wife either, but given its name, it might be a flower suitable for a wedding ceremony.

It’s quite a bummer that my wedding ceremony won’t have any.

“A Sparkle of Newlywed Wife? Those are natively growing in the Baumeister Margraviate!”

“Eh? Really? Neither the employees nor I have heard anything about that.”

“That is no wonder, Cindy-jou! After all, I discovered them by chance when I explored the Baumeister Margraviate!”

As usual, Doushi-sama loves to explore. And thus, he managed to even find a place where the Sparkle of Newlywed Wife grows.

“Doushi-sama, I must take my hat off for you finding Sparkle of Newlywed Wife in a warm place like the Baumeister Margraviate.”

“It is true that the south is rather hot, but that does not apply in the upper parts of the mountains! Sparkle of Newlywed Wife’s are growing en masse up there!”

I see. If it’s the mountains, the air up there is cool. I guess it won’t be weird for Sparkle of Newlywed Wife to grow up there.

“But Doushi-sama, it’s quite challenging to go pick those flowers up in the mountains. Monsters could be living there, too.”

It’s just as Cindy-san says. Speaking of famous mountains in the Baumeister Margraviate, there’s the Great League Mountains. That place is infested with wyverns and other flying dragons.

It’s not a place where you can easily pick flowers, and the number of days until the ceremony is limited, too. Also, because there’s a lot of other preparation to do, everyone is busy.

“It is another mountain, not the Great League Mountains. That place is safe because no monsters live there! As long as you invest one day to pick them up, it will be more than enough time! You should strike while the iron is still hot!”

“Ah, that is the Mizuho proverb which Haruka-sama taught you, isn’t it?”

“Lea, Dominique, you can choose the flowers you like on-site!”

“Me too?”

I heard from Elise that you will be helping Lea until the wedding ceremony.”

“Elise-sama…”

“Well then, let us be off!”

“E───eh! Even if there might be no monsters there, it’s dangerous for you to take two amateurs there! I’ll go as well!”

Doushi-sama promptly decided to collect some Sparkles of Newlywed Wife’s. He put Dominique-nee-san and me, who could actually move relatively freely until the ceremony, into a huge basket he took out of his magic bag and then flew off to the south while carrying the basket.

“Doushi-sama, we’re going so faaaast!”

Cindy-san came after us with her flight magic, but for him to fly even faster than her while carrying the basket with us two…nothing less of Doushi-sama.

Let’s have a thrilling trip right before the wedding──though you usually wouldn’t let a bride head out to pick the flowers for the wedding by herself.

“We have arrived! This is Mt. Sands, roughly located halfway between Baulburg and the Demon Forest! A lot of Sparkle of Newlywed Wife’s are growing…on its summit!”

“Wow, that’s incredible. Then let us hurry and collect those Sparkles of Newlywed Wife’s right away.”

“…”

“Are you okay, Dominique-nee-san?”
