“Am I? Flying across the untouched Baumeister Margraviate at a high speed…feels nice, don’t you think?”

“Lea-san, I think you’re perfectly suited for being Erwin-sama’s wife.”

After a flight time of a few hours, we safely arrived at our destination. It was really fun to cut through the wind while watching the abundant nature below us.

Because Cindy-san continued to fly at full speed in order not to lose sight of Doushi-sama, she looked quite exhausted, and Dominique-nee-san’s face was pale as well. Since the basket, which Doushi-sama used to transport us, didn’t shake much at all, I didn’t feel sick or anything.

“Dominique-nee-san, are you bad with heights?”

“I’d love to know anyone who’s not bad with such a height…ah, there’s one right in front of me, huh…?”

Was it that frightening? Watching a flock of deer dash across grasslands that looked like the sea because of the wind was kind of like being on a sightseeing tour. That’s fun, isn’t it?

“Do you think so as well, Cindy-san?”

“That was the least of my problems…”

Doushi-sama appears to be able to fly as fast as only a few of the best magicians can. Cindy-san apparently was only barely able to keep up with him. Moreover, Doushi-sama flew while carrying us as luggage.

“I wonder why I had to come here as well, but it’s true that plenty of flowers that look like Sparkle of Newlywed Wife’s are growing here.”

“They’re truly dominating the summit. Their beauty doesn’t betray the rumors about them either.”

This mountain wasn’t all that high, and as it seemed that no monsters or wild animals were living on the summit, it had apparently become a paradise for Sparkles of Newlywed Wife’s.

Surveying the summit, golden-shining Sparkles of Newlywed Wife’s were blooming all over the place.

“Lea and I still have more things to prepare for the wedding ceremony. We will gather the Sparkles of Newlywed Wife’s as quickly as possible and return to the mansion afterwards.”

“Ah, but you have to wait until midnight to pluck the flowers which can be used during the ceremony.”

“Why is that so, Cindy-san?”

“The golden glow, the most prominent feature of Sparkles of Newlywed Wife, only occurs during the one day when the flowers bloom. They quickly wither away, which is one reason it’s so hard to obtain them. Even if you take back the blooming flowers that are currently glowing, they will have withered away by the time of the ceremony, losing their pretty glow. It’s necessary to take them back while firmly grasping the flower buds and put them in a vase with water.”

“So it’s a flower with a short blossom, huh? Are you saying there’s no other way to confirm whether a flower is about to bloom unless you wait for the dead of the night?”

“It’s just as you say, Dominique-san. You cut the flowers with the buds that faintly shine at night, take them back, and put them into a vase. If you do that, you’ll be able to enjoy the Sparkle of Newlywed Wife blooming and shining on the appointed day of the ceremony.”

Nothing less of a flower shop clerk.

Usually, she leaves most of the work to their employers, but her knowledge about flowers is outstanding.

“Cindy-san, that basically means…”

“Yes, we have to wait until night, and then we need to check which bud to cut…”

“In short, we’re going to camp up here.”

Flying over with Flight in the depths of night would be dangerous because of the bad visibility. We will set up camp here, wait until night, and go back to the mansion once the sky starts to become bright.

“Camping, huh? That sounds fun.”

“Right! Camping is very enjoyable indeed!”

“Leaving Doushi-sama…aside, but don’t you have any reservations about this, Lea?”

We aren’t adventurers, so we don’t get many opportunities to camp outside. Isn’t it wonderful that I can take a short camping trip before my marriage?

Besides, Erwin-sama will camp out every now and then as an adventurer, so it’ll be very helpful for me as his wife to understand my husband’s work.

Didn’t Elise-sama previously talk about how fun camping is? As her childhood-friend, Dominique-nee-san must enjoy it as well.

“When it comes to a mountain summit, the nights are cold.”

“Everyone, I grilled some meat!”

When we stepped out of the women’s tent, Doushi-sama had built a hearth out of ricks, lit it on fire, and grilled thinly sliced wild boar meat, which had been marinated in soy sauce, on top of a hot iron plate. He was truly skilled at this. He also grilled veggies alongside the meat, but Doushi-sama ate only meat for the most part.

“Doushi-sama, wouldn’t it be better to also eat the vegetables?”

“”Dominique, your character truly resembles that of Elise!”

Because Doushi-sama is a very self-centered person, he doesn’t really listen to the opinions of others. But this is also a key component of who he is.

“I will grill this here as well!”

“Intestines?”

“I carefully processed the boar intestines and pickled them in especially spicy miso!”

“You made them, Doushi-sama?”

“No, when Margrave Baumeister was running experiments, I had him give me some because it was delicious when we sampled it together.”

Figures…

Doushi-sama likely doesn’t even know how to cook.

“It’s delicious. Just as Elise-sama said, Master sure loves dabbling with stuff like this.”

“I want to eat a delicious meal together with Sensei, so I will research it whenever I have some free time.”

“If you drink liquor after eating those slices which were pickled in salty miso, it will refresh your mouth, allowing you to eat a lot more of them!”

I know that! Master taught me that they’re delicious but not good for your health.

“If you place some of the cheese made by local farms on top of a cold bread and heat it up over a fire, the cheese will melt, making the food very delicious!”

Food tastes great when you camp like this and sit around a fire together with others. It’s a rather sketchy menu…no, I think this sort of menu actually fits the occasion best.

“Let us make a dessert.”

I borrowed a frying pan, which Doushi-sama usually didn’t use, albeit having it in his magic bag, and made flambe.

“Whoa! Flames are flickering across the pan! How exciting!”

“The alcohol in the rum is burning, so you can eat it without worries, Cindy-san.”

“A warm dessert is quite unusual!”

“We eat it at the mansion while garnishing it with Master’s ice cream. The combination of warm fruits and cold ice cream is exquisite.”

Since we don’t have any ice cream with us, it’s just a warm flambe. But, given that we’re on top of a chilly mountain, eating something warm is better for our bodies.

“Ooohh! No wonder you are marrying Erwin! It is truly delicious!”

“I’m a maid, after all. This much is no problem for me.”

“Your skills have improved quite a bit. With this, I won’t need to worry even when you get married.”

“Eeh!? For you to praise me is totally unexpected, Dominique-nee-san! Is it going to snow in hell?”

Maybe this world is coming to an end?

“Humph!”

“Ouch, that hurts…”

Dominique-nee-san, please don’t injure my frail body right before my marriage.

“It would have been no problem if you simply accepted the praise as is, Lea.”

“Now then, it is about time!”

As we chatted cheerfully over our dessert, it was time to grab the flowers. We headed over to a patch with plenty of Sparkles of Newlywed Wife’s, discovering several flowers that were already glowing.

Because they seem to have bloomed while glowing for most of the day, they’ll probably wither away very soon. As I considered that, I could also feel their transiency.

“Oh, there are several faintly glowing buds.”

We just need to collect those, right?

We went ahead and plucked them.

“Those will bloom on the day of the wedding!”

“Because some flowers will also bloom too early or too late, gather a somewhat bigger number of them.”

At times like this, Cindy-san really acts like a flower shop clerk.

---

“I’m done.”

“I’m also done with it, so let’s go to sleep in preparation for tomorrow’s departure.”

“Dominique-nee-san, you really don’t have a shred of sense for aesthetics, don’t you…?”

“What is it all of a sudden?”

“Please look at the night sky.”

We’re on a high mountain and on top of that in an area with no illumination. If you look up to the sky, you can see a plethora of stars twinkling like little gems.

“This is…pretty.”

“The flowers are beautiful as well, but so are the stars.”

Not only I, but also Dominique-nee-san and Cindy-san continued to stare at the starry sky for a while. It was so pretty that it moved me deeply.

“This is a great memory before your wedding!”

“That’s true, Doushi-sama.”

I was somewhat skeptical when he suddenly brought us here in order to collect Sparkles of Newlywed Wife’s, but I got to camp, eat outdoor food, and watch the beautiful Sparkles of Newlywed Wife’s as well as stars. It has become a truly lovely memory.

“Once things calm down after the wedding, you can go on a trip with Erwin next!”

“That’s a nice idea.”

“It is good that we managed to secure Sparkles of Newlywed Wife’s to adorn your wedding ceremony! I will sleep now!”

He can be somewhat forceful, but Doushi-sama is kind to women. I heard from Erwin-sama and Master that Doushi-sama is unexpectedly popular, but I can understand it after today’s events. I mean, he showed me such a pretty starry sky.

One day, I’m going to come here and watch the starry sky with Erwin-sama, Haruka-sama, and Anna-san.

---

“Well, how to put it…Doushi really always decides things on the spot.”

“He went to get decorative flowers for Lea’s and my wedding ceremony, and even someone as serious as Dominique had fun, not to mention Cindy, so isn’t it just fine?”

“Still…”

“Still what, Wend?”

“I’m jealous that they got to eat my new wild boar miso pickles prototype as camping food.”

“…Sometimes I really don’t get you, man.”

After safely collecting Sparkle of Newlywed Wife’s, we took a light breakfast after waking up early in the morning, and went back to the mansion. Master and Erwin-sama already awaited us when we arrived, but it doesn’t look like they worried all that much.

Then again, I hear Doushi-sama contacted them through the MHCD or something like that.

“Dear Uncle, please be aware of planning things more carefully.”

“I will do so next time!”

Elise-sama scolded Doushi-sama a bit while making mate tea for us. Elise-sama is the conscience of the Baumeister House after all. And as might be expected, even Doushi-sama won’t do anything that would make Elise-sama furious for real.

“Camping in the wild, huh…? How nice…”

Master looked very jealous after hearing about our little trip. But, if it’s camping, he’s doing it a lot when heading out as an adventurer, isn’t he? Or is there some sort of difference?

“There is a definite difference between camping when working as an adventurer and setting up a tent, lighting a fire to make your own food, and spending the night while gazing at the night sky.”

“You think so?”

Sure, the camping was fun, but is it that different from camping that Master and his friends usually do? In our case, you can also see it as us having fun, since we camp so rarely.

“Besides, I heard that you often camped out alone in the Savage Lands until you enrolled at the adventurer prep school in Breitburg, Wend. How is that any different?”

“It is! That was just a part of my training! I just wanted to be alone somewhere during my free time.”

“You wanted to be alone that much? Well, it’s not that I can’t understand the feeling, but…”

“Sometimes I want to spend the night by myself while watching a campfire. And even though our craftsmen finally brought a new prototype tent, only Doushi was able to use it so far!”

“Doushi has a lot of free time on his hands…or rather, if Doushi were busy, it’d mean that the Kingdom is in a dangerous situation. That’s why it’s fine like that.”

“Doushi-sama is the Helmut Kingdom’s ultimate weapon. It’s better for things to be peaceful without him getting a turn.

“Anyway, after listening to the story, I started to feel an urge to camp as well. I’ll take a day off today.”

Ehhh!? All of sudden talking about taking a day off…there’s no way that person is going to accept that…

The instant I thought so, a person entered the room. It was none other than Roderich-sama, the house manager.

“I’m sorry to say, Milord, but you won’t have any days off until the wedding ceremony between Erwin and Lea. Today’s schedule is also tightly packed. Come now. Let us work hard and cheerfully to develop the territory today as well!”

“Roderich, you can understand it as well, can’t you? If I can take a sudden, quick holiday, it will allow me to energetically work, starting with tomorrow, as the break will serve as an opportunity to refresh myself and vent some stress.”

“Who knows? Personally, I never experienced a sudden holiday. Oohh! It’s time! Master, first up is the creation of new reclaimed land in the outskirts of Baulburg.”

“Wait! I want to have a day oooooff!”

Even though he resisted to the bitter end, Master was dragged away by Roderich-sama. Master should be the most important dignitary of this territory, yet he seems like the most difficult for some reason…is not my imagination.

“Erwin-sama, is it normal for a man to suddenly feel like being alone?”

“…I think it can happen…”

I see. Then, once I become Erwin-sama’s wife, I must pay close attention to that part as well.

Given that we have obtained the Sparkle of Newlywed Wife’s, I’ll continue preparing the wedding ceremony for today.

---

“Father, Mother, thank you very much for raising me. I, Lea, will be marrying Erwin-sama.”

“”…””

“Dominique-nee-san, thank you kindly for all the help and care you have granted me since my days as a child and for training me as a maid. I, Lea, shall become a good wife for Erwin-sama.”

“…”

“Umm…isn’t there something missing here? Like, 『I’m so sad that my cute daughter is getting married』, or 『I’m going to miss you, whom I’ve dotted like a little sister!』? I mean, this is the perfect scene for some tears to flow.”

Even though their adorable daughter is getting married, my parents are acting like it’s no big deal. Even though we’re seeing each other for the first time in a long time after they came from the Stadtburg, where they usually live, to Balburg for the marriage.

The same also applies to Dominique-nee-san. Her cherished protegee is finally getting married, so it should be a moving scene that remains in our memories for the rest of our lives…

“No, didn’t we meet with you just last week, Lea?”

“You’re often coming to the capital as Margrave Baumeister-sama’s attendant, aren’t you?”

“T-That’s…”

Master often designates me as his attendant when heading to the capital. So yes, it hasn’t been that long since I last saw my parents. But last week was just a normal meeting!

“Lea, it’s true that you’re marrying soon, but that doesn’t mean your life will change drastically. It’s not like you’re leaving this world either…”

“Certainly…”

Just like with Anna, I’ll have a few days off after the marriage ceremony, but it’s not like I’m going to stop being a maid. Anna-san married Erwin-sama as well, but she hasn’t stopped being his maid or anything like that.

After all, there are only a few maids who can directly take care of Master and his wives inside the mansion.

“Therefore, I believe it’s worthy of congratulating you for it, but…a moving scene?”

“Uuhh…”

Dominique-nee-san, please don’t question me with such a serious look on your face.

“Anyway, the wedding ceremony is going to start soon, so please change into your wedding dress. Candy-san is waiting.”

“Now that you mention it!”

Candy-san accepted the task of putting the wedding dress on me. He came all the way here from the capital for me, his friend.

“I’ll hurry!”

---

After getting Candy-san to help me with putting on the wedding dress, I moved to the church, and the wedding ceremony finally began. Erwin-sama and I exchanged the vow in front of the priest and all invitees. Then Erwin-sama put the ring on my ring finger. And lastly, we had the kiss of oath.

Then, at last, came the time to toss the bouquet.

“I often hear that the person who catches the bouquet will be able to marry next, but has anyone checked whether that’s actually true?”

“…Leaving aside whether it’s next or not, most will marry at some point.”

Erwin-sama, today the unmarried, young women related to Baumeister House are aiming for the bouquet…or are they?

“Lea-chaaaaan! Erwin-chaaaaan! Over heeeeere!”

“Candy-san, huh…? Is that actually okay?”

“Umm…I guess…”

If it’s Candy-san with his physical abilities, I’m sure he’ll be able to snatch the bouquet without hurting any of the young women in the audience.

“I never heard anything about that kind of bouquet toss!”

“But, it’s not like we can’t throw it either. Eyyy!”

Leave it to chance, I tossed the special bouquet with all my strength towards the unmarried women.

Thereupon…

“Hooo───! Got it───!”

“””””””””…”””””””””

Even though he was the furthest back behind all the unmarried women, Candy-san grabbed the airborne bouquet silently and nimbly like a cat, before performing a magnificent landing. All the attendees could only watch him, who squealed with a bassy voice out of pure joy, in silence.

“Yahoooo───!”

“It’s wonderful that Candy-san is so happy about it!”

![](file:////tmp/wps-alejandro/ksohtml/wpsGX3oFi.png) 

“Yes…I suppose…”

Afterwards followed a party only for the closest friends and family, and the Sparkle of Newlywed Wife’s, which was so much work to get, was very beautiful. They decorated the banquet venue everywhere, and everyone talked excitedly about it.

“If we get an order for Sparkle of Newlywed Wife’s next time, I can go and get them, but it’s a lot of work…no, this is also magic training!”

Cindy-san seemed very cheerful. But, the Sparkle of Newlywed Wife’s blooming on Mt. Sands is the prettiest when you see them for the first time over there, I think.

“Erw, how are you going to spend your holidays with Lea?”

“Let’s see…I think we’ll go to the capital,” answered Erwin-sama to Master.

“Stadtburg!? I’m so looking forward to it!”

I’ve grown up in the capital after all. So I’ll be able to guide Erwin-sama around.

If he likes, we can also stay at my family’s home…no, we’re newlyweds, so that’s out. In a luxurious hotel…

“Even though you were so deeply moved about camping out on Mt. Sands last week?”

“Dominique-nee-san, something like that is fine every once in a while. No matter how touching the scenery might be, if you constantly look at it, it’ll eventually lose its glory.”

“As always, you’re quite the smooth talker, Lea.”

“The capital it is then. That place is huge, so there are still a lot of places I don’t know, even after living there for three years.”

“Erwin-sama, I will guide you around.”

The next day, we left on our honeymoon, allowing us to spend uninterrupted quality time as a married couple. And then I returned to being a maid.

---

“I’m a married woman despite being a maid!”

“That’s the same for Anna-san and me as well. Having said that, given that we also have to take care of our family’s household, Master was so kind as to say that it would be fine to hire new maids and train them while lowering our workload.”

Now that I’ve become a wife, I also have to take care of my household. At the same time, it’s quite possible that the mansion will be rather short-handed when Anna-san and I go on maternity leave. I guess that means we have to prepare for that.

“Dominique-nee-san, please leave it to me! I’m going to strictly drill everything into the newcomers they need to know!”

“Hmph!”

“Ouuch…I’m a wife and yet…”

“Isn’t that true for all three of us? Because the newcomers will be chosen to take care of things around Master, they’ll have to be people with extremely outstanding abilities. If you’re not careful, they could pass you by in no time, Lea.”

“Somehow this has turned into quite the amazing story all of a sudden!”

“Nowadays, the Margrave Baumeister House is a high-ranking nobility of established reputation. Accordingly, there are many maids who want to work here.”

“I see.”

She’s right. I cannot be negligent with this. I must focus myself a lot more and master the way of a maid!

“I will introduce the newcomers to you first. Lea, Anna-san, please teach them everything they need to know.”

“Understood.”

“You can count on me!”

At first, I started out as a maid thanks to Dominique-nee-san’s introduction, but this path is very deep. I’ve become Erwin-sama’s wife, but as his wife, future mother of his children, and maid of the Baumeister House, I must do my best.

I’ll continue to be a maid. Forever.

“I wonder if any of the newcomers are going to manage to become Master’s wives.”

“Hmph!”

“Ouuch…”

“You don’t need to think about such unnecessary things. Now, let’s go.”

## **Hachinan tte, sore wa nai deshou! – Volume 23 – Prologue – In the Far Northern Reaches**

“Is this everyone you managed to gather, Keitzel? I see that all of the regulars are present, but what about the supporters who endorsed our ideal?”

“It seems like those people were just talking. Even though we went out of our way to invite them to our great project 『World Conquest Alliance』…”

“No helping it. History books tell us that the demon kings and nobles, who achieved great feats in ancient times, also had few followers at the beginning. But many of them, who possessed outstanding foresight, left their names in history. Geniuses who achieve great things are rarely understood by ordinary people at first. In other words, the ten comrades gathered here are all excellent men who can predict the future. Of course, the same applies to you as well, Keitzel. Be proud of your foresight.”

“You’re absolutely right. I’m sure our aspiration will come to fruition.”

I, Otto Heinz, the leader of the 『World Conquest Alliance』, have been sparing no effort to bring back the great and powerful demons of old since our contact with the humans. In addition to doing lobby work with politicians from the ruling and opposition parties, I held guerrilla speeches in various places to gather like-minded souls for our cause.

Being told that it was forbidden to hold rallies without permission, I was arrested by the police several times. At those times, the young police officers would treat me like an idiot, but in the end, it was just the rambling of corrupt government dogs. It didn’t leave any impression on me.

Fortunately, the number of supporters of the 『World Conquest Alliance』 exceeded a hundred as our ideology continued to gradually spread among the younger demons. The idea of obtaining power, influence, and whatever you want by making use of our large mana pools to freely use magic, as the kings of old did.

The 『Magic Training Courses』 endorsed by me were extremely popular, and a few dozen young, jobless demons started to practice their magic in the countryside, outside of public attention. Their demon instincts should awaken very soon.

As might be expected, even I didn’t wish for a conflict between fellow demons. The target of our regained magic prowess would be the humans.

In contrast to the demons, who were worried about their declining birthrate, the humans were increasing in number like rabbits. Soon they’ll run out of living space. And it’s obvious that they’ll target our subcontinent next, then.

Accordingly, we’re going to conquer the world and place humans under our control.

However, no matter how many times I explained this to the government and the wealthy, they didn’t approve of our idea, citing moral reasons and a lack of personnel and funds. Given that there are also reasonable people among humans, they claimed they could gain more from them through trade. None of them could see the danger waiting for us demons in the future.

Even if they were to make good money now and even if we’re lacking soldiers, it’s crucial to decide and act swiftly, yet…

This is why these foolish politicians, who are yapping about peace at any price and can’t think ahead, are so damn useless!

Hence, I decided to take action myself. I resolutely made up my mind to leave this country. Staying in the demon country would only corrupt our minds. Which reminds me: there was someone who illegally fled to the demon country for his own research. Moreover, he wasn’t punished for it either.

We spent the last month rigorously training our magic out in the wilderness, and today was the celebratory day when we would officially leave for the outside world, but… according to Keitzel’s report, not a single one of our supporters was going to join us.

“When we previously called for their participation, many of them said that they’d join in, and yet…”

“What about the donations?”

“It’s a lot less than expected, too.”

This has turned into a really saddening outcome. Keitzel and my other comrades appear to be deeply worried, but I won’t get depressed over a setback of this level.

“All of you, it certainly might be worrying to have such a small number. But, look, it’s not just about gathering many people when accomplishing a great feat. Even if you get many people to get together, they’ll just stand in each other’s way, and fights over the leadership will break out among them, turning them into what’s often called a disorderly mob. In the past, many people failed at achieving greatness for this very reason.”

“You’re right. Such demon kings existed in the past.”

“Correct, Keitzel. Just having big numbers isn’t enough. I see no reason to be depressed about this situation. After all, you, me, and the others here are the true elites who possess the necessary motivation, decisiveness, and ability!”

“”””””””Yeeeaaaaa!!!””””””””

“We ten have a lot of mana too! Magicians with a lot of mana are regarded highly in the outside world, or in other words, the human lands. I hear you can obtain status and riches by being such a magician. In other words, we can achieve a lot in the outside world, even with a small group.”

“True. As long as there are ten of us, we do not need to fear hundreds or thousands of humans.”

“It’s just as you say, Keitzel.”

“So, Comrade Otto, what are we going to do after leaving this country and entering the Lingaia Continent?”

“We can, for example, invade some place and create a new demon nation. We will sell our magic power to the human leaders, and if they hire us, we will turn them into our puppets while ruling over the human land ourselves.”

“”””””””Yeeaaaaah!””””””””

“But, it’s still too early for that. First, we have to obtain another big power.”

“Comrade Otto, what power are you speaking of?”

Keitzel asked me, representing the others.

“Actually, I bought something like this at an antiquarian bookshop.”

It was something I had discovered by coincidence. It was a very old document written on parchment, but it was an investigation report of the Ancient Magic Civilization, which perished on Lingaia more than 10,000 years ago.”

The demons of the past dispatched research teams when the Ancient Magic Civilization perished overnight. Documents from that time still remain.

“Comrade Otto, you did well to have found something so valuable.”

“It was sold to the bookshop after having its price beaten down. Recently, there’s a tendency among demons to deem such things acceptable as long as they can earn some money with it. With the values and culture of the ancient demons having become obsolete, precious documents like this one are being pawned off for cheap at the bookshops of this city.”

Even this deplorable tendency should be addressed once we achieve our big goal.

“So, what was written in that document?”

“According to this, they not only investigated the Lingaia Continent, but also the ice continent in the north.”

“Are humans living on that ice continent as well?”

“As can be predicted, only a few people have settled down there. There are no civilians over there. Because the country followed some sort of intention with it, the army apparently established a base on the ice continent. But when the Ancient Magic Civilization perished, the things necessary to survive in that icy land stopped being transported there. They didn’t suffer any direct damage from the large explosion that brought down the Ancient Magic Civilization, but they apparently returned to Lingaia. Ever since then, the ice continent has remained uninhabited, according to the document.”

“Comrade Otto, are we possibly heading over to that uninhabited ice continent? And if yes, for what reason?”

“The number of humans who settled over there with the intention of living there was zero. But it has the advantage of being outside of public attention. Accordingly, what if a state or army has been secretly developing and producing weapons over there? This was one of the worries mentioned in the document. 『Under the eternal layers of ice in the far north…』. Unfortunately, I cannot read the letters beyond that because they have become too faded, but it’s very likely that we’ll find the source of our new power over there. Since it’s an area where an intense winter is reigning, I think it’s going to be a challenge, but I’m sure we’ll be able to recover that source of power. I plan to head over there. How about, my fellow comrades?”

“I agree with this plan.”

I expected that Keitzel would support this.

“I will join as well!”

“Me too!”

“Me as well!”

Everyone agreed to participate in my suggestion.

“Very well. All that’s left is to put it into practice! This rotten Republic of Zontark has no future left! We will revive as powerful demons and rule over this world!”

“”””””””Yeeaaaaah!””””””””

“No matter how small our numbers might be, we ten should be able to achieve everything we put our mind to. Our first destination will be the far northern lands. We will definitely secure the source of our power, the legacy of the Ancient Magic Civilization, in that place!

---

“The Empire is finally in the process of getting a hold of all the chaos caused by the civil war. The restoration is proceeding smoothly, and you can already see us growing even further. The possibilities of the land in the north…the government has been considering how to use that land economically, besides migration, since before the civil war. Sadl,y it seems like it’s a place that’s very unwelcoming for humans.”

“Count Burdon, it’s a challenge to even farm land that’s covered by thick layers of ice all year long. Maybe you can fish some and find promising mineral resources. The real target of the territorial expansion should be the eastern continent.”

“But, Viscount Heart, the Helmut Kingdom should be headed for the eastern continent. We must make haste or the Empire will be put in a tough situation.”

“The eastern continent is further away from Lingaia than the western demon continent. Besides, Helmut Kingdom’s real aim is likely the southern continent. That Earl Baumeister…no, he has become a margrave, hasn’t he? I hear he used his own soldiers to annex many southern islands. The aim of the Helmut Kingdom is probably to have the Margrave Baumeister House provide colonization support for the southern continent.”

“Well, our Empire can’t make a move towards the southern continent, after all.”

“Still, Margrave Baumeister, huh…? Going by the rumors, he has taken girls from those southern islands as his wives…”

“I hear the retiree of the Duke Philip House is basically being treated as his wife as well. He seems to have played an active role during the civil war as well, but right now he’s probably in the center of attention among the nobles.”

“They say the retiree of the Duke Philip Hose gave birth to his daughter. The high-ranking nobles in the imperial capital are fighting behind closed doors about how they can somehow build a connection to him through marriage. As far as His Majesty is concerned, he probably would prefer them to stop with this.”

“Even though the civil war ended just recently, the courtiers at the imperial court are acting just as usual.”

“We hate that place, and that’s why we applied to research this wintry land.”

“You’ve got a point. It’s far more significant to explore the icy region.”

We were ordered to explore the northern continent by His Majesty. I, Earl Burdon, and Viscount Heart succeeded in building a base camp near the beach located at the southern tip of the northern continent. Having said that, most of this continent is locked up by ice, so it’s impossible to do agriculture over here.

As such, we have to rely on the regular delivery of grain and vegetables through magic airships.

The lucky part is the abundant fishing grounds and the animals that live in these northern lands. They were evaluated as animals because they don’t possess magic stones inside their bodies, but we might find them in the monster domain once we send out an exploration team from the base camp.

“Earl Burdon, we will likely face many difficulties in the northern exploration. As such, we must be thoroughly prepared. We also have to report back to His Majesty.”

“True. But it sure is a pain that we cannot use magic airships for the explorations.”

This freezingly cold continent is swept by a terrifying blizzard every few hours. It’s no problem during good weather, but if a magic airship is caught by a blizzard mid-flight, it will definitely crash. We can only use the usual magic airships around the most southern coast, where we also built our base camp.

“I guess we should be thankful for not having to worry about running out of supplies.”

“In the future, we can try to maintain this base camp as a fishing port, and if there are rich mines further inside the continent, it’d be fine as well, but…”

“We’ll have to wait for the results of the investigation. With the airships out of the race, the only method for the exploration group to move will be dog sleds, I suppose.”

“It’s a big help that we got Duke Philip to sell us many wolf hounds.”

“Wolf hounds are resistant to cold, and although they have large builds, they also possess stamina. They could be put to use during the civil war, but the Duke Philip House’s Dog-Sled Corps is famous.”

“Since we also got him to lend us sled drivers, we’ll send out several exploration teams once everything is ready, and create a map first and foremost.”

The creation of a map is essential for the Empire to prove its claim on this northern continent. You can rightfully call it our most important task over here. Viscount Heart’s and my families have been involved in land surveying and map creation for the imperial army for generations, but that work comes with a lot of danger. Sometimes you have to enter monster domains, and many dangerous species also exist among the animals in unexplored areas.

Above all, even if we’re all nobles belonging to the Empire, no noble would be happy about someone arbitrarily making maps of their territory. Because of that, landed nobles would occasionally plot assassinations by criminals who hid in uninhabited areas, attacks by monsters and ferocious animals, and accidents to get rid of us.

The Empire has concluded a ceasefire with the Helmut Kingdom more than 200 years ago, but both sides have been secretly sending in people to create maps of the other side of the Gigantic Rift. The objective is to be prepared for a potential future war.

Drawing maps and such is apparently considered intelligence work, but the people actually doing the work are people like us, known as hawks even among the imperial army.

Given that we don’t directly appear on battlefields, society doesn’t see us as such, but drawing up maps comes with many dangers, and many of our ancestors died in the line of duty. Creating maps is not that challenging, but at the same time, it’s crucial for a nation.

Because it’s a special skill, we kept a completely neutral stance during the civil war. Even Duke Nürnberg didn’t go so far as to meddle with us. Since our map-making skills would be necessary, regardless of who wins in the civil war, I guess you can only call that natural, though.

“Our current mission is to draw up a map of this ice-covered land as quickly as possible.”

“I guess we should hurry with the preparations.”

“Yes, so it seems.”

Moreover, we must ensure we regularly send reports to His Majesty. After all, he’s our most prominent sponsor.

I hear the courtiers in the capital have been noisily chirping around, but even if they denounce us as incompetent in the imperial palace, it’s unthinkable for them to come to this freezing cold place and carry out the explorations themselves. It sounds like the kingdom has such nobles as well, but they hadn’t found a method other than ignoring such people, either.

“Not having to deal with those people is already a big boon from coming to this northern region. The rumored Margrave Baumeister seems to have it even more difficult than we.”

Be it a royal or imperial palace, the only purpose in the lives of courtiers seems to be criticizing others.

“No kidding. I’m sure the land survey folks in the Helmut Kingdom must be thinking the same.”

“Which reminds me, I heard rumors that the kingdom dispatched its special friendship delegation.”

“The one, which was carried out every five years, got dragged into the civil war and didn’t serve much purpose. Since the trade volume between both countries is going to increase, they’re apparently going to increase the mutual visits.”

“I didn’t know that.”

Viscount Heart has sharp ears, considering that we’re so far up in the north.

“There’s also the diplomatic negotiations with the demon country. This is unofficial information, but His Majesty seems to have visited the kingdom in secret a little while ago. In return, the kingdom is going to send over His Highness Crown Prince Wald as leader of the friendship delegation.”

“It’d be great if both countries could forge a food relationship.”

Us making maps is in preparation for a war, but there would be nothing better if those maps were never used.

“The crown prince of the Helmut Kingdom is coming to our Empire, huh…? The courtiers must be kicking up a fuss like a bee nest that has been poked with a stick.”

“It’s going to end with them just making a racket anyway. Let us speed up the preparations to send out the exploration teams while providing accurate reports to His Majesty.”

“That sounds like a good idea.”

Still, a temporary friendship delegation, huh? I wonder which nobles will be accompanying the crown prince. Margrave Baumeister? There’s also the matter with the daughter born between him and the retiree of the Duke Philip House, so I guess they won’t deliberately visit the imperial capital in this phase.

---

“Wald, are the preparations of the friendship delegation progressing smoothly?”

“Yes, everything is going as planned.”

“I see. In that case, it’s fine, but at present, I cannot allow any of our ministers to participate. The fruits of this sort of event only manifest over a long period of time. If you, the next king, let many young nobles, who will likely steer this country in the future with you, participate in this, they will be able to build personal connections with His Majesty Peter and his retainer,s which will in turn make future negotiations easier. If possible, I’d like one major noble to participate, but I don’t have the luxury to ask for that under the current circumstances.”

“Father, let us have Margrave Baumeister participate in that case.”

“Margrave Baumeister, eh…? That man is quite busy himself. Will it be okay?”

“That is the very reason for his participation in the friendship delegation. We must have him work for the sake of the Kingdom for a long time to come. If he joins the delegation, he’ll also be able to get a bit of a break.”

“Oh, I see. There won’t be much practical work during the friendship visit. Its ultimate objective is to show the friendship between the two countries to the Empire’s nobles and people. Besides, I hear Margrave Baumeister is on close terms with His Majesty Peter as a former comrade-in-arms. Moreover, he’s a major noble, so I think it might be a good idea to have him participate.”

“Then let us go ahead with that.”

In reality, it has been planned for me, the crown prince of Helmut Kingdom, to go to the Holy Empire of Urquhart as leader of the friendship delegation. The previous friendship delegation didn’t yield much result due to the sudden death of the late emperor and the civil war, so this visit will serve as a substitute for it.

Furthermore, the matters that the Empire and Kingdom must discuss have increased. A visit every five years won’t be enough to address this, so it’s necessary to provide more opportunities for officials from both countries to meet.

The upcoming friendship visit is a first test run for this.

After telling my father about the delegation’s lineup and the progress of the departure preparations, I received the advice that it’d be best to have another important person join, besides the crown prince. But it goes without saying that all the ministers are currently busy with the demon country negotiations.

In addition, the friendship delegation is an event planned to allow promising young nobles of the Kingdom to meet with His Majesty Peter and young imperial nobles. It’d bear little meaning to have an older noble participate, even if they might be important.

Having said that, if the friendship delegation doesn’t have a single major noble with it, it might be regarded as unimportant. Accordingly, I suggested that Margrave Baumeister join. He’s young, and he’s good friends with His Majesty Peter and his friends. And above all that…

“(It’s going to be a trip to another country with Wendelin! How wonderful! That is truly what friends do!)”

After returning to my room, I savored the joy of having accomplished my plan atop my bed. Given that my wife and child would probably hear me if I celebrated loudly, I continued to rejoice inside my mind.

“(I’m going on a trip with a friend! Moreover, to a foreign country! As if I wouldn’t look forward to that!)”

With this, no one should doubt that Wendelin and I are best friends anymore. I was deeply relieved that my father had approved Wendelin’s participation in the friendship delegation.

“(There are also events like meeting with His Majesty Peter and young imperial nobles, but they’ve included quite a bit of freetime in the schedule. In other words…)”

We’ll be able to travel incognito during our free time to sightsee in the imperial capital and enjoy commoner desserts and meals as well. As might be expected, my exclusive cooks won’t be allowed to come along this time. As such, I’ll be able to fully enjoy the local specialties of the Empire instead of “food that is suitable for a future king.”

‘(Where should we go? Oh, right! I have to get a sightseeing guide for the imperial capital as soon as possible!)”

Controlling my nagging advisors and attendants should go well at the destination. Exploiting that opening, I’m going to have fun in the capital with Wendelin.

“(This sure is going to be lots of fun. Also…)”

Let’s finish up all the accumulated work until the friendship delegation departs. If someone brings up work-related matters during this precious trip, it’d completely spoil it.

“(I must make sure that Wendelin cannot say he hasn’t heard anything about this)”

I’m going to send out the participation order for Wendelin as soon as possible.

“(Wendelin must be busy as well. As long as I tell him early on and get him to finish his work ahead of time…)”

…he will be able to enjoy the sightseeing with his best friend without any distress.

“(I’m so hyped about this)”

I’m already totally excited. Let’s get fired up and quickly wrap up all the work so that it turns into a fun trip to the Empire.

---

“Eh? Again? Roderich, the Friendship Visit Delegation is already a thing of the past, no? Last time it turned into a disaster as we got dragged into the civil war, you remember?”

“It’s not a Friendship Visit Delegation, but a Friendship Deepening Delegation. I’m told that the opportunities for mutual visits between the two countries will increase from now on. First, His Highness Wald will visit the empire, taking many young nobles as a delegation to assess the situation. If there are no particular problems, the chances for ministers and high-ranking nobles to visit the Empire will increase a lot more.”

“And they’re telling me to participate in that Friendship Deepening Delegation? Moreover, is it His Highness Wald’s order?”

“Yes. According to the decree we received from the palace a bit earlier, that seems to be the case.”

“Young nobles…includes me?”

When I returned in the evening after finishing my public works, Roderich brought in a decree from His Highness Wald. According to it, I was to join the friendship deepening delegation, which would be dispatched to the Empire with him as its leader.

“Given that it’s the first group, they seem to prioritize young nobles who might be placed in important positions in the future. Since His Highness Wald, and not His Majesty, serves as the delegation leader, it’s probably been decided like that with the future of the Kingdom in mind.”

“And that’s where I come in, huh…?”

“Do you hate the idea? Personally, I believed that you would be rejoicing, claiming that it would be a great opportunity to have some fun in another country, Milord…”

“Do you take me for a little kid!?”

I couldn’t help but retort.

“Normally, I would be happy about the participation in the Friendship Deepening Delegation. But, you see…”

“Is something the matter?

“Friedrich and the other babies are becoming bigger with every passing day! Not being able to observe them would be terrible!”

I really wonder… just how cold are the people of this world to those who have just become parents? Leaving aside my daily work, which Roderich has scheduled so I can finish by evening, if I head out to a job where I’ll be staying over, I won’t be able to see my babies every day, will I!?

“In reality I’d like to take a maternity leave, but while holding back on that I’ve been using my magic every day for the sake of the Baumeister Margraviate, and yet…I’d like to be spared from going to the Empire right now.”

I mean, I can go there whenever I feel like it anyway. Once my babies grow up, it might be nice to go on a sightseeing tour in the Empire with my whole family.

“Umm…men cannot take maternity leave…”

“That’s why I’m enduring so hard, okay!? If I were to speak frankly, I feel like taking maternity leave for at least three years.”

“Even the maids in this mansion don’t take maternity leave for three years. The limit is one year at most.”

He’s got a point, I guess. Even on Earth there exist mixed views about men taking maternity leave, so it’s only natural that it’s even more complicated in this world.

“In the first place, even if you were to take maternity leave, you are absolutely useless when it comes to raising the children, Milord.”

“…You really don’t hold back at all, do you…?”

He’s right. I have basically no experience in how to raise children, but…so far as it goes, I am the lord of this land.

“Rather than having you raise the children yourself, it will make everyone much happier if you were to develop your territory with your special magic. There is a common saying called ‘the right person in the right place’.”

“…”

I couldn’t return anything because Roderich’s argumentation was just too sound.

“If you are worried about the burden on Elise-sama and your other wives, you do not need to. We have maids for this very reason!”

“…”

Now that he mentions it, it does sound reasonable. Otherwise, it’d be too much with that many babies. My wives would collapse from all the baby-care work.

Probably because I grew up in a family of office workers to begin with, I couldn’t understand the idea of leaving the care of your babies to babysitters…or maids.

“With that said, it would be great if you could join the Friendship Deepening Delegation for the sake of the future and growth of Friedrich-sama and the other babies, Milord.”

“It sounds like it’s going to take quite some time…that visit…

“No, with your magic, you can return to this mansion whenever you have free time, right, Milord?”

“You’ve got a point there.”

I don’t know about the other participants, but I have Teleport at my disposal. It allows me to return to my mansion in no time and check on my children, even if I’m working on a construction project far away.

In that case, it’d mean I can play around in the Empire to my heart’s content without having to do any work? Only young nobles will participate in the Friendship Deepening Delegation, so it’s not like it’s going to be a work meeting.

“(Somehow I’m starting to look forward to this. I guess I’ll go and visit Peter and the others for a bit) If His Highness nominated me, I cannot change it. This too is a noble’s duty.”

Even if it’s a Friendship Deepening Delegation that’s half play, it’s impossible for me to turn down a decree from the crown prince.

“I see. Will you accept it then? That is wonderful to hear. Then allow me to change your schedule, starting with tomorrow.”

“Huh? Change my schedule?”

“Yes. If you are going to participate in the Friendship Deepening Delegation, the usual public work operations in the territory will be suspended. As such, I must have you work harder until the day of your departure, Milord.”

“For real?”

Is he going to make me work even more than I already am?

“Come to think of it, you are able to use Light as well, so it should pose no problem for you to work at night as well. Though I shall make sure that you secure enough sleep to recover your mana. You will be able to take a good rest during your trip with the Friendship Deepening Delegation.”

“No way…”

“Please enjoy the Empire to the fullest.”

Just like that, it was decided by Roderich that I’d be working all day long, except for the times when I had to sleep, to develop the Baumeister Margraviate during the time until my departure to the Empire. My entire schedule was crammed with work except for the times when I ate, slept, or took a bath. I wondered whether this couldn’t be considered a violation of the Labor Standards Act or something like that, but unfortunately, such a law didn’t exist in this world.

Ah, I’m a noble to begin with, so I guess you can’t really describe me as a laborer…

It was also impossible to look for a different job at Hello Work. Hence, I ended up toiling away without rest for the sake of my darling babies.

“Which reminds me, you were able to go to the imperial capital with Teleport, weren’t you, Milord? Since you do not need to board the airship of His Highness and the rest of the delegation, you can work for the two days it’s going to take them to get there.”

“…Eh?”

“Milord, there exists nothing as precious as time in this world!”

“…”

Never before did I feel so strongly that Roderich must be an oni.

---

“Delicious sweets, check! Tea, check! I also have games with me. I must make sure not to be negligent in preparing my wonderful time with Wendelin during the two days of travel from Stadtburg to the imperial capital.”

We’re going to travel to the imperial capital in a magic airship, but a book said it’s normal to eat, enjoy some time, talk about random stuff, and play games with your friends during a boat trip.

As crown prince, I never did anything like that up until now, so I’m really looking forward to it.

“I really hope my time with Wendelin arrives soon.”

A two-day trip with my friend. I’m really looking forward to this.

I mean, there’s no way that additional documents would arrive on an airship mid-flight, so this is the best opportunity. As long as I wrap up all paperwork before getting on board, I’ll be able to enjoy my trip with Wendelin uninterrupted.

“We’re going to talk during the flight and deepen our friendship. I’m so looking forward to that.”

I have become the leader of the Friendship Deepening Delegation, but there will be almost no real work waiting for us over in the Empire. I’ll get the Empire leaders to remember my face as the next king. In addition, I think I’ll manage a few friendly get-togethers for the young nobles of both countries.

As for the remaining schedule…

“I’m going to enjoy an Empire sightseeing tour with Wendelin! And I’ll deepen our friendship! Isn’t that wonderful!?”

Since many of the young nobles, who will be participating in the Friendship Deepening Delegation, have already started to board the airship, Wendelin should soon arrive as well. I really would love to have that fun boat ride with the two of us as soon as possible.

Ah, I hope you can show up soon, Wendelin!

+++

# **Chapter 1 – Friendship Deepening Delegation**

“Ah, Your Highness! It looks like we arrived at almost the same time, doesn’t it?”

“So it’d appear… Wendelin, I guess you’re usually quite busy?”

“Yes. It was decided that I wouldn’t need to travel by airship if I could use Teleport on a beck-and-call basis. My House Manager Roderich’s handling of personnel is quite rough.”

“I see…the development of a territory sounds rather challenging.”

“Indeed. Especially since it originally used to be an empty backward region. Roderich has been steadily flooding me with work.”

“I understand…I suppose that makes sense. The Baumeister Margraviate is going to become a crucial base for the future southern expansion of the Kingdom. Thus, we cannot slack on developing the region…(personally, I think that Roderich is working you way too hard!).”

“Huh? Did you say something?”

“No, nothing. …Now then, let’s try heading over to the reception hall.”

After arriving at the imperial capital with Teleport, I quickly headed over to the port. And just as I got there, His Highness Wald was getting off the magic airship. I apologized to him for only joining the delegation at the destination, but it’s good that he didn’t seem overly angry about it.

Frankly stating the truth by saying, 『In reality I wanted to leisurely travel by airship as well, but I was late because I’ve been developing my territory up until right before the Teleport』 and 『All of it is Roderich’s fault』, would be honest, but for people standing above others, like high-ranking nobles, this would be rather questionable. It’d be the plain reality, but putting the blame on your subordinate is what small-minded people do.

Having said that, I cannot help it since I have this character by birth. Besides, it’d be better for the Margrave Baumeister House for Roderich to incur His Highness’s enmity than me…then again, that’d be impossible, wouldn’t it…? I guess Roderich will have to have an opportunity next time when His Highness visits our territory.

After I joined the Friendship Deepening Delegation, we began moving toward the reception hall while being guarded by imperial knights. First, we’re going to have an audience with Peter, the emperor, and then there will be a welcome party with a buffet that will also serve as breakfast…or something like that, right?

Given that I had joined them over here and had only a vague recollection of the schedule, I wasn’t very confident about this.

“How wonderful for you to have come all the way here. I would be more than happy if you could enjoy the welcome banquet we prepared.”

It was only natural, but Peter truly felt like an emperor at times like these. Standing next to him, Emela also seemed like a master magician, and not like Peter’s de facto wife. They’re probably making sure not to show any opening towards the high-ranking nobles who are trying to trip them up wherever they can.

“It is a great pleasure for me to meet you for the first time, Your Majesty.”

“Your Highness Wald, we are close in age and have the duty to shoulder a country. It would be on good terms with you.”

“My thinking. I would like nothing more than either. It would also be of great benefit for the peace and development of both our countries.”

The other day, they met at the beach of my territory in absolute secrecy, but His Highness wouldn’t make the blunder of divulging something like that.

Their interaction really felt appropriate for the official conduct between two young leaders of a nation. I wouldn’t be able to imitate that.

While I was pondering all this, we were led into the reception hall, and the banquet started. The young nobles of the Friendship Deepening Delegation were amiably talking with young imperial nobles while enjoying wine, food, and desserts.

Because His Highness and Peter were the leading actors, they went around together, greeting influential nobles.

Therefore, I’m currently enjoying the food and sweets by myself.

Eh? You’re asking why I’m not going around to greet people myself?

No, I mean…this place is full of people I don’t really know…

I’ve been properly doing it up until now, you say?

Well, at that time, Elise and my other wives were with me.

Anyway, I can’t remember the names of nobles, and Elise isn’t with me, so I don’t really know most of the nobles. Talking with a noble and acting like I know them, while in reality not having a clue, would be extremely rude if it were revealed.

Hence, I reached the conclusion that it’d be safer not to talk to anyone to begin with, so now I’m a wallflower at this banquet.

Given that I was probably chosen for the reason that it might be better if there’s at least one high-ranking noble in our delegation besides His Highness, they probably don’t expect that much interaction from me anyway. Since it’s not about any practical business, it should be fine as long as I’m just present. Just like with the Olympics, participation in itself bears significance.

“Hmm, I see. I’d say this is a marinade made out of the trout that swims upstream in the rivers of the Philip Dukedom. Together with the small floured potatoes as garnish, this meal has a great balance.”

Nothing less of a party sponsored by the Empire’s government. They gathered the best ingredients from land and sea in the Empire and had their first-class chefs prepare them into wonderful dishes. It’s truly bliss for my tongue.

I assumed that someone would talk me up, but unexpected people stayed clear of me. Considering it very closely, I’m better known here for being a magician. The people participating in this welcome party are mostly nobles. There’s almost no magicians present. Of course, it’s not like there are none here at all, but most of them are at the elementary level, so they might feel bad about talking to me.

If Burkhart-san were here…well, he hasn’t been invited since he’s neither young nor nobility.

It’s not like I excel in communicating with others to such an extent either, so developing a deeper friendship with fellow magicians…that doesn’t seem to be likely. Talking up a stranger is quite a challenge, you know?

“Mmh, yeah…this roasted meat is great.”

With me being a wallflower for the rest of this party being set in stone, I went around the tables and enjoyed the various dishes. Occasionally, some of the young imperial nobles looked at me, but I can totally understand them; they want to talk to me because they’re curious, but I suppose they can’t really make up their minds to go for it.

But, guys…you should expect me to make the first step here. After all, I’m as hesitant about this as you are.

“The northern seafood is outstanding. They have turned white-fleshed sashimi into carpaccio, but it’s fresh, doesn’t stink, and is truly exquisite. Ooohhh! They also have a sushi corner!”

This is probably a sign that the Duke Mizuho House’s power has grown.

I mustn’t underestimate these dishes as mere party food. Their deliberate treatment of the nobles of the Kingdom to Mizuho cooking means they want to show off the close relationship between the Empire and the ducal house of Mizuho.

“(Nah, I think I’m reading too much into this) Oh! There’s even soba here!”

Given that I ate plenty of meat and fish dishes, I really appreciate soba as a finisher.

![](file:////tmp/wps-alejandro/ksohtml/wpsdTR4zc.png) 

Since it was served in a small bowl, I gulped it down quickly.

“(I’m tempted to get another serving, but I mustn’t forget to get a dessert at the end)”

However, in contrast to the Baumeister Margraviate, the variation of fruits was somewhat small. They weren’t using chocolate either.

However, then I noticed the Mizuho sweets. Since most of them are identical to Japanese confectionery, they’re easy to eat.

“This steamed bun with its moderately sweet red bean jam filling is delicious. They also have sweet red-bean soup!”

At first, I worried about how to spend my time at a party with almost no one close to me, but once it started, I was able to focus on the food and desserts, and the time unexpectedly flew by.

“Starting with tomorrow, we’re going to sightsee the city, huh? For the first time in a while, I’ll be able to enjoy a vacation by myself───”

It’s not as though the Empire and Kingdom will suddenly become close friends, even if I work hard by myself. The other young nobles, who want to make a career, should work hard instead. I’ll have fun in the Empire.

“Yo, Wendelin. What are you doing here all by yourself?”

“I’m enjoying the delicious food.”

Alfos had been greeting the influential nobles of the Kingdom, just like Peter, but now he chatted me up. The work as Prince-Elector Duke Philip, who assists the emperor, seems to be quite a burden. Well, it was a burden on Therese as well.

“Umm…did you talk with any other imperial noble besides me?”

“No, not at all.”

I mean…wouldn’t anyone be nervous about suddenly talking to a stranger?

“…Well, you see…when the news about your participation in the Friendship Deepening Delegation became known, it caused a bit of an uproar among the imperial nobles…”

“Ah, I see where you’re coming from.”

We participated in the civil war and achieved quite a bit. That is an unmistakable truth, and nobles will acknowledge other nobles with big military achievements. I think it’s only logical for the imperial nobles to cause a ruckus when they hear about my joining the delegation.

But…

“Leaving aside Duke Nürnberg, I killed many magicians and soldiers. There might be some among those nobles who lost their friends or relatives because of me. Don’t you think it’d be quite challenging for the other side to call out to me? And calling out to them from my side as the perpetrator seems questionable at best.”

That is why I’ve become a wallflower. It’s not weird at all for me to silently enjoy the imperial dishes by myself. Rather, I think it’s overflowing with the typical Japanese consideration of others.

“I’d like you to rather thank me! I’ve been quietly enjoying dishes and desserts so that the Friendship Deepening Delegation doesn’t fail!”

Right! I’m currently acting in the most optimal way!

“Well, it feels like an excuse, no matter how you look at it…but, it’s true that some of the nobles here lost their relatives because of you…”

After finishing speaking with Alfons, I turned my attention back to the Mizuho sweets.

But man, I must say…it was a truly delicious party.

“Wendelin, it seems you have enjoyed the party, and that’s what counts most, but couldn’t you have been…a bit more…flexible?”

“Even if you say that, what should I have done…? The dishes and desserts served at the party were great.”

“Oh well, whatever…”

I had fun for a while, but after the banquet ended, I was lightly chided by His Highness.

Come to think of it, even he, who’s known for usually lacking presence, took his close aides with him and greeted many imperial nobles, starting with Peter.

But, as someone who doesn’t have any official position, there would be no point for me to greet the nobles of the Empire for no particular reason…and since some among them might have lost their relatives to me, it’s unlikely that they’ll become my friends either way.

“That’s how I am if my wives aren’t with me.”

“Everyone appeared to be awed by you, given that you could calmly enjoy the served food by yourself while being the center of attention.”

“I don’t get what you mean.”

I simply enjoyed the dishes and desserts to my heart’s content…

“Wendelin, usually the Royal Head Wizards and the candidates for that post would go around to make themselves known at the party held during the Friendship Visits. Especially the candidates. The Royal Head Wizard is well-known among the imperial nobles, so all of them would see this as a great opportunity to build a connection with him.”

I see. So it’d be better to be well-known even in the Empire to become the Royal Head Wizard?

“Did Doushi also make himself known to the imperial nobles during a previous Friendship Visit before becoming the Royal Head Wizard?”

“According to my father, he hasn’t done so in advance. Instead, he participated in a Friendship Visit Delegation after becoming the Royal Head wizard. And just like you, he was totally engrossed with the dishes, wine, and dessert during the parties. That’s probably why the imperial nobles were awed by you doing the same, Wendelin. They thought that Wendelin, the 『Strongest Candidate for becoming the next Royal Head Wizard』, was appraising them while pretending to enjoy the food and deliberately avoiding calling out to any of them.”

“…No, I think there are several misunderstandings at work here…”

They’re probably overthinking this. I became a loner during the party. So, why was I arbitrarily labeled as an amazing person for simply enjoying the dishes and desserts?

“In the end, I guess that means everything worked out just fine. Although we’re here with the intention of building a friendship, the dignity of our nations must also be kept in mind. As I thought, it was a good idea to have you participate, Wendelin.”

“Haaah…”

Look, I really just enjoyed the food during the party… What’s more, starting tomorrow, I’ll be able to have plenty of fun by spending a few days freely exploring the imperial capital, but…

“(Oh well, whatever!)”

If other people selfishly believe I’m doing my job properly, it’s lucky for me. I have to relax as much as possible from tomorrow onwards, so I’m going to quickly return to the lodging house today and go to sleep early.

++++

# **29-sai Dokushin wa Isekai - Chapter 90 – Finally Found It in the Deepest Ruins**

[Now, what was the name of this restricted area?]

[The Prison Tower of Sorrow, I think? It’s dangerous here, you know?]

[There’s definitely something there.]

We whispered to each other as we watched the towering white tower, or rather, building-like structure, from the shadows of a distant rock. The reason we didn’t approach too close was because what appeared to be white-armored security robots were patrolling the area.

Judging from the sun’s position, it was still early afternoon. The white tower was located two days’ travel from the ruins of the evacuation shelter, via the beastman village we’d visited during our salt trade.

It was a tower-like structure constructed of the familiar white structural materials. There were few windows, giving the overall building a sturdy feel. A shining antenna-like object extended from the top of the tower, flashing periodically. It seemed to be an active facility. That was obvious, though, given the mechanical soldiers patrolling the area.

[Hey, do you think we can destroy it?]

[I think I told you before, but there’s no way to defeat those white-bodied soldiers. No matter how much magic or arrows we spray at them, it only serves to slow them down.]

At first glance, they appear to be a human wearing white armor, but their flat head lacks any kind of peephole, and various parts of their body periodically flash. They don’t appear to be carrying any weapons, and judging by their light, brisk steps, they appear to have decent mobility.

[I wonder if I can destroy it with this thing?]

I took out a long-range magic gun from the treasure box and switched it to sniper mode. It has a holographic-like sight, but it doesn’t have a high-magnification sniper scope, so it’s a bit unclear whether I can hit anything accurately from a distance.

[I wonder. It seems to have about the same power as a magic arrow, so it’ll be difficult, right?]

[I agree.]

If shooting doesn’t work, the only thing left to do is try physical attacks. But now…

[Are you really going to investigate here? Wouldn’t it be better to find a safer place to investigate like we did last time?]

[Hmm, but Rheal says that one of the things we’re looking for might be here.]

『Yeah, I can feel the vibrations of the quasi-deity. It’s definitely here.』

[She definitely says it’s here. Well, let’s give it a try. If necessary, we’ll run away, so for now I’ll just charge in alone. Cover me from here.]

With that, I leap out from behind a rock.

[What?! Don’t be so reckless!]

[Rifana, cover him.]

[Yes.]

Rifana’s probably gonna get mad at me later. Oh well, let’s save that for later. I’ll think about the rest after I overcome the obstacle in front of me. As I run, I pull out the Enhanced Sacred Wood Staff from the treasure box.

Perhaps noticing me running towards them, one of the patrolling mechanical soldiers turned toward me and sounded a warning beep. I ignored it, combining wind magic and magic art to close the gap with explosive acceleration.

『Biiiiiip!!』

[At least say something meaningful!]

I thrusted my magically imbued Sacred Wood Staff into the white armor, gouging it out. A thud echoed, like two cars colliding, and the white mechanical soldier was sent flying. Incidentally, the reinforced Sacred Wood Staff I was holding also shattered.

[No way!?]

The mechanical soldier I struck didn’t move anymore, but two more rushed toward me from elsewhere. I pulled a large bush knife from my waist and wrapped it in magic power.

The shoulder part of the mechanical soldier rushing toward me snapped open. Acting on a sudden, unpleasant premonition, I quickly moved and hid behind a nearby rock. As I did so, a familiar gunshot sound echoed, and the rock began to shatter. It seemed I was being shot at with the same intensity as the magic gun I’d obtained the other day.

[That’s scary.]

Muttering, I took out a long-range magic gun from my treasure box, leaned out from behind a rock, and fired back in single-shot mode. I hit a few shots, but they didn’t seem to do much damage. It seemed this gun just wasn’t powerful enough.

This time, I fired back in rapid-fire mode, hitting the robot in succession, but it just leaned back a little and didn’t even stop moving.

Next, I concentrated my magic power and fired a level 2 pure magic bullet, but this didn’t produce much of a difference from the magic gun. In other words…

[It’s not working at all!]

One of them pinned me down with gunshots, while the other calmly closed in on me. Are you trying to kill me in close combat? You idiot, I’m better at close combat!

I waited for the right moment to leap out from behind the rock and swing my bush knife, imbuing it with as much magic power as possible, at the approaching robot soldier.

With a bang, the bush knife shattered into pieces.

[You’re kidding me!?]

That much magic power should be enough to cut through even Orichalcum, but the mechanical soldier’s white armor didn’t suffer a single scratch. As expected, the impact wasn’t enough, and it stomped away, but that’s all there was to it.

The white mechanical soldier swung its arms around in an unnatural position and struck me. The movements themselves were clumsy and easy to dodge, but if it hit me, it looked like it would break a bone or two. I thought about grabbing its swayed arm and throwing it, but the machine firing from behind was firing nonstop, not afraid of accidentally hitting its own ally, leaving me with no opening to land a joint lock or throw.

At this point, anything would do as long as I could hit it. I took out a long-range magic gun from the treasure box and swung it hard, hitting the mechanical soldier in front of me. It felt pretty good. The magic gun didn’t seem broken either, so I continued to strike with it.

It seemed Elmina-san and Rifana had distracted the machine firing from behind, and it no longer fired towards us. Now was my chance to take this one down. After a few hits, the mechanical soldier was crushed in various places and unable to move.

I grabbed its leg, closed the distance, and slammed it into the other mechanical soldier that was firing repeatedly at the rocks where Elmina-san and Rifana were hiding. A deafening impact rang out, and the mechanical soldier broke into pieces.

[I hate it, even though I have to admit. The only strategy that works is the unga-bunga one.]

I muttered to myself, gazing at the long-arm magic gun that had become distorted from repeatedly hitting the white mechanical soldier. If I could hit it hard with the same material as the mechanical soldier’s exterior, I could defeat it. At least I knew that.

Confirming that new troops were appearing with a warning sound, I picked up the remains of the mechanical soldier in both hands.

[Owwwwwwwwww!]

---

[I was really shocked.]

[But, it’s okay since we defeated them.]

Elmina-san, who was trying to rebuke the astonished Rifana, was also smiling wryly.

[I didn’t want to fight like that either.]

I had no choice but to try it as an emergency measure after all my weapons were destroyed, and it just so happened to work. I really didn’t want to hit armor that would shatter my Sacred Staff or Bush Knife with my bare hands.

[What else are you going to do? Your weapons are broken, aren’t they?]

[There are loads of them lying around!]

[So you’re going to fight the same way after all.]

[It’s an astonishingly effective method, so it can’t be helped.]

I went around collecting the remains of the mechanical soldiers scattered around. By the way, what on earth is this white material? It looks more like ceramic than metal. Is it even possible to make such strong ceramic?

『I’ll explain next time, so let’s move on.』

Really? It’s unusual for you to rush me.

『Even I’m not comfortable staying in a powerless state like this.』

You’ve been messing around with people so much, and now you’re on the receiving end of it now. Well, compared to your original power, it’s still pretty much powerless.

[Shall we move?]

[Yes, let’s be careful.]

Rifana nodded silently. The entrance to the Tower Prison of Sorrow was just around the corner.

---

[I wonder what kind of facility this is?]

[I have no idea.]

The interior of the building was teeming with mysterious machines. Occasionally, automatic machine guns firing magic bullets appeared from the walls and ceiling, so I had to be on guard. I destroyed them all by throwing the remains of mechanical soldiers at them.

The shuriken? I tried throwing it, but it just bent over without even scratching anything!

[Well, it doesn’t look like a military facility. What we’re looking for seems to have been used as a large-scale power source, so maybe it’s an energy production facility?]

We guessed it might be some kind of power plant. We found what looked like a staff break room and an office-like room, but didn’t find anything in particular. We couldn’t find a floor plan, so the three of us wandered around the facility.

After climbing up and down stairs for a while, we finally reached what seemed to be the innermost part. It was like a checkpoint.

[At the end of the hallway in front of us is a sturdy-looking door, and on both sides are glass, making this a checkpoint-like room.]

[This place has a rather ominous atmosphere.]

[Let’s leave the hallway in front for now and check the spaces on the left and right first.]

After investigating, it appeared that this was indeed a checkpoint. It seemed there was an important area up ahead. There were magically sensitive switches in the glass-walled spaces on both sides, and pressing them simultaneously would open the front door.

[If we hadn’t been there, you’d be stuck here, wouldn’t you?]

Elmina-san grinned. I was originally planning to explore the ruins alone, after all.

[I’m glad I followed your advice, Elmina-san.]

[And me?]

[I’m glad Rifana decided to come along!]

I’m really glad I didn’t go alone and rely on the two of them.

[But now, we’re split up.]

[There’s no other way around this. It looks like we won’t be able to explore any further without taking some risks, you know?]

[I don’t think there’s any traps here that would kill anyone who presses the switches. In fact, isn’t it more dangerous inside? Either way, it’s pointless unless you and God go together.]

[That’s right, I’ll prepare myself.]

As Rifana said, we had no choice but to move forward. I handed them both a pistol-shaped and a long-range magic gun, and had them open the door and continue on.

[Be careful.]

[Don’t get hurt, okay?]

[Be careful, you two.]

We called out to each other and had the door opened. It was dimly lit inside, but it seemed to be a fairly large space. There didn’t seem to be any traps, so we carefully made our way down the cool, white corridor.

『I found it.』

I saw it appear at the end of the corridor.

Rheal’s voice echoed in my head.

[What is this?]

**『The quasi-deity』**

[This? This… Is this what they call a quasi-deity?]

At the very back of the ruins, atop a strange device, was the quasi-deity. Its appearance was…

[Isn’t that a naked girl?]

Inside a capsule filled with a mysterious, light-green, glowing liquid, a naked girl was floating there.

Her body is young, and she’s probably about the same age as Sherry or Karen. Her eyes are wide open and vacant, and it’s unclear whether she’s conscious or not. A glowing crystal-like object is attached to the center of her chest, and periodically emits a flash of light. The countless cables connected to the capsule appear to absorb the light as soon as it glows.

『That’s the vessel for the quasi-deity. Okay, let’s have it quickly.』

[Wait, wait, wait, explain a bit more. Is she still alive?]

『At least her body. Her soul would have been shattered the moment the deity descended upon her, and even if her soul had been able to withstand the deity’s descent, I think the constant excruciating pain associated with the formation of the quasi-deity would have rendered her an invalid. Right now, that’s just a lump of flesh with the quasi-deity attached to it.』

[What will happen to her if we remove the quasi-deity from her?]

『Her body will probably die. But don’t worry about it, her soul is long gone. She’s no different from a skeleton, just a body with flesh still attached.』

Even though I say that, I can’t help but feel reluctant.

『If you care about her, it’s best to release her from her quasi-deity as soon as possible. Otherwise, her body will be left alone there until this facility decays away one day. Besides, you’ll do whatever it takes to get back to where you belong, right? Is this the time to hesitate over something like that?』

Rheal whispered in my head.

『Now, remove the quasi-deity shining from her chest with your own hands. Let’s put an end to this.』

[…Okay.]

I reached out and touched the capsule. My hand slipped into the capsule. It turns out this wasn’t a capsule, but just a pillar of mysterious liquid.

I reached out to the girl’s chest and touched the hard crystal. The girl didn’t respond. Her blank gaze remained fixed in midair.

[Here we go.]

I gathered my strength, gripped the crystal, and pulled it out in one go. With a sensation like tearing flesh, the crystal was pulled from her body, and the pale green liquid turned red blood. While I stood there, stunned, the crystal I’d pulled out began to sink into my hand.

[Ehh!? Ah!?]

A sharp pain pierced my flesh. For some reason, the crystal, the size of a clenched fist, sank into my palm without penetrating.
