At the same time, a sharp pain like tearing flesh spread from my palm, down my arm, and shoulder, throughout my body. It felt as if shards of glass were clawing at my insides. The pain was so intense that I collapsed to my knees and onto the white building materials.

[Gah!? Guh, ahh!?]

I scratched my whole body, writhing in excruciating pain. It felt like something hard was crawling under my skin.

『I forgot to tell you, but apparently absorbing a quasi-deity hurts.』

You said it too late.

My whole body hurt so much I couldn’t move a single finger. The pain was so intense I almost lost consciousness, only to be brought back by the pain again. This repeated over and over again.

How much time had passed since I’d been enduring the pain? The intense pain gradually subsided.

I somehow managed to stand up, my trembling body shaking, and let out a heavy breath. My whole body was wet with sweat. It was truly uncomfortable. I endured the pain and used purification to wipe away the discomfort.

I wonder how long I’d been suffering for.

『It wasn’t that long. About the time it takes to make five instant noodles.』

Stop with that lame analogy.

『Then it’s about the time it takes for five Titans of Light to return to the sky.』

Stop it.

Now that I’d calmed down, I managed to stand up and opened and closed my right hand, where the quasi-deity crystal had first entered. For the time being, there didn’t seem to be any problems.

[So, was the absorption successful?]

『It was successful. Well, it will take a little time to fully extract its power, though. You’re still a long way from full recovery.』

[Alright.]

At least that’s enough, as long as we’ve taken a step forward.

『I think this should restore about 80% of your power.』

[That’s good to hear.]

I turned my attention to the liquid the girl was floating in. There was nothing floating there anymore. Neither the color of blood nor her body was there.

『It seems like the body has disintegrated since losing the quasi-deity.』

That’s terrible. There’s no evidence of her existence left anywhere. Everything has perished, vanished. And I was the one who made it happen.

『There’s no point in worrying. She perished long ago. All that’s left here is but a faint remnant.』

I can’t just accept it that easily. They’re probably worried about me anyway, so I’ll head back.

---

[We were really worried about you, you know!?]

When I returned to the checkpoint, the two elves were very angry with me. They could hear my cries of anguish from the open door, so that’s to be expected.

[I’m sorry.]

[Are you okay?]

[For now, I don’t feel unwell. It seems like it’ll take a while for me to get used to it, so please look forward to future updates.]

In reality, nothing seems to have changed. The useless Goddess said she’d be concentrating on her work for a while to deal with the quasi-deity I’d absorbed.

[Shall we go back to the village for now?]

[Yes, it might be best to rest for a while. You never know what’s going to happen.]

[The closest village from here is the Snake folk settlement.]

[Snake folk?]

[They have giant snakes for their lower bodies.]

[Lamias… There’s all kinds of them in this world.]

Thinking about the Snake folk I’d yet to meet, I glanced toward the already-closed door at the very back. Those imprisoned in the Tower Prison of Sorrow were gone.

I left the ruins vowing to myself that at least I, at least, would remember the existence of the nameless girl who’d been imprisoned here.

+++

## **91 – Heading to the Snakefolk Village**

Hi, it’s Taichi.

After being completely beaten down by the Gods, I fled to a place where I seduced my wife’s mother and her childhood friend. It’s not entirely my fault, as it’s a plot by a useless Goddess.

『It’s not right to blame others. Ultimately, it’s your choice, right? You can firmly refuse if you want to, you know?』

I know, damn it!

『Well, it’s a man’s shame to refuse the food that’s set before him, right? They say heroes love women, right? I don’t think it’s good to drag yourself too much by the customs of your home world, do as the saying goes』

Ah, shut up, shut up. And right now, the one whispering in my head, trying to drag me down the path of depravity, is the source of all evil, Rheal, the useless Goddess.

『Yes♪ This is the incredibly cute Rheal☆』

Shut up, please. I just want to sort out the situation.

『Yes, yes, I’m busy dealing with the pseudo-deity, too, so I’ll see you later. It’ll take a few days, so enjoy your time.』

Confirming that the useless Goddess had sunk into the depths of my consciousness, I sighed. I opened my eyes and was greeted by the ceiling of a simple tent. It was just big enough for three people to sleep side by side, and I was currently lying there alone.

The light from a campfire was visible through the not-so-thick tent fabric. Outside the tent, my wife, Melchina’s biological mother, Elmina—my mother-in-law—and Melchina’s childhood friend, the dark-skinned elf Rifana, were probably on night watch.

I stared at my right hand, illuminated by the faint light.

It was a familiar palm. There were no particular holes, no scars, and it looked just like any other. However, just a few hours ago, a pseudo-deity had entered my body through this palm.

In one word, it was a 『horrific experience』.

The pain, as if my insides were being sliced ​​to shreds by hard crystals, lasted for apparently fifteen minutes. It’s strange to say “apparently” since I experienced it myself, but while I was writhing in pain, I wasn’t even aware of the passage of time. I later asked the useless Goddess about the elapsed time.

Now, this 『Quasi-Deity』 I had absorbed this time was, in a nutshell, like a crystallized version of the power of the Gods of this world.

Long ago, ancient people would drag Gods, who could be considered higher-dimensional life forms, down from their thrones and turn them into ‘pseudo-deities’, using them as energy sources and weapons to achieve great prosperity.

The reason I absorbed such a thing is simple and clear: to replenish and reclaim the power that had been stolen away from the useless Goddess and I by the Gods. That’s why I’m currently traveling to forbidden areas throughout the Great Forest.

For now, here’s the first of the things I acquired today.

I was able to obtain my first quasi-deity just a few days after starting my exploration… but I wonder if that’s going well. I don’t know how many I’ll need, but I’m sure the useless Goddess will tell me that once she’s finished processing the quasi-deity that I’ve absorbed this time.

But still, I feel really depressed. After all, absorbing a quasi-deity is extremely painful. I’m not sure if I could still attempt it knowing that. It was the first time I’d ever experienced pain so intense I wanted to pass out, but at the same time, it was so painful I couldn’t pass out.

Ah, this is really depressing… No, I mustn’t let negative thoughts get the better of me. I’ll think about something fun. For now, I’ll think about the snakefolk settlement I’m heading to tomorrow.

The snakefolk who live in the settlement I’m heading to tomorrow are apparently a strange species with the upper body of a human and the lower body of a giant snake. From what I know, the half-human, half-snake demi-human is a Lamia. In this world, they’re called the Snakefolk, though.

We planned to rest there for a few days. Elmina said that the Snakefolk have fairly high combat abilities, so as long as we’re in the village, we’ll be safe and not be attacked by monsters.

Rifana looked a little confused, but I wonder if she hates snakes? I don’t really dislike snakes or any reptiles myself, so it’s no problem.

However, in my original world, Lamia was one of the most popular characters in the non-human girl category. They had the upper body of a beautiful woman and the lower body of a giant snake, and were known for using their beauty to deceive men and suck their blood — that’s the kind of existence they were back in my world, but I wonder what it’s like in this world? I can’t wait to meet them.

While thinking about meeting the Snakefolk I had yet to meet, I rested my body until the night shift changed.

---

A small bird I don’t know the name of chirps somewhere. The forest, shrouded in morning mist, was still quiet, with only the chirps of birds, the faint rustling of leaves, and the occasional crackle of firewood in the stove in front of me.

After taking over the night shift just after midnight, I was bored and had built a makeshift stove to keep watch over the pot.

[Good morning, Taichi-kun. How are you feeling?]

As I absentmindedly stirred the pot, a gentle voice rang in my ears.

[Good morning. There seems to be nothing unusual happening so far. Oh, I made a stone bucket over there to store water in.]

[Oh, thank you. How thoughtful.]

Elmina-san emerged from the tent, smiled and thanked me, walking toward the stone bucket where the water was stored.

Shortly after, Rifana also woke up, rubbing her sleepy eyes and walking toward the water source where Elmina-san had gone. It seems Rifana isn’t a morning person. Why is it that a normally grumpy girl is so adorable when she wakes up staring blankly? Maybe it’s the “gap moe” thing.

[Hmm, I guess it’s about right.]

I muttered as I tasted the finished soup.

I removed the meat from the bone-in meat we’d brought from the elf village, washed the remaining bones thoroughly, and quickly parboiled them.

Immediately cooled it in cold water to remove any bits of meat, then crushed them roughly and threw them into a pot of clean water. Once it boiled, I simmered it over low heat.

[Oh, that smells good.]

[I was bored, so I slowly simmered the bones to make soup.]

[I see.]

I carefully removed the scum, added herbs, and simmered them. Finally, I strained the soup through a rough, clean cloth to create the soup base.

I then used some salty dried meat as a seasoning, added some dried vegetables, and the herbs I picked yesterday to adjust the flavor, and the soup was complete. Garnish with some canned biscuits and fruit we found while exploring the ruins, and this was our breakfast.

[Morning.]

[Morning. Breakfast’s ready.]

[Mnn…]

Rifana seems to have washed her face, but she’s still not fully awake. I’m sure she’ll be feeling better by the time we finish eating.

[What kind of people are the Snakefolk?]

[Hmm, they’re normal? They just have large snake bodies. They don’t seem to be very good at magic, but they seem to be quite strong. To be honest, I’ve never had much contact with them.]

[Really?]

[Yes. I sometimes bump into them at Cait Sith or Birdman settlements when I’m out buying supplies, and we occasionally exchange information.]

[Are you sure it’s gonna be alright?]

[It’s going to be just fine, maybe.]

Well, Elmina-san and Rifana are elves, so I’m sure they’ll be okay, but I wonder if it’ll be the same for a human like me. I remember hearing that the people who live in the Great Forest are extremely exclusive towards outsiders.

[It’ll be fine. I’ll protect you, Taichi, no matter what.]

[That’s so cool. Hold me.]

[What are you talking about this early in the morning?]

[I’m fine with it, though.]

Elmina-san’s bold words made my heart flutter. Rifana immediately pointed this out, but doesn’t it make your heart flutter when someone says they’ll protect you no matter what? I’ll follow her example.

After clearing away breakfast and retrieving our tents, we decided to set off immediately.

Since my weapons were destroyed, I equipped myself with a long-rifle-style magic gun I’d recovered from the shelter ruins. It could double as a blunt weapon in a pinch!

[How long will it take to get to the snakefolk village?]

[If we travel at our usual pace, it won’t take long. Why don’t we prepare some souvenirs along the way?]

[Souvenirs?]

[We were thinking about hunting some animals to trade with lodging.]

[I see.]

So, before we set off in earnest, we decided to prepare some souvenirs to take to the snake folk village. Neither of us had hunted around here before, so it looked like we’d be doing it blindly. Will that be okay?

[I found it. This is black elk droppings, and it’s fresh.]

[So they’re heading that way… I’ll circle around them from downwind, follow me, quietly.]

[Aye, ma’am.]

Within 30 minutes, the two seemed to have captured their target. I couldn’t find any droppings or footprints, though. I needn’t have worried at all!

After a few minutes of following the two as they blew through the forest like the wind, they suddenly stopped. I quickly stopped as well. Confused by their sudden presence, Elmina-san ducked down in some bushes a short distance away, while Rifana pulled me into a nearby one.

[What’s wrong?]

[Shh, it’s coming, so stay quiet.]

Rifana held my head down with one hand, quickly readied the bow she was carrying, and unloaded an arrow from the quiver at her waist.

The forest was filled with silence.

All I could hear was the faint rustling of leaves, the chirping of birds, Rifana’s breathing nearby, and my own heartbeat.

After lying low for a while, something caught my attention. It was a fairly large presence, moving at a slow speed.

Emerging from deep in the forest was a huge deer, towering above me. Is this it? A moose or something?

It was much taller than me. Probably just under three meters. It must have weighed about a ton? Can we kill it with a bow and arrow? Do I need an anti-material rifle or something? Will everything be okay?

Next to me, Rifana silently drew her bow and pointed the arrowhead towards the moose (tentative name). The moose (tentative name) stopped moving, seemingly wary of something.

In the next moment, the arrow shot forward, carried by the wind, piercing the moose’s (tentative name) eye. The huge body convulsed and collapsed with a thunderous roar. When I jumped out from the bushes, Elmina-san had already finished it off, slamming her knife into the moose’s (tentative name) thick neck.

[That was a good shot.]

[It just happened to stop the movement at a good angle.]

Although humble, Rifana didn’t seem to mind Elmina-san’s praise, as her ears twitched up and down in delight. What’s this, so cute?

[Taichi-kun, sorry, but could you lift this up to that tree?]

[Got it.]

Taking a rope from the treasure box, I tied its hind legs and hoisted it up from a nearby large tree. Anyway, we need to drain the blood first. Without it, the meat would stink and be inedible.

Its heart was still beating, as blood gushed out vigorously from the neck Elmina had cut open. Hmm, I’m getting used to this sort of scene. I guess I’m adjusting well to this other world.

[What should we do? Won’t it be too much work for just the three of us?]

[Well, it’s not impossible. Let’s just remove the organs for now. We’ll leave the actual dissection to the Snake folk village.]

[Got it.]

We used water magic to drain the blood, then cut open the stomach and removed the organs. We’ll put the organs in a treasure box! Skinning and dissection would be too much work for just the three of us, so we decided to stuff ice made with water magic into the stomach, store it in a treasure box, and bring it to the Snakefolk village for the Snakefolks to dismember.

[Shall we go then?]

[Yeah.]

[Let’s go.]

Elmina-san immediately took off, and Rifana and I followed. The forest around here was relatively calm, and there was none of the oppressive atmosphere typically associated with forests teeming with monsters.

We ran like the wind through this refreshing forest for about an hour. As if sensing something, Elmina-san stopped in her tracks. My detection hadn’t picked up anything yet, but I wonder what Elmina-san sensed?

[It looks like we’ve entered Snakefolk territory. Let’s take it easy from here.]

[How did you know?]

[Look at that tree over there. The bark is scraped off, right?]

Sure enough, when I looked at the tree Elmina-san was pointing at, I saw spiral marks that looked like they’d been made by a giant file or something.

Huh? How big is a Snakefolk if they could wrap themselves around such a thick tree? It’s not like it was a Roll Me or anything like that. If they wrapped themselves around someone, I bet the whole body would suffer compound fractures. Well, maybe the flesh would be scraped off and grated before the compound fractures occurred.

[That sounds dangerous if they wrap themselves around an enemy.]

[They seem to be good at sneaking up and strangling.]

The Snakefolk were more powerful than I expected.

Well, I guess you need to be powerful to survive in a forest like this. I glanced at Rifana, but she didn’t seem particularly pale. Maybe she just doesn’t like snakes.

I walked unarmed, sandwiched between Elmina-san and Rifana. As a human, if I were carrying a weapon, the snakefolk might be wary of me.

[It’s always nerve-wracking meeting someone for the first time.]

[There’s no need to worry so much. They’re not going to suddenly attack with Rifana and me here.]

[To begin with, I think you’ll fare just fine even if you get attacked.]

[Just because it’s fine doesn’t mean I’ll be okay if I’m attacked or hated.]

I’m not the kind of person who feels good or exhilarated when someone shows me hostility. Isn’t it natural for a human to prefer kindness over hostility or malice?

We walked like this for another 30 minutes, and there were multiple reactions to my presence detection.

[There is something nearby. If we keep walking like this, we’ll be surrounded.]

[You can see it clearly, don’t you? Well, there’s no need to worry. Let’s keep going.]

Elmina-san continued walking with a confident smile. Where does this courage come from? Experience, perhaps? This is what they call adult composure. After walking for a few minutes, three snake-like figures appeared before my eyes. There were still six snake-like figures hiding nearby, and now we were completely surrounded.

[Halt.]

The snake-like figures blocking my path were all armed with spears. Their upper bodies were beautiful, and their lower bodies were giant snakes. I was struck by their “lamia”-like appearance, just as I’d imagined. Their upper bodies were beautiful, of course, but the seductiveness of their snake bodies was captivating. Their scales, reflecting the sunlight filtering through the trees, sparkled brilliantly, making them incredibly beautiful.

[An elf… that face seems familiar. What business you have, that you brought a human to our village?]

The snakefolk in the middle asked, expressionless and emotionless. She, too, was strikingly beautiful. The figures flanking me, presumably her subordinates, stood a step back and quietly gazed my way.

[We came here hoping the three of us could stay in your village for a few days. We’re not planning on doing you any harm.]

[A lodging…? Your village is certainly far from here, but… why are you here in the first place?]

[We’ve been traveling around restricted areas for a while now. I brought some gifts, so could you let us stay without asking too many questions?]

[Restricted area…? Well, I won’t ask too much. But, I’d like you to explain more about this human man.]

The snakefolks and Elmina-san’s gazes converge on me. Ugh, it makes me a little nervous when all these beautiful women are paying attention to me.

[I’m Taichi. I’m good at general combat and blacksmithing, and I can use magic pretty well too! You’re so pretty, Onee-san. Your scales sparkle and you’re super cool.]

I gave her a thumbs up and a wink. This will surely make the snakefolk girl fall for me, and the situation will be resolved peacefully. No doubt about it.

[…what was that for again?]

[Hmm, what’s this? A shameless boy?]

[Hey, you know…]

[Ouch! My side hurts! Stop scratching! Sorry for messing around!]

Rifana was actually serious about pinching the soft spot in my side. No matter how high my level and stats get, that kind of thing hurts, so please stop.

[Ouch… But, I don’t know what to talk about. What do you want to know?]

[What is your relationship with them?]

[This is my mother-in-law, and this is my wife’s childhood friend. They’re both my partners.]

[???]

The snakefolk woman looked confused as I explained, tilting her head. It was kind of adorable when an expressionless beauty suddenly showed such a confused expression.

[I don’t really understand, but I reckon you three are close. So can you swear you have no ill will toward our village, or the people who live in this great forest?]

[At least, I don’t currently have any. I can’t guarantee that this will remain the case forever, or for as long as I live. But, at the very least, I don’t think I’ll ever want to harm anyone from my wife’s hometown.]

[That’s honest.]

The snakefolk woman nodded, then turned her attention to Elmina-san and Rifana.

[So, you two elves. Are you willing to bet your life on this man not to harass us with ill will?]

[Of course.]

[If that were to happen, I’d kill him and then die myself.]

It’s heavy! It’s heavy! But knowing that you’d be so prepared to do that for me is, like, a huge blow to my heart. I must never betray this trust.

[In that case, I’ll allow you to stay in our village. Follow me.]

The woman twisted her snake-like body, turned around, and began to slither forward. The two women next to her also turned their backs to me and followed suit. The way the snake-people moved, their upper bodies completely still, was quite strange.

As I walked behind her, I gazed at the snake-like body writhing seductively before my eyes. Yes, it was beautiful, sparkling in the sunlight filtering through the trees. The snake woman who’d been speaking with us earlier had beautiful emerald-colored scales that occasionally shone with rainbow colors in the sunlight. Truly beautiful.

The snake women walking on either side of her seemed younger than the woman in the middle. Both of them had reddish scales. Their scales also sparkled beautifully, sometimes sparkling like rubies or something. As I continued to admire them, my eyes suddenly met with the three women who were looking back at me. I felt a bit embarrassed.

[Human, aren’t you afraid of us?]

[Huh? No, not at all. You’re all beautiful. Your scales are beautiful too.]

[Hmm…?]

The snakefolk woman continued walking with a look of dissatisfaction on her face.

[You’re a strange human.]

[Why is that?]

I was suddenly insulted. Why?

For some reason, the snakefolk women’s bodies undulated about 30% more as they walked ahead. Their movements are dynamic and impressive. And they keep glancing back at me. What’s up with you guys?

I suddenly glanced to the side and saw Elmina-san grinning, and Rifana looking pouty for some reason.

[What is it?]

[Nnn? Nothing in particular?]

[Hmmph.]

I know, I know this kind of thing.

After spending this much time in this world, I’m starting to get the hang of it. I’m not that dim-witted either. So, that’s what it means, right? It’s rare to see a human man who calls a snakefolk beautiful, so the three from before were a little interested in me, right?

Even if that’s the case, what should I do? Well, I guess I’d best just go with the flow.

+++

## **92 – Welcomed (?) in the Snakefolk Village**

The Snakefolk settlement was located on flat land, backed by mountains. Like the Beastkin village, it was surrounded by a log wall. Passing through the gate, several shacks and workshops came into view. Farther back, on the mountain side, there appeared to be some kind of kiln or furnace, from which smoke rose high into the sky.

[Is this the settlement? There seem to be fewer buildings than I expected.]

[Yes, it seems like there are far fewer buildings than the number of people.]

Rifana agreed. Elmina’s gaze seemed to be directed toward the mountain beyond the village.

[Doesn’t that mountain somehow resemble the mountain where the Shelter was?]

[Really? If so, perhaps the Snakefolk settlement is built using ruins.]

As we were talking, we arrived at a plaza-like area. Apparently, this is the central plaza connecting various parts of the village, and there seems to be a fair amount of foot traffic. For some reason, the Snakefolks passing through the plaza keep staring at me.

[It might be a little unsettling, but please use this plaza as you like. This is quite sudden for us, so please give us some time to prepare a proper lodging.]

[Oh, you’ll prepare a place for us to sleep? That’d be great. By the way, Taichi, could you take that out for me?]

[Yes.]

At Elmina’s request, I took out a moose (provisional name) from the treasure box. A massive body estimated to weigh just under a ton suddenly appeared in the plaza, making a whoosh. Ice crunching as it flew out of its stomach, which has been cut open to remove its organs.

[We hunted it to bring back as a souvenir. Skinning and butchering was difficult for just three people, so it’s still a bit incomplete.]

[That’s a big one. We’ll handle the rest of the dismantling.]

[It’s supposed to be a gift, so sorry for the trouble.]

While Elmina was busy talking with the Snakefolks, I used earth magic to create several stone buckets, purified them, and then sorted the organs by type. I buried the inedible ones on site, so all that’s left here are the ones that can be eaten once processed.

As I prepared for camp, I glanced sideways at the snakefolk dragging the carcass of the giant moose (let’s just call it a moose) with several other people. They’d be providing beds for us, but I wonder what kind of beds they’d be? I remember reading in a book or something that snakes sleep in tree hollows or holes they’ve dug in slopes.

[Hey, are you alright?]

As I was setting up the tent, Rifana, who was working with me, asked me worriedly. Hearing this, I opened and closed my hands several times, and tried moving my shoulders.

[Hmm, I’m not feeling particularly unwell. It’s not getting any better, either.]

[So, you can’t ask the Goddess inside your head?]

[It’s busy processing the power it absorbed, so it’s not responding. It said it’ll be done in a few days, so I guess we’ll just have to wait patiently.]

[That’s pretty unreliable… But, don’t push yourself. I swear you start doing weird things if I take my eyes off you for even a second.]

[What do you mean, weird…]

Rifana gave me a hard look, and I couldn’t help but smile bitterly. What exactly did I do? I don’t have a clue… But if I had to guess, I’d say I ran into Behemoth’s flamethrower, saw Elmina naked when I went to pick up some iron, and attacked the ancient robot soldier. Yeah, thinking about it, I’ve messed up quite a bit.

[I won’t let you say you have no idea… Anyway, what should we do now?]

[What do you mean?]

[When I say resting, I don’t mean just sleeping, you know?]

[Yeah, that’s right… I saw something that looked like a kiln or furnace in the back, so I think I’ll go take a look.]

[Hmm…]

She seemed dissatisfied.

[Oh my? Is that what you want, Rifana? You want me to get cozy with you in broad daylight?]

[Wha…?! I didn’t say that!]

[Hahaha, sorry, sorry. I’m a bit cynical, so I can’t help but tease you to see your cute reaction.]

“Swish!”, Rifana angrily moved her hand to slap me, and I let her slap land anyway. Her face was bright red, and she looked really cute.

[Have you two finished setting up yet?]

While the two of us were messing around, Elmina returned. She said she was going to greet the snakefolk leader as a representative, but it seems she’s done with it.

[The tents are set up. Shall we also make a simple stove and a stone bucket for storing water?]

[Sure, please do.]

[You got it.]

Using earth magic, I quickly built a simple stove and a stone bucket for storing water, and filled the stone bucket with water. Earth magic is really useful. It makes it easy to shape earth and stone, making it extremely useful when camping.

[Rifana, let’s go gather firewood with me. Taichi-kun, you can relax in the village in the meantime.]

[Can’t I just help you gather firewood?]

[We’re here to give Taichi-kun a break, so behave yourself. You’re free to roam the village freely, but don’t cause any trouble, understand?]

With that, Elmina pulled Rifana away. Left behind, I scratched my head, wondering what to do.

[Well, whatever.]

Elmina’s actions seemed a little obvious, but I didn’t think it would turn out too badly. There was no point in just standing there, so I started walking toward the smoke rising from the mountain side.

After walking for a few minutes, I noticed something.

[Why are they staring at me sooooo much]

Stares pierced me from all directions. The snakefolk have such strong gazes. The ladies who seemed to be having a chat, the ladies who were carrying some kind of load, and the ladies who were butchering a moose (temporary name) all stared at me. Even little girls were peeking out from the shadows. It’s really scary when people are staring at you like this!

Hmm? Little girls? Come to think of it, I haven’t seen any men. Are the snakefolk, like the harpies, a race with only females? If so, where are their fathers?

I stopped and looked around, but as expected, there were only women in sight. I smiled and waved to a little child looking at me from the shadows, but she quickly hid.

Hmm, they seem to have a very exclusive, or rather wary, attitude towards humans…it doesn’t seem like they’re marrying wandering humans like in the village of Arachnea or anything, so I wonder what they’re doing?

Apparently, the harpies capture male elves or beastkin in heat and are like, “Ahhh!” The ones who get attacked seem to just think of it as being bitten by a stray dog ​​and give up. In the end, they get a good deal and there are no hard feelings for the girls.

It really is an incredible culture, those harpies.

Me? I’m not going to give up or anything, I’m in the position of being healed, so I have no complaints.

As I was walking with this in mind, I arrived at my destination. It seemed the source of the smoke was indeed the smoke from the furnace for smelting iron. In the workshop, several snakefolk girls were sweating profusely as they turned on the bellows and threw fuel and what appeared to be iron ore into the furnace.

As I observed the sweat-soaked girls at work, I suddenly noticed the Green-Scaled Snakefolk, who’d guided me to the village, standing right next to me. Their silent movements were terrible for my heart.

[What are you doing, human?]

[Sightseeing.]

[Sightseeing?]

[I told you before, we do blacksmithing too. I’d be happy if you’d lend me your equipment. I’d also like some iron.]

[Hmm.]

The Green-Scaled Snakefolk slinked along, speaking something to the older Snakefolk woman, who seemed to be the master of the blacksmithing. I couldn’t hear what they were saying over the noise from the blacksmithing.

The two of them glanced at me a few times, then headed over to me together. Yeah, the Snakefolk’s swift movement is a bit strange until you’re used to it.

[You’ll need to pay if you want a share of our iron.]

[Payment, huh… Hmm, how about a whetstone?]

I pull out several whetstones I’d carved and shaped from river rocks while collecting iron ore near the Cait Sith settlement. I used my blacksmithing skills to select these from the many sandstones and slate lying around.

The boss lady inspected some of the whetstones I’d brought out and pointed to a few that were of good quality. Hmm, she certainly has an eye for quality.

[Very well, I’ll give them all to you.]

The boss lady nodded and brought out several mismatched iron blocks from the fire. I hit them with the hammer I’d taken from the treasure box, and they all seemed to be of quite good quality.

[So, how much iron can I have?]

The elder sister tilted her head and thought for a moment, then handed me a few of the iron ingots and placed the whetstone she’d specified earlier next to herself. Hmm, she’d like a little more. I’d need a few more iron ingots to remake not only the sword but also the shattered bush knife.

[Can you give me a few more? If you like, I’ll cut the whetstone to your specified shape for free. This one is of good quality, but it’s a little big, isn’t it? I’m happy to sell it by the piece.]

The elder sister considered my suggestion for a moment, then began drawing lines on the whetstone with wax. I used earth magic to shape the whetstone exactly as indicated. She drew quite delicate curves, so it was quite challenging.

After stroking the whetstone with her hand and inspecting it, the elder sister gave me a firm thumbs-up. She then gave me another iron ingot for free. I gave her a thumbs-up as well, and the deal was complete.

Come to think of it, the elder sister remained quiet for the entire exchange.

[You really aren’t afraid of us, are you?]

[Huh? Yeah, I’m not scared. There’s no reason to be afraid.]

[No reason to be afraid?]

[First of all, I’m strong. I could probably run away even if you all came at me in a group.]

Saying this, I picked up a rock at my feet and crushed it in my hand. The shattered rock spilled out from between my fingers.

[And now, although we’re currently apart, one of my wives is an Arachnean. Do you know what Arachnean is? Their upper body is the same as a human’s, and their lower body is a giant spider. So what if their lower body is a giant snake? They’re all incredibly beautiful, and their scales sparkle and are so pretty. I’m actually curious to know what they feel like.]

Saying this, I gazed intently at the snake’s emerald-colored scales. Hmm, this person’s scales look the most beautiful. Sometimes they even shine with rainbow colors.

[…do you want to touch it?]

[Can I?]

She silently nodded and held out the tip of her tail toward me. Wow, I thought it would be hard and rough, but it’s actually much smoother and moister than I expected. I rubbed it gently and found it had just the right amount of elasticity, and it felt cool and comfortable.

[Huh…! Fuh… Is that enough?]

After I’d been petting her for a while, the Green-Scaled Snakefolk called out to me. She seemed restless, as if she was holding back something. Perhaps I’d made a mistake while touching her tail?

[Thank you. Your scales feel so soft, I’d like to touch them forever. I’ve always thought your scales were beautiful. Sometimes they shine with rainbow colors.]

[Mm, muh?! I, I see.]

There’s something suspicious about the way her tail moves. Is it okay? Maybe I touched her in an unintentional, embarrassing way. I’m sorry.

[I-I have some business to attend to, so I’ll be off now.]

[Ah, yes.]

The Green-Scaled Snakefolk left with incredible speed. It’s amazing that a snake’s body can go that fast. I shifted my gaze and saw the master tilt her head and offer her tail to me. I thoroughly enjoyed it, but I realized that each tail felt quite different to the next.

For some reason, all the Snakefolks who were present at the scene took turns offering their tails. I thoroughly enjoyed each one, but I wonder what it was all about? I felt like a masseuse.

---

[What’s going on here?]

Rifana looked down at me with a forced smile, veins bulging on her forehead.

[Well, it feels good to me too.]

After the tail massage, the ladies at the forge stopped their work and welcomed me. They had prepared fruit wine, fruit, dried meat, and other items from somewhere and began diligently tending to me.

Right now, the snake bodies of the older sisters are wrapped around my legs and waist, my arms and the back of my head are wrapped in soft breasts, and I’m feasting on the fruits and fruit liquor that are being brought to my mouth. It’s a truly wonderful orgy.

I tried to ask them what was going on several times, but the older sisters just smiled and didn’t answer. They were extremely silent, but I wasn’t being treated badly or anything, and they seemed to be treating me just fine, so I just let them do what they wanted.

Sorry, I lied. Honestly, the situation was so amazing that my brain refused to think. After all, you’re surrounded by beautiful women, and this is an orgy of wine and women. It’s a man’s dream.

[G-e-t o-u-t!]

[Ouch, ouch, ouch! It’s pulling everything out!]

Rifana, eyes wide, grabbed me by the collar with both hands and pulled hard. Stop! There are girls crying!

[Let go of him! This is mine!]

“Grrr!” Rifana threatened the snakefolk sisters. With looks of resignation, the sisters began to untie the snakefolk scales that had wrapped around me. The moment they were released, the scales that had been on the other side scraped against my limbs and waist, as if reluctant to let go. It hurt a little.

Finally, the smithy boss sister, who had been hugging me from behind, released me, and Rifana took over. Seeing us like this, the sisters shrugged with a look that seemed to say, “Oh well, I guess there’s no other way”, and after gathering the food and drinks they’d brought with them, blew me a kiss and left. It was kind of cute to see Rifana brushing away the seemingly desperate blown kiss with her hand.

[I knew something strange would happen the moment I took my eyes off you, didn’t it!?]

[Well, they took me by surprise too… I’m so sorry, please forgive me!]

When I tried to play dumb, she started choking me for real, so I tapped Rifana’s arm and gave in. She’d better stop choking me with a smile on her face like that, it’s scary.

[No, Rifana. You have to be open-minded and accept things like this. If you don’t do it in moderation, he’ll get away, you know?]

[Uuh~…!]

After being warned by Elmina, Rifana stopped choking me and hugged me. Elmina also gently snuggled up to me.

[But you have to pay attention to us too, you know?]

She whispered softly in my ear, sending shivers down my spine. Is this a sign that I’m going to have trouble with women today? No, this must be good luck, not trouble with women. Thank goodness… No, this is just as the Bad God had planned, isn’t it? I’m not grateful, am I? I guess this is just a womanizing problem after all.

But, it’s hard not to be happy when a beautiful woman fawns over me! I won’t be able to move for a few days anyway, so maybe I should just let myself be carried away by the rapids!? Think, think. Remember the wives waiting for me back home. Stay cool. Have a will of steel.

[I’ll be fine even if you don’t pay attention to me, too.]

Rifana looked up at me with teary eyes. My will of steel was easily shattered.

**93 – She Finally Appears**

Hammering red-hot iron.

I continued hammering, mindlessly, solely focused on transforming the iron in front of me into even stronger steel. I kept turning it over and over, hammering away. While hammering like this, I forget about a lot of things. That’s right, a lot of things.

Like the Snakefolk ladies staring intently at me! Well, it’s nice when they busily wipe my sweat and bring me drinks, though.

Right now, I’m making a steel sword. That said, I’m not forging ordinary steel; I’ve infused it with my magic power through the hammer, transforming it into a sword made of magic iron, or rather, magic steel, a material whose properties have been greatly altered from those of the original iron.

When large amounts of magic power are infused into iron or steel during the forging process, their properties change, transforming them into materials known as magic iron or magic steel.

Magic iron and magic steel allow magic power to circulate through them better than regular iron or steel, and their magic power retention is greatly increased. If the magic power being imbued has an attribute, the product itself will be imbued with that attribute’s magic power, and may exhibit special effects.

For example, a weapon made from magic iron or magic steel imbued with wind-element magic power will be lighter than it appears, will be sharper, and will be imbued with the wind attribute.

However, such items are not in circulation in large quantities.

Firstly, there are few blacksmiths who can infuse enough magic power into iron or steel to transform it into magic iron or steel. This is because with that much magic power one can achieve some success as a mage instead. There are also very few mages who practice blacksmithing.

Secondly, rather than going to all that effort, it is much easier to use magic metals such as mithril. This is because simply forging it as is will produce performance that matches or exceeds that of magic steel. Imbuing it with magic power is also easier if it is forged together with materials from monsters that possess elemental magical power.

Thirdly, no matter how much effort is put into forging it, its performance will inevitably be inferior to that of a first-class weapon made from mithril or orichalcum.

To be honest, materials like magic iron and magic steel aren’t that popular. They require a lot of effort, but their performance isn’t that great, and unlike magic metals, they rust easily.

However, for me right now, they’re extremely useful metals. As long as I put in the effort, I can achieve performance almost on par with mithril weapons. I have plenty of magic power, after all.

I put the forged steel into a simple furnace made with earth magic and heat it with fire magic. Once it’s red-hot, I hammered it again, folded it, and forged it. I repeated this process to form a rod, and then hammer it again to shape it into a sword. I checked the blade for distortion and balance, then hardened and temper it with water and fire magic, and sharpened it on a whetstone to complete the blade.

All that’s left now is to make the handle from the sacred tree, and create a sheath and belt from the leather and metal fittings given to me by the snake people, and my magic steel longsword will be complete. Including the handle, it’s about 1.5 times the length of my arm. It’s roughly the same length as the Crystal Core Silver Sword that was shattered by the gods. I adjusted the balance of the sword in almost the same way, so for the first time in a while, I finally have a weapon that feels right in my hand.

I tried swinging it a few times and it didn’t feel strange. That’s strange, isn’t it? I thought my sword skills would deteriorate after I lost the skill point system. But, it feels better than I thought. Well, maybe my skills have actually deteriorated and I just don’t feel it.

I also tried out various magic attacks by infusing magic power through the blade. Both flash attacks, which prioritize sharpness, and explosive attacks, which prioritize destructive power, seem to work without any problems. I borrowed some engraving tools from the snake people and engraved magic letters to increase its durability, so it shouldn’t break so easily.

The ladies at the blacksmith seemed interested in the finished magic steel sword, so I handed it to them. They examined it closely, tapped it lightly with a small hammer, listening to the sound it made, and lightly swung it around as if to check its balance.

Apparently satisfied with the sight, the magic steel sword returned from its sheath. That was fine, but then the Boss Onee-sama’s snake body wrapped itself around me. One after the other, the other Onee-samas also came and wrapped themselves around me. Everyone’s cheeks were flushed, and their eyes were crazy. This isn’t good. That’s when I thought to myself…

A loud bang rang out, and the snake body that had been wrapped around me tightened. Ouch!?

[You guys abandoned your duties halfway through yesterday, too. You won’t be forgiven for doing that two days in a row.]

Looking in the direction of the sound, I saw a green-scaled snakefolk with blue veins and an expressionless face. Judging from the large dent in the ground beneath her face and feet, it seemed the sound from earlier had been her slamming her snake body into the ground with all her might.

Yeah, if you get hit with that snake body, it’s unlikely you’ll get away with more than just breaking a bone or two. It’s actually quite scary.

After being scolded by the Green-Scaled Snakefolk lady, the ladies at the blacksmith’s shop looked clearly dissatisfied, but in the end they reluctantly let me go. Thank goodness, I was saved. If things had continued like this, my chastity would have been lost at lightning speed.

[I’ll come back tomorrow to make a shorter blade, so see you next time.]

With that, I waved my hand, and the ladies at the blacksmith’s shop smiled brightly. When the Green-Scaled Snakefolk lady glared at me, they stuck out their tongues. What a long tongue they have.

After walking a little further, the Green-Scaled Snakefolk lady, who had been walking (crawling?) a little ahead of me, turned around with an exasperated sigh.

[Human, you’re a bit too careless. It’s fortunate that I happened to be passing by, but if I hadn’t, things would have gotten a lot worse.]

[Well, that’s fine then. If I really don’t want it, I can resist.]

[So that’s fine then?]

[It’s a man’s greatest joy to know that you desire us so much. You’re all beautiful, after all.]

Hearing my words, the Green-Scaled Snakefolk lady tilted her head, expressionless.

[For you humans, isn’t it unbearable pain to have sex with hideous monsters like us?]

[Huh? No, not at all.]

What in the world is she talking about? We stared at each other with expressions that seemed to say something. Well, the other one had a blank expression, though. That’s what her eyes were saying.

I don’t really understand why people would be reluctant. Unless a man absolutely hated snakes, wouldn’t he normally welcome them? Am I the normal one? Well, I mean, they’re so beautiful, after all. Common sense would tell you they’d be welcome.

[You’re a strange guy, after all.]

[That’s terrible… Now that I think of it, where are we heading?]

I followed the Green-Scaled Snakefolk lady, who sighs and resumes her movement. It seemed that we’re heading toward the rocky mountain at the back of the village.

[I told you we’d prepare your lodging. They’re ready now, so I’ve come to show you around.]

[Oh, the lodging. I’m curious to see what it’s like.]

It can’t be worse than a tent. Suddenly, I’m curious to know what kind of lodgings the Snakefolk prepare.

After walking for a few minutes, admiring the Green-Scaled Snakefolk lady’s slithering, seductive bodies, I come across a gaping hole in the cliff face of the rocky mountain. It’s clearly not a natural cave; it’s a large, rectangular hole. It looks like even a large vehicle could easily access it, but to me, it looks like a giant loading dock or something.

[So this is a dwelling made from ruins after all. Is this entrance still active?]

[It can be opened and closed, though I can’t tell you the details.]

[That makes sense.]

It’s probably some kind of key to protecting the dwelling. But if that’s the case, then that means the power source here is still active. Perhaps a quasi-deity is sleeping here too.

[This way, follow me.]

The inside of the facility was dimly lit. They probably have good night vision, or some other ability to compensate for their vision with something other than sight. I’m sure there are snake species with pit organs that sense temperature, and perhaps these girls also have something similar somewhere.

Like the Shelter Ruins and the ruins where I recently obtained the quasi-deity, these ruins seem to be made of a white, ceramic-like material. The space immediately inside was very large, and I imagined there were large vehicles lined up, or perhaps a large amount of supplies stored there. This facility was probably a military facility or a supply depot or something.

The ceiling was high, and what appeared to be corridors stretched out at equal intervals from both walls. It seemed this facility was huge, consisting of at least four floors. There seemed to be a second, third, and fourth floor above the ground floor I was currently on. There might even be a basement.

[You’re looking pretty intently.]

[This is the first time I’ve seen something like this. I’m curious.]

She glanced my way, but it didn’t seem like she was scolding me. There seemed to be a lot of rooms here, though. The building’s structure was simple, so I wouldn’t get lost, but they’re all probably similar, so I might get the wrong room if I didn’t memorize them carefully.

I was guided to the third room from the front, on the right side of the farthest row. It was a good place to remember. If it had been somewhere in between, like the third or fourth row from the back, I might have made a mistake.

[This is your room.]

[Yes, thanks. Where’s the key?]

[Only an inside lock. We don’t have any thieves among us, but if you’re worried, keep your important things with you.]

[Very well. I guess it’ll be fine.]

I always carry everything in a treasure box anyway. I don’t know how she interpreted my words, but the Green-Scaled Snakefolk lady nodded in satisfaction, opened the door, and went inside. I followed her.

[It’s quite spacious inside.]

[It’s a bit cramped for us, though.]

The room seemed to have some sort of fluorescent lighting, and it was quite bright. The room was about the size of a twin room in a hotel. In the middle of the room was a round, bed-like bedstead. It was about the size of a double bed. I immediately walked over to the bed and checked its firmness.

[Wow, it’s pretty soft. What kind of mat is this?]

[Mat? Ah, bedding. It’s a cloth bag stuffed with animal hair, with another cloth on top.]

Apparently, a clean sheet had been placed over the animal hair mattress. It must be something precious.

[Thank you for preparing such a high-quality bed. I’m sure I’ll sleep well on this.]

As I turned around, I saw the Green-Scaled Snakefolk lady standing before me. Her expression was as expressionless as ever, but there was a strange “color” in her eyes. Alarm bells rang in the back of my head, and I instinctively jumped back.

[Hmm… S-Sorry.]

Seeing my movements, the Green-Scaled Snakefolk lady cleared her throat and moved back, putting some distance between us.

[I was careless. That was a close call.]

[Well, I mean… are you alright?]

[I’m fine.]

She was back to her usual expressionless face, and there was no longer any strange aura about her. It seems like the snakefolk are a race that’s very instinctive. That’s why they don’t get along well with humans and have retreated to the Great Forest.

[Pardon, but I’ll excuse myself now. Feel free to roam around, but please refrain from entering any rooms other than your own. I’ve assigned the two rooms on the hall side to the elves.]

[Yeah, got it.]

[I’ll show the elves around. Be careful if you go out.]

And with that, the Green-Scaled Snakefolk lady left the room.

『That was a shame. You should have just let yourself go.』

No, that one’s a bit dangerous. If she doesn’t attack with a bit more rationality, she might break my bones. Quite literally.

『That’s true. It seems they retain a much stronger aggressive instinct than the Arachneans』

Don’t just say, “Oh, really?” out loud. How’s the progress?”

『No progress』

Go home. Come on! Hurry up and get to work!”

『Just kidding, kidding. Progress isn’t bad. I have something I’d like to show you.』

As the Fallen Goddess spoke, my chest suddenly began to heat up. My heart started beating faster, and the heat spread from my chest to my entire body, gradually fading away.

[Wh-What…? W-What are you doing…Ahhh!?]

A bright light filled my vision, and the abnormal heat in my body immediately disappeared. When the light cleared, I saw a familiar figure on the round, fluffy bed.

[Yay☆ Your eternal lover, Rheal-chan, is here!?]

As Fallen Goddess struck a strange pose, I gave her a fairly serious smack on the head. She quickly crumpled to the bed. Her short dress had flipped up, revealing her pure white panties, and I’d never seen such an unpleasant panty flash before.

[Isn’t that a bit harsh? Surely this is the part where you’re supposed to sob at the sight of my stunningly beautiful beauty, lick my feet, or even get carried away and push me down?]

[Hell no.]

As Fallen Goddess raised her torso and protested, I gave her another smack on the head. That head feels really good to hit.

[It hurts!?]

[When I saw your face, I couldn’t help but hit you. I’m not sorry.]

I looked down at the Fallen Goddess, who was looking up at me with teary eyes. Yes, she was a beautiful girl without any flaws.

She had divine silver hair that looked rainbow-colored depending on the angle, a beautiful face, and a girlish body with underdeveloped curves, clad in a simple white dress. Her perfect figure was pure yet intensely lustful.

[You have such naughty eyes… I can’t help it, it’s fine.]

Fallen Goddess narrowed her eyes lasciviously and gently lifted the hem of her dress to show off her dazzling thighs. I unsteadily moved my face closer to her.

[Hmmph!]

[It hurts!?]

I headbutted her with all my might. The Fallen Goddess clutched her head and rolled around on the round bed.

[Why are you materializing? Are you stupid? Are you asking to die?]

[I can at least create a vessel with my pseudo-deity power. Having a body I can move around on my own is convenient in many ways.]

[Oh. You’re not going to tell me you’ve used up all your pseudo-deity power, are you?]

[Tehee☆]

The useless goddess tapped her head and stuck out her tongue.

[Just kidding! I’m lying! I’m properly regaining my power back! Or rather, I regained some of my power as a pseudo-deity, which is why I’m able to materialize!]

Perhaps sensing my murderous intent, the useless god waves her hand in a panic. Is that true? This guy.

[But, the power I’ve regained is minimal. Still, it’s enough to fool those kids after I materialize.]

The useless goddess waved her hand and shrugged.

[So, how much of my power will be restored?]

[For now, I’ve restored the storage’s functionality! And the contents are still intact!]

Wow, what a smug look on your face. I want to pinch those flared nostrils.

[Wow, that’s a bit smug.]

[Smug?! What do you mean, a bit smug?!]

[Well, when you say contents, all that’s left are my clothes, my favorite foods, seasonings, and some small weapons… Ah, I have some godsilver and black steel stakes. I wonder what else I have.]

It’s been a while since I’ve used my storage. I unpacked the contents and checked them.

[A decent amount of cash, gold, silver, and treasure, and a spare weapon… Oh? I found something good.]

I took out a quarterstaff made of godsilver from my storage. Come to think of it, this was the only one I didn’t use in the battle with the gods, and left it in my storage. I made it, but it was a weapon I never used, as it was overshadowed by the others, and I never thought it would come in handy now.

[This is more durable and works better as a staff than a sacred tree reinforced with Behemoth material.]

I swung it lightly before putting it away in storage. Yeah, it’s a bit inconvenient to carry around. Maybe someday I’ll be able to shrink it down to the size of a pen using the same mechanism I used on the Godsilver Sword.

After checking everything out, I looked over at the bed and saw the useless goddess lying there, looking listless and lazily. From this angle, I couldn’t see, but her legs were probably wide open, exposing her entire body. She looks like a beautiful girl, but she’s like that.

[You should be a bit more modest. That’s why I’m not attracted to you, even if you look good.]

[What’s the big deal? I’m just a useless, useless thing, you know? If you’re not going to appreciate me anyway, there’s no need to bother, right?]

[Ugh, this is so annoying.]

She was sulking to the core. Maybe I’d bullied her a bit too much.

[No matter what I say, I can’t get by without you, so cheer up.]

[Are you just trying to appease me because it’s convenient? That’s not heartfelt, I’m not motivated.]

Apparently, she was completely upset. I had no choice, so I sat down right next to Fallen Goddess’s head and stroked his sparkling silver hair.

[I’m sorry. You and I are in this together, comrades of one mind and one body. I’m sorry for making such a disrespectful remark. I’ll apologize, so cheer up, okay?]

[Hmm… Then I’ll forgive you if you kiss me. Hmm.]

[Right…]

The Fallen Goddess asked for a kiss and gently closed her eyes. Seriously, I wish she’d stop doing things like this. It’s dangerous in many ways. Besides, this guy is really cute, if you just look at her. I’ve treated her roughly up until now just because she’s a bad goddess, and now she’s materialized and is attacking me like this, that’s not right. It’s not right.

[Hurry up, you coward…]

As I hesitated, the goddess’s arms stretched out, wrapped around my neck, and pulled me close. A soft touch met my lips, and an indescribable sweet scent filled my nostrils.

[Mmmmm!?]

[Hnmm…]

Just as I was about to complain, her tongue slipped into my mouth. My tongue tried to escape, but the bad goddess’s tongue entangled itself around mine, sucking out my saliva, making a lewd sound that echoed through the quiet room. A tingling sensation numbed the depths of my brain, and excitement heated my body.

[Hehehe… I’m an Evil Goddess who rules over decadence, hedonism, and all evil pleasures.]

The Evil Goddess let go of my lips and licked the corner of my lip. Alarm bells were ringing. No more.

[It’s fine, alright? You don’t have to hold back… Just take it all――]

[Taichi? Are you there?]

The sliding door opened, and Rifana entered the room. A silence as if the air had frozen filled the room. My excitement level plummeted as well. Thank goodness, I thought it was over. I was saved.

[Again?! Again, huh? By the way, who is that woman!?]

“Grrr!” Rifana roared. I wasn’t saved after all.

## **Someday Will I Be The Greatest Alchemist - 641 - Fluna’s Talent**

A beautiful, clear voice echoed throughout the passages of the gloomy dungeon.

「Yah!」

Fluna swung her sickle spear horizontally, quickly bringing it back to her side then followed up with a flurry of thrusts.

With a single horizontal swing, she decapitated a Kobold Soldier’s head, and the four remaining Kobold Soldiers immediately stopped in their tracks to avoid it. She attacked the unsteady Kobold Merchants mercilessly with consecutive thrusts, striking them in their throats and hearts, taking them down.

Fluna learned the Taijutsu skill relatively quickly, so I expected her to have some potential, but she was more gifted than I could imagine.

Firstly, perhaps because she was a mermaid, Fluna had a really strong lower half.

Swimming underwater at high speeds must surely require substantial strength. And that translates to leg strength in her human form as well.

When she performs a lunge using the spear, her steps were sharp and powerful.

That directly contributes to the spear’s overall destructive power.

That said, it didn’t mean that her arms were weak. It might seem like she doesn’t use her arms when she swims underwater, but she had to move with all that water resistance, so it only makes sense that she had high physical abilities.

The reasons they generally chose to run away from monsters was because sea monsters were enormous and they did not have weapons.

「It might be interesting to train the Mermaids.」

「Mhm, seems like it. If they had Master’s equipment, they could become strong warriors both at sea and on land.」

Kaede and I observed Fluna from behind as she fought.

As Fluna’s support, Berkut stood alert diagonally behind her, so Kaede and I were relatively carefree as we critiqued her fight.

Though, neither Kaede nor I neglected watching our surroundings.

The monsters that spawned in the middle floors of the dungeon were no problem for Fluna and Berkut together. They also had really good equipment, but Kaede and I nodded in admiration as we watched Fluna fully utilize her equipment.

Fluna’s level had risen considerably, and with Berkut, she was now capable of fighting in the middle floors without any danger, so I thought it was time that she train with a knife..

「Fluna, how about you try using the knife now?」

「Y-yes!」

Fluna stored the sickle spear into her magic bag that appeared as a bracelet, and took out the large knife and held it with both hands.

In addition to Berkut, Kaede also took turns to back up Fluna.

I watched attentively from the rear, kept an eye on everything and was prepared for surprise attacks.

Kaede, who used claws, would occasionally assist Fluna in fighting against superior species of Orc-type and Kobold-type monsters as she increase her combat skills and increase her level.

I think having a strong lower was greatly advantageous, no matter the weapon used.

And on top that, I feel as though Fluna, whether it’s specific only to her or if it’s because she’s a Mermaid, had exceptional eyesight.

Fluna kicked the face of an Assassin Wolf, a wolf-type monsters, from below, then drove a knife into its head as it recoiled upward.

It was then that the next Assassin Wolf attacked Fluna.

The Assassin Wolf was a monster that inhabited dark, dense forests and dark caverns, and as its name suggested, it was a wolf-type monster that excel in surprise attacks and ambushes.

This time too, one tried to sneak up on Fluna as she was focused on another wolf.

「Too slow!」

However, Berkut did not allow such an attack happen. With the tip of her spear, she slammed the wolf into the ground.

Gyan!

As the Assassin Wolf yelped from being slammed to the ground, Fluna plunged her knife deep into its head.

She swiftly withdrew her knife from the Assassin Wolf’s head, and dashed towards the Assassin Wolf that Kaede had trapped in her silk.

A short while later, Kaede returned to my side.

「Master, let’s take a break.」

「Okay. Okay, shall we move back a bit to a safe area and take a break?」

「Yup, I’ll call the two then.」

I took out some prepared tea from the Item Box then handed it over to Fluna and Berkut.

「「Thank you!」」

Perhaps exhausted, Fluna’s face was showing signs of fatigue.

「Fluna, are you tired?」

「…yes. I am somewhat exhausted.」

「It can’t be helped, Fluna. You’ve never fought monsters before, haven’t you? Moreover, even though we initially fought the weaker monsters, they’re still monsters from a high level dungeon. It’s only natural that it would tire you physically and mentally.」

「Yup, Fluna, you did your best.」

「Thank you very much, Takumi-sama, Kaede-chan.」

Even Kaede voiced her encouragements to Fluna, who seemed sheepish.

「Takumi-sama, should we head home for the day very soon? We can return tomorrow or the day after.」

「You have a point. Let’s go home then, shall we? Fluna, Berkut, you can stay at our place today.」

「「Yes!」」

I heeded Berkut’s suggestion and decided to head home for the day.

If the exhausted Fluna stayed over, she’d be able to focus on her recovery.

When I offered for Berkut to stay as well, the two responded so eagerly that it shocked me.

Did they want to stay over that much? Now that I think about it, I don’t recall Berkut having ever stayed over before.

Once we were done resting, we concluded our dungeon diving for the day and returned to the Sanctuary mansion.

It might be worth providing the Mermaids equipment and training them. I should discuss that with Fluna sometime.

Fluna’s talent was beyond expectations, it got me curious about the abilities of the other Mermaids.

# **642 - Establish a Mermaid Unit**

After having dinner together with Berkut and Fluna, we talked about what transpired today.

Fluna-san felt embarrassed at Maria’s praise.

Sophia agreed, even saying that having a strong lower body was important in various martial arts, so a race that naturally has that characteristic could potentially be outstanding fighters.

Berkut and the Aligerous Tribe rarely had the chance to eat seafood. It was only recently that they were able to trade with Accuros and eat seafood regularly, and Berkut apparently loves fish.

Strengthening the combat skills of the Mermaids, who were the sole suppliers of marine products, would directly lead to the greater yields.

With the number of citizens in the Sanctuary increasing, demand for marine products continued to rise. Considering this, it made sense to provide the Mermaids equipment, combat training and power leveling.

Of course, there were risks involved, so it was only for those who wish to participate.

Even though Sophia, Maria, and Marnie were busy with raising their children, they welcomed the idea of Takumi’s partners increasing. Akane didn’t share their sentiments, but if the people involved agree to it, then it was fine.

# **645 - Mermangers Vs Sea Serpent**

The Sea Serpent and Fluna’s unit began fighting.

「Hmph, they call it a Sea Serpent, but it’s just an overgrown sea snake.」

Actually, Fluna and the others had previously fought a Dragon-type, serving as their benchmark.

It was a fire-element Fire Dragon, but compared to the Sea Serpent, its scales were far sturdier, and its fangs and claws were extremely sharp and powerful. Moreover, the Sea Serpent is only able to emit a pseudo-breath water current, but the Fire Dragon could breathe actual fire. The difference in their destructive power was incomparable.

**Gishaaaaaーー!!**

With a roar, the Sea Serpent lunged at Fluna and her unit, eager to devour the feast right are in front of it.

「Let’s go!」

「「「「Roger!」」」」

Maintaining their fish scale formation, Fluna and the others swam into the ocean and the Sea Serpent opened its large mouth and dove headfirst.

The waves caused by the Sea Serpents dive rocked the small boat I was watching from a short distance away, and the mermaids who retreated held it steady for me.

Fluna seemed intent on fighting the Sea Serpent in an underwater battle.

---

Fluna’s unit dove into the water and the Sea Serpent chased after them.

With how they are now, they could easily shake it off, but the Sea Serpent would switch its target to their fellow Merfolk if they did, so they deliberately slowed down to lure the Sea Serpent into chasing them.

『Disperse!』

At Fluna’s signal, the five of them changed courses in five different directions like flower petals opening.

The Sea Serpent lunged at the place where the fish scale formation had been gathered until just before, snapping its jaws shut, only to eat seawater.

Gishaaaaa!!

The sound raised by the Sea Serpent was not a roar, however, but a shriek of agony.

The unit that dispersed in five directions had sped up, turned around, and pointed their sickle spears towards the Sea Serpent, becoming one unified spear.

As they pierced its gigantic body and withdrawing quickly, the five had been too fast for the Sea Serpent to grasp an opening for a counterattack.

As Fluna and her unit swam freely and at high speed, they drew traces of red, blue, green, yellow, and pink.

It wouldn’t have made sense if the sickle spear that could cut a dragon’s scales wouldn’t cut the scales that the Sea Serpent was proud of. It shrieked at the continuous onslaught.

Instinctually realizing that it was in a predicament, the Sea Serpent tried to target the evacuating mermaids as it escaped, but it felt more pain than it had ever felt before.

Gishaaaaaa!!

Intense pain came alongside the loss of vision for the Sea Serpent.

Fluna’s unit did not fail to notice the Sea Serpent’s plan to escape. At Fluna’s hand signals, Lana and Mina gouged out the Sea Serpent’s eyes and took away its vision.

『Finish it!』

Fluna and her unit turned into five arrows from different directions aimed at the Sea Serpent wriggling and thrashing in the ocean from its injuries and blindness, piercing deep into its neck.

And with well timed slashes, the mermaids were able to decapitate the head of the Sea Serpent.

The body of the decapaitated Sea Serpent continued to thrash for a while, but that, too, stopped moving soon after.

---

The battle underwater seemed to have concluded.

The surface of the ocean calmed, as if the chaos never happened.

It was then that Fluna and her team emerged from the water. I knew from their presence that the five were safe, but seeing them with my own eyes was more reassuring.

I never even considered that Fluna and the others, who had already won against a dragon, would have lost to a Sea Serpent, but I am a complete amateur when it comes to underwater battles.

「Takumi-samaー！」

They waved their hands.

It seems Lana and the others dragged the Sea Serpent up. I suppose they wanted me to collect it.

I moved the small boat closer to Fluna and the others to store the Sea Serpent into my Item Box.

Looks like we might have a Sea Serpent Barbecue at the beach today.

+++

# **646 - Barbecue at the Beach**

On the beach, Sophia, Maria, and Marnie as well as our children were sitting on the chairs I had laid out for the barbecue.

Today, because the Sea Serpent appeared, they hadn’t gotten as big of a catch with the net, but using harpoons, they did manage to catch several large catches they had never done so before.

To celebrate the defeat of the Sea Serpentー a fitting debut for the Mermaid Squad Mermangersー and their safe catch beyond the barrier, we were having a seaside barbecue.

This was my daughters’ first time at the beach, so they were absolutely delighted. Especially Flora, now capable of walking on her own, was waddling on the sandy beach.

Marnie and the maids were having a hard time keeping up with her.

Perhaps wanting to enjoy the barbecue and have playtime with the kids, Madam Elizabeth, Madam Rosalie, and Madam Lumia quickly tidied up their work and joined us with their subordinates.

Rather, at this point, they’ve completely assimilated as top three of our Government, but were Valkyra Kingdom and Yggurle Kingdom really okay with this?

I created a grilling station using earth magic. Though limited in quantity, the Sanctuary produces some charcoal, but we buy the rest from the Papeck Company. This time, we bought it.

Outside of the Sanctuary, charcoal and firewood were still used for heating during winter, but since I installed heating magic devices into the homes when I initially made the housing in the Sanctuary, and the stores here mostly sold an array of magic devices, so there wasn’t much demand for charcoal.

It’s only when we have barbecues with everyone like today that we use it.

「Okay, the charcoal is lit.」

「Takumi-sama, could you please help break down the Sea Serpent?」

「Roger.」

Once the coals were smoldering, Laeva asked me to help her with dismantling the Sea Serpent.

What I saw was Fluna and the Mermangers were working hard to take apart the Sea Serpent they hunted.

「Fluna, I’ll help with the dismantling too.」

「Ah, Takumi-sama, thank you very much!」

「「「「Thank you very much!」」」」

When I mentioned that I was going to help, Fluna smiled and thanked me, and Lana and the others looked just as happy.

They might have been too happy with me helping, but everyone was waiting so I quickly helped.

「First, let’s cut it into segments of the same length then break it down from there.」

「Wait a minute. If possible, we would like to keep it so the bones are still connected.」

「Roger! Then let’s separate the meat from the bones first.」

「Thank you very much.」

I thought we would slice it into round pieces first to make it easier to dismantle, but then Laeva requested that we keep the bones largely intact. She must have something planned for it. It was more work, but we couldn’t cut corners when it comes to craftwork.

What I took out was not a dismantling knife, but the Holy Sword Vajra.

The Holy Sword Fudou had the Light and Fire attributes, so it would be bad if I charged too much magic power into it.

Not that Vajra was a good sword for dismantling either though. If Golan-san and Doganbo-san were to see this, they would be furious.

Doganbo-san and Golan-san planned to bring alcohol and join us later, so I had to do this now.

The body structure of the Sea Serpent was close to a snake, so I made my cuts with that in mind.

I was using it for the wrong purpose, but as expected of Vajra. It glided like butter and before I knew it, we finished dismantling.

「Fluna, can you cut it up for the barbecue?」

「Yes. Everyone, let’s cut it down to size.」

「「「「Roger.」」」」

I left the task of cutting it to fillets for the grill to Fluna and the Mermangers.

「Ohh! We made it in time!」

「We brought the booze!」

Just then, Doganbo-san and Golan-san arrived with large casks.

That was a close call. If they saw me using Vajra to dismantle that serpent, they would have definitely told me off.

The barbecue on the beach was started off lively.

The flavor of the Sea Serpent was absolutely delicious.

One might assume that the meat would be tough because it’s like snake meat, but the Sea Serpent was not tough. It had the right amount of chew and was a very juicy meat that felt similar to some of the highest quality chicken meat.

「Nom, nom.」

「You don’t have to rush, there’s plenty more where that came from.」

Among my daughters, Flora, who was a Beastkin, was already growing her teeth and weaning. Even now, her mouth was all messy as she bit into the sea serpent meat.

「Yummy~!」

「Right? It’s so good.」

Marnie spoke to Flora as she wiped her mouth.

That’s right. Flora had already started saying some simple words.

However, her first word was “Mama”. Was it hard to say “Papa”?

+++

# **647 - Something That Isn’t A Monster**

At a ghost town on the outskirts of the former Divine Empire of Sydnia. In front of the town’s church, monsters had formed a line.

Undead monsters like Skeletons and Ghouls, humanoid monsters such as Goblins, Orcs, and Ogres. A variety of Wolf-type, Snake-type, Lizard-type monsters. All these monsters were lined up orderly.

The scene of all these species of monsters just lined up without any fights breaking down was bizarre, but there was no one to witness and judge it to be as such.

This was a ghost town, after all.

Baal took a chunk of flesh from the Flesh Tree and bestowed it to the goblin at the front of the line.

Baal’s hand with the flesh sank deep into the goblin’s chest, and when he withdrew his hand, a change began to occur within the goblin.

The goblin’s body bulged and deformed in waves, and as it did, the goblin’s child-like physique grew two-fold, and two small horns protruded from its head.

「Hohoho, this is equivalent to roughly two evolutions.」

「Hmph, is it a monster that isn’t truly a monster? Well, it could serve the armed forces well.」

Agares and Buer assessed the evolution of the goblin.

「What a shame it can not be used on higher species of monsters.」

「Lord Baal, it can’t be helped. The higher species of monsters not only possess high intelligence, very few would follow others.」

Baal sighed as he looked at the queue of monsters in front of him.

They obey the ruling class of their species, but they generally do not listen otherwise. The only exception being in some cases where goblins obey orcs and ogres as underlings, but majority do not obey the rulers of others species.

「We are not human, but not monsters either, after all.」

「…that’s true. Mutated monsters gain intelligence and are more easily commanded. That should suffice.」

「Moreover, this goblin mutated to two evolutions. Greenhorn adventurers stand no chance against it.」

Now the size of the human, the goblin knelt before Baal in greeting, then left the abandoned church.

The goblin that evolved twice had the strength equivalent to a Goblin Knight. Considering how this can be reproduced, it wasn’t a bad result.

The next in line was a Skeleton, and Baal similarly embedded a chunk of flesh into it as well.

GatagatagaClattering bones

The Skeleton’s bones glowed and darkened.

「Hou, it’s roughly equal to a Skeleton Knight this time.」

「No, Agares. I think it’s a bit better than a Skeleton Knight.」

To Agares and Buer, witnessing Baal forcefully evolve monsters had piqued their interest.

That must have been influenced by the nature of the humans they had previously been. As proof of this, Gamigin, Malbas and even Gremory were not present. The two meatheads and the former harlot Gremory were all uninterested.

「Up next is a wolf monster? They’ve got fighting potential if they pack together.」

「Conversely, they have no strength if they don’t move as a pack.」

Agares and Buer watched expectantly as the wolf monster as it went through an extreme transformation.

Its flesh bulged and tore, and from its shoulders grow another another wolf head. Its stature grew twicefold and its fangs grew bigger and sharper.

「Ohh! It’s a success, Lord Baal!」

「Indeed. I can’t understand the rules of the transformation. The gap in strengths are too drastic.」

「Even monsters who were similar by nature have their individual differences.」

The monster that became a two-headed wolf seemed to have been enhanced greatly, so much so that Agares clapped in delight. On the other hand, Baal was had a more complicated reaction, unable to grasp a pattern in the enhancements.

「Next is the orc, huh…」

When Baal embedded the chunk of flesh into the orc, its body darkened and it grew one size larger.

「One level, I see.」

「Hmm, is it because its base abilities were high? Or is there perhaps another reason?」

It seems the Orc’s mutation was relatively minor. Agares and Buer seemed disappointed as well.

After that, Buer continued to implant chunks of flesh into one monster after the other.

「Phew, finally done.」

「Good work, Lord Baal.」

「With this, the strength of our forces has risen sharply.」

「Yes, there’s only a bit of flesh remaining. Gamigin and Marbas, strengthen our forces.」

「「Understood.」」

The Flesh Tree had greatly shrunk in size, and all that remained was reserved for Baal’s growth.

From near the center of the continent, the time until the uprising against humanity was only a little ways away…

+++

# **648 - My Daughters Are Apparently Amazing**

The Sea Serpent barbecue was very exciting.

Flora was frighteningly excited by her first time on the beach, so much so that it was difficult for her to fall asleep that night.

Even so, Beastkin children truly do grow up quickly.

She was happily running around on a sandy beach that even adults have difficulty walking on.

「Takumi-sama, you can’t think Flora was the same as ordinary Beastkin children.」

「Eh?」

The day after the barbecue, everyone was talking about the event yesterday over tea in the living room, and the topic of Flora came up, so I spoke of how amazing the growth of beastkin children was, and Marnie responded with a straight face.

「Uhh, what do you mean?」

「No matter how fast normal Rabbitkin babies grow, they couldn’t move like Flora does now.」

「I-is that so?」

Even when I looked at Marnie to see if she was joking or lying, it didn’t seem like she was.

「No matter how much she is labeled as a Beastkin, Flora is special. They don’t normally move this much.」

「I see~ Flora is amazing. Lulu, did you know?」

「Yes. Catkin babies don’t move like Flora-chan nya.」

Impressed, Akane, who had been listening in on the conversation, asked Lulu-chan, and she said that Flora was also special even compared to Catkin babies.

「Takumi-sama, Haruka and Etoile also had higher physical strength compared to other Elven and Human babies.」

「Eh? Really?」

Maria said something even more shocking.

When I looked at Sophia, she confirmed it so it must be true.

「In Haruka and Etoile’s case, they’re growing slightly faster, but it would be more fitting to say that their physical abilities were high for a baby.」

Their growth specifically was ever so slightly faster, so their bodies were not all too different from normal babies, but apparently, their ability to turn over, crawl, and stand was definitely earlier.

I didn’t know how long it took for normal babies to roll over or crawl, so I never noticed.

「Hold on a minute. Haruka and Etoile can already stand?」

「Yes, Takumi-sama. It happened while you were out power leveling with Fluna and the others.」

How could this have happened? To have missed a milestone of my daughters’ growth…
