「Takumi-sama, Flora was quick to speak as well.」

「So their brains are developing quickly too?」

「Akane-sama, it’s not that they grow fast, but rather that they are excellent nya?」

「About that, maybe what Lulu’s saying is right.」

As I was stunned by how little I knew about my own kids, the Great Spirits Sylph, Undine, and Dryas suddenly appeared together.

「Uwah, stop showing up out of nowhere all of a sudden.」

「It’s nothing new.」

As hopeless as it was, I protested with the three, and they dismissed it as expected.

「Now now, we came here to answer your questions, so isn’t it fine?」

「That’s right~ but that said, even we oneechans don’t know the exact answer~」

「Yes. It’s more of a guess, really.」

Undine, Dryas, and Sylph spoke as they sat down on the sofa, casually asking the maid for tea.

「So what is your guess?」

「It’s simple. The children of an outstanding father would normally inherit a portion of that ability, would they not?」

「That’s right. You may have forgotten, but you have the blessing of Goddess Norn.」

「Indeed~ Moreover, your level is at the top of this world~」

So that’s it. My body was created by Goddess Norn herself. Compared to ordinary humans, my stats were far better, and it was easier to acquire skills because of the effect of the blessing.

When I came to this world, I was just desperate to survive at first.

「Pa~ Pa~~ Ugg~~」

As I was in a daze, I didn’t notice that Flora had approached and climbed on me.

「Huh? Ahh, you want a hug? Wait, Flora!」

「Ay.」

「Y-you can talk?」

「She’s not that good yet, but she has gotten much better these past few days.」

「N-no way, I thought she could only say stuff like mama…」

I was happy she called me Papa for the first time, but I couldn’t help but be stunned at how fast she’s started talking.

Wait, Flora, she climbed on me so easily. Were babies able to do this? No, let’s not think about it. Yup, let’s just believe this was all because of Goddess Norn.

According to Sylph and the Great Spirits, her quick development did not mean that her lives were shortened, they even said it was the opposite, as she would likely live longer than normal Beastkin.

I was relieved to hear this. Because it was possible for that her lifespan would have shortened with her quick development.

+++

# **649 - My Daughters Are Amazing**

Learning that my children were different from normal kids, I used Appraisal on people for the first time in a long time to see.

When I first came to this world, I appraised every single plant and monster, but even then, I almost never used Appraisal on people. I felt uncomfortable peaking at other people’s statuses for my own benefit.

That’s why I had never used Appraisal on Etoile, Haruka, and Flora since they were born.

Let’s look at their statuses, starting with Flora who climbed onto me.

**Flora**

・Race：Rabbitkin

・Age：０ years old

・Job：

・Level：１

・Status: Healthy

・Vitality：20

・Magic Power：12

・Strength：15

・Agility：20

・Stamina：20

・Dexterity: 12

・Intelligence: 15

・Unique Skill

・Passive Skill

・Active Skill

Lightning Attribute Magic Lv1 (Sealed)

Water Attribute Magic Lv1 (Sealed)

Earth Attribute Magic Lv1（Sealed）

・Blessing of the Great Water Spirit Undine

**Etoile**

・Race: Elf

・Age：0 years old

・Job：

・Level: 1

・Status: Healthy

・Vitality: 10

・Magic Power: 20

・Strength: 10

・Agility: 10

・Stamina: 10

・Dexterity: 10

・Intelligence: 20

・Unique Skill

・Passive Skill

・Active Skill

Light Attribute Magic Lv1 (Sealed)

Spirit Magic Lv1 (Sealed)

Water Attribute Magic Lv1 (Sealed)

Wind Attribute Magic Lv1 (Sealed)

・Blessing of the Great Wind Spirit Sylph

**Haruka**

・Race: Human

・Age：０ years old

・Job：

・Level：１

・Status: Healthy

・Vitality：15

・Magic Power: 10

・Strength: 10

・Agility: 10

・Stamina: 15

・Dexterity: 10

・Intelligence: 10

・Unique Skill

・Passive Skill

・Active Skill

Ice Attribute Magic Lv1 (Sealed)

Fire Attribute Magic Lv1 (Sealed)

Water Attribute Magic Lv1 (Sealed)

Earth Attribute Magic Lv1 (Sealed)

・Blessing of the Great Fire Spirit Salamander

I wrote down my daughters’ appraised statuses on paper.

「These aren’t the stats of a baby.」

「Yes. Everyone’s statuses are so high!」

「So they have inherited our and Takumi’s abilities.」

Sophia, Maria, and Marnie were excited upon seeing the written statuses. They’re also glad that our daughters’ statuses were excellent.

My feelings towards my children wouldn’t change based on their status, as long as they were healthy, that’s enough for me.

「So each of them had inherited some of Takumi’s magic attributes. That’s amazing.」

「Flora’s a Beastkin but she has just as much magic power as Haruka, a human nya.」

Akane and Lulu spoke of the children’s magic attributes.

Regarding Flora’s status, there was a show of growth, likely due to her rapid development. And as for her magic power and attribute compatibility, despite how characteristically incompatible the Beastkin were with magic, she had three attributes she was compatible with, and her magic power on par with her human sister Haruka, much to her mother Marnie’s delight.

And Haruka’s magic power and other stats were also high for a normal human baby, so even though Flora was a Beastkin, she had the potential to become a mage stronger than average humans.

「Etoile’s magic power and intelligence are high as well. Even for the Elven race, these stats are not that of a baby.」

When the topic moved on to Etoile, Freesia-san and Dante-san arrived.

「Did something happen? Is something the matter with Etoile?」

「What happened!? Is Etoile okay!?」

「Mother, Father, please calm down.」

「Etoile is fine. We were discussing their appraised statuses.」

「Oh my, Etoile-chan’s status, you say?」

「Where, show it to me too.」

When I handed the paper listing her stats to them, Freesia-san and Dante-san celebrated.

「Dear, this is amazing. Etoile-chan is a genius!」

「Woah! As expected of my grandchild!」

「Please, she is also my grandchild.」

「O-of course. She is our grandchild, after all.」

Ignoring the rowdy pair, I took notice of Haruka’s status.

「It’s amazing Haruka is compatible with four attributes.」

「Takumi-sama, the human race was said to be an average race, so four attributes is outstanding.」

「Right? Maria also has great aptitude for magic, so I’m just worried about anything more.」

Maria didn’t seem to be worried about anything either, but I was worried about the statuses of my truly outstanding daughters.

「It will be alright, Takumi. That’s precisely why we had sealed the children’s magic.」

「Undine and the others sealed it?」

「That’s right. We bestowed them our divine protection too. Normally, when a child has the aptitude for elemental magic, they should still have the status of a Lv0, but they are the children between Takumi, Sophia, Maria, and Marnie. They have yet to reach a year of age, but are already Lv1.」

「It’s definitely dangerous. That’s why we suppress it with our power.」

「So that’s why. Thank you, Undine, Sylph.」

As for the seal, they will release it once the children were old enough to understand and when there was no longer any danger of an accidental magic discharge.

I was really happy that my girls were excellent, but I was worried that they would have a hard time because of it.

+++

# **650 - Educating Grandparents?**

When we learned that our children Flora, Etoile, and Haruka, were excellent, their mothers Sophia, Maria, and Marnie began discussing our daughters’ education plan.

Wait, it’s way too early for that. …was what I would have liked to say but it would be futile.

「I will teach Etoile swordsmanship and shield techniques.」

「What are you saying, Dante? Etoile-chan will use a bow.」

「The frontlines would be dangerous for Etoile-chan. She has Spirit magic too. She would do well as a mage.」

「Mother, Etoile-chan has the Light magic attribute. She should become my successor as the next Saintess.」

「No, Lady Mimir, her mother Sophia was a former knight. Etoile should aim to be a knight too.」

「That won’t do, Dante. If she swings a sword, her hands would become rough and calloused.」

「It’s no different if she uses a bow though.」

Dante-san and Freesia’s debate continued with neither side compromising. They were the grandparents, after all. But Yggurle Kingdom’s Queen and Princess too…

And for Maria, who supposedly didn’t have any family…

「Haruka-chan would be nice as a normal bride.」

「Martha, what are you saying? I will never let Haruka-chan marry!」

For some reason, Vanga-san and Martha-san were quarreling while doting on Haruka.

But, Vanga-san. I should be the one saying those words.

Ever since the kids were born, Vanga-san and Martha-san visited the mansion more frequently. Vanga-san and Martha-san loved not only Haruka, but also Flora and Etoile, as their grandchildren.

Well, at least they weren’t arguing about whether she should be a knight, a mage, or, god forbid, a Saintess, so that’s a relief.

Etoile in particular had the rare Light attribute, so Mimir wanted her to be a Saintess by all means.

I thought they wouldn’t be in a hurry to search for the next generation Saintess since they were a long living race, but more than anything, I wouldn’t give Etoile to Yggurle Kingdom. That’s practically the same thing as marrying her off.

Such were things that I wanted to happen only after my lifespan ends.

And the ones keeping Flora, who was running around by herself, were Madam Elizabeth and Madam Rosary. And Charlotte-san was there to keep the two in check.

「I wouldn’t mind if either Flora-chan or Haruka-chan succeed the Vold Family’s barony.」

「Mother, please do not say such absurdities.」

「Then would you like to marry into the House Packard?」

「Oh my, in that case, what do you think of House Portfort? You have no more than a 10 year difference with my grandson.」

「Madam Elizabeth, Madam Rosary, no matter what, your esteemed houses are not families that commoners can marry.」

Marnie’s face paled and said it was impossible.

That’s what I thought too. Ever since she came to live with us in the Sanctuary, she had more chances to meet royalty and nobility, but Marnie was a Rabbitkin from an impoverished village. The only person with a high position in the small village was the village chief.

「Flora-chan would make a great warrior nya. I’m jealous nya.」

「Really nya. Both the Cat Sith and Rabbitkin are races not well suited to be warriors too, she’s amazing nya.」

「Look, Flora-chan, it’s Miri-oneechan nya.」

「Lala too, Lala is an oneechan too nya.」

Today, the Cat Sith family made a rare appearance.

Mappo-san and Poporo-san voiced their envy as they watched Miri and Lala chase and play with Flora.

Among the Beastkin, Catkin and Dogkin were hunting races, so they had combat abilities suitable for warriors, but Rabbitkin, Raccoonkin, and Ratkin were unsuited to be hunters and warriors. The petite Cat Sith was a race even less suited to be warriors.

Mappo-san longed to be warrior because he knew he couldn’t do it.

In the Cat Sith village, the best they could do was to hunt small animals with a short bow, and no one made hunting their profession.

Wait, everyone is talking about the future of my daughters as they please, but they were MY daughters.

Marriage was absurd.

I wouldn’t let Yggurle Kingdom have them.

Of course, the same goes for Valkyra Kingdom. I would not let them marry into Madam Elizabeth’s Vold Barony, nor Viscount Packard’s House. Of course, it was the same for Madam Rosary’s House Portfort.

+++

# **651 - Too Early To Tie**

In a room within the Royal Castle towering over the Capital of Valkyra Kingdom. Five men gathered in the room that only a select few were permitted entry to.

One was the ruler of this nation, King Lobos Valkyra.

His Prime Minister, Simon von Portfort.

The Commander of the Knight Order, Galahad von Bauer.

The Earl Reud von Rockford.

And lastly, Margrave Godwin von Volton.

Naturally, there was a reason why these five key figures supporting Valkyra Kingdom had gathered.

「As they were Iruma-dono’s daughters, it’s understandable, but I suppose he would dislike a blatant political marriage.」

「My wife and Honorary Baroness Vold had been taking various matters into consideration.」

Yes, the secret gathering between the King of Valkyra Kingdom, its Prime Minister, Knight Commander, Earl, and Margrave was to discuss Takumi’s daughters, Etoile, Flora, and Haruka.

The one that leaked this information was, of course, Simon’s wife, Rosary.

Having learned of the exceptional statuses of Takumi’s children, Rosary wanted to confirm with Simon if their grandchildren already had fiancées while she still continued to seclude herself in the Sanctuary.

Simon immediately understood the meaning behind her sudden inquiry. After all, he had served as the Prime Minister for many years.

「Queen Lumia wanted Miss Etoile for Yggurle Kingdom. Even Princess Mimir had considered her to be the next Saintess.」

「If they are considering her as a Saintess, does that mean that Etoile has the aptitude for the Light attribute?」

When Simon relayed the information on Etoile, even King Valkyra was astonished.

「No, Your Majesty. If an Elf were to have the aptitude for the Light attribute, they would wish to become the Saintess, even if it weren’t Princess Mimir.」

「Indeed. Just as Godwin had mentioned, Yggurle Kingdom is one step ahead with Miss Etoile.」

Margrave Volton and Earl Rockford judged that Yggurle Kingdom had the advantage with Etoile.

「Regarding Miss Haruka and Miss Flora, it isn’t only Rosary, but even Madam Elizabeth was aiming for the revival of the House Vold. If that was ill suited, she even considered her parental family, House Packard and the Viscounty.」

「Madam Elizabeth has grown stronger. Her daughter, Lady Charlotte, also works for Iruma-dono. You could say their connection runs deep.」

When Simon mentioned that Elizabeth was aiming for Haruka and Flora, Margrave Volton grew wary of Elizabeth’s shrewdness now, as though her previous dispirited self was all but a lie.

「No, more importantly, does there anyone here with exception to myself have someone of a suitable age?」

「Your Majesty, surely a marriage to the royal family is impossible, is it not?」

「What do you mean, Simon? Iruma-dono is the representative of the Sanctuary. It would be no exaggeration to call the Sanctuary a small country now. Well? You could even say that it’s a marriage between royal families.」

「Your Majesty, is that not quite forceful?」

Among the members present, the only ones who could immediately provide children of a suitable age to match Takumi’s daughters was King Valkyra. Even Simon would have to coordinate the engagements of his grandchildren. Though engagements between small children were often cancelled, there was proper procedures that must be followed. In comparison, talks of engagements involving the royal family often took longer to finalize. Even now, there were still princes whose betrothals have yet to be set…

「Your Majesty, in terms of matching ages, do you mean _that_ prince?」

「Would that one be unwise?」

「It would likely enrage Iruma-dono…」

Simon’s concern was understandable.

The youngest prince of King Valkyra was now six years old. Age-wise, he was a good match with Takumi’s daughters, but this youngest prince posed a problem.

His eldest son, the crown prince was famed for possessing both exceptional character and abilities similar to the wise King Valkyra, and it was said that Valkyra Kingdom had a bright future ahead. On the other hand, the sixth prince was spoiled. Likely due to the presence of a capable heir, his education had been neglected, so he became a selfish and prideful child. He was only six years old too.

「There’s nothing we can do though! Everyone but Ruvos is engaged. There’s the option of taking Iruma-dono’s daughter as a concubine as well, but of course we can’t say that out loud.」

Aside from his youngest son, everyoneー including those that he could marry outー already had fiancées. None of those fiancées would willingly switch from the main wife to concubine.

「Your Majesty, shouldn’t we first ask Iruma-dono and his wives?」

「O-oh, come to think of it, that is so.」

「If it’s Iruma-dono, he might say that marrying into the royal family is out the question.」

「Urk… that’s possible.」

Earl Rockford advised King Valkyra, who had begun talking about the sixth prince, to calm down. It was then that Galahan pointed out that, based on his character, Takumi would not even want to have ties with a royal family.

Takumi was the type of person who would rather not stand out, to the point that he even hid the fact that he was the Custodian of the Sanctuary and the Protector of the Spirit Tree. Galahad could not imagine Takumi wanting to be related to the royal family.

「T-then should we try talking to him indirectly about his daughters’ betrothals?」

「The moment we ask about that, it would no longer be indirect.」

「Now, now, Prime Minister. As the one who he has known the longest, let me ask first. If we leave it to Madam Rosary after that, she might be able to steer the conversation to the favor of House Portfort.」

「Lord Volton! That… may work. In that case, shall we leave it to you?」

「And while you’re at it, make sure to look into the detailed statuses of Iruma-dono’s daughters.」

「I understand.」

And so, the five concluded their secret discussion regarding the leaked information on Takumi’s exceptionally abled children.

Though, no matter who the partner may be, Takumi would not delight at the thought of his children’s betrothals.

+++

# **652 - Takumi Firmly Refuses**

When it turned out that Etoile, Haruka, and Flora’s statuses were exceptional, Madam Lumia first, then Madam Elizabeth, and Madam Rosary began making some moves.

That won’t do. My girls were still only babies.

Despite that, Margrave Volton visited the Sanctuary.

So why was Margrave Volton coming to see my daughters?

「Wow, the three would really grow up to be beautiful.」

「W-well, thank you for that.」

Such words put a smile on my face.

「Look, Dear. Flora-chan and Haruka-chan are adorable too, aren’t they?」

「Ohh, do they take after their mother? They are similar to Iruma-dono as well.」

That wasn’t all. Even Lord Simon, the Prime Minister of Valkyra Kingdom, was here.

So why did Lord Simon come? What of his duty to his country? Would they be alright if he leaves the Royal Capital so easily?

Lord Simon said that he came to meet Madam Rosary, but that was definitely a lie.

As I thought that, Lord Simon and Margrave Volton approached me.

「Iruma-dono, you have such adorable daughters.」

「Margrave Volton, thank you for coming personally to congratulate us.」

「What, that’s how you and I are, no?」

Margrave Volton’s reason for visiting was more or less to bring felicitations.

「Also, I heard that all three children have the aptitude for multiple attributes. Regarding that, may I hear the details, Iruma-dono?

「Umm, isn’t asking about someone’s status a breach of etiquette?」

「Now, now, aren’t you and I closer than that?」

All of a sudden, Margrave Volton asked about my daughters’ statuses.

Of course, I refused from the point of privacy of personal information, but this world obviously had no laws for data privacy protection. Rather, it was actually more difficult to refuse since high ranking individuals such as nobles could order you to disclose it.

Well, I live mostly in the Sanctuary now, so that doesn’t concern me.

「Settle down, Lord Volton. Such talks are not rushed, now are they?」

「Ohh, my apologies, Lord Portfort. I must have gotten ahead of myself.」

Lord Simon curbed Margarve Volton’s advances.

「By the way, Iruma-dono, your children have yet to be engaged, are they not?」

「It hasn’t even been a year since they were born, so there’s no way they would already be engaged.」

So Lord Simon did indeed come to talk about engagements. My children haven’t reached one year old yet, you know? Seriously, give me a break.

「Well, given how high infant mortality is, it is rare even for nobles and royalty to have a betrothal set before the age of 1. However, infant and child mortality is practically nonexistent in the Sanctuary, is it not?」

「Of course, dear. This is the Sanctuary, where the Great Spirits have manifested. The Great Light Spirit Selene is here as well, it would be impossible for infants and children to die prematurely.」

「Ohh, indeed, indeed.」

According to Lord Simon, it was rare, even for nobles and royalty, to set engagements for babies under a year old due to high infant mortality rate in this world.

However, he said that this logic did not apply to the Sanctuary, and Madam Rosary even doubled down on it.

Sure, in the Sanctuary where we and the Great Spirits live, we would immediately respond to anyone who falls ill, so serious cases were few and far in between. Even before this, it was very rare for the people of the Sanctuary to get sick.

This was believed to be due to the sacred power of the Spirit Tree that filled the Sanctuary, as well as the influence of the Great Spirits’ manifestation.

「For the same reason, the children of the royal family who were less likely to perish prematurely, there were rare cases where their betrothed were decided upon at the moment of their birth.」

「Well, even those only happened on rare cases. And it’s troubling to be compared to the royal family.」

It bothered me that my children were being compared to those of royalty. In my previous life, I was raised by an ordinary salaryman household, and I myself had become an ordinary salaryman.

However, Lord Simon and Madam Rosary pointed out the flaw in my reasoning.

「The current state of the Sanctuary is comparable to a small nation with an influence beyond a large nation. And you, Iruma-dono, are its representative.」

「W-well, that is true.」

「Now, we are not talking about an immediate engagement. it’s enough if you keep this conversation in the back of your mind.」

Lord Simon said as such, and Madam Rosary nodded in agreement, but my instincts were telling me that this was not as simple as it seemed.

Lord Simon came all the way from the capital to assess my children, and for some reason, Margrave Volton kept emphasizing his connection to me.

For as long as my pupils are black, I will not let my children be married off.

+++

# **653 - Increasing Parameters**

I thought it couldn’t be helped that Margrave Volton and Lord Simon were being annoying.

But I’d rather they didn’t strategize behind the scenes with Madam Lumia, Mimir, Madam Elizabeth and the others, leaving my wives and I out of it.

In a room in the Lodge at the annexed district by the entrance of the Sanctuary, Margrave Volton, Prime Minister Simon of Valkyra Kingdom, his wife Madam Rosary, and the honorary Baroness Elizabeth had gathered.

「So, is Miss Etoile non negotiable for Yggurle Kingdom?」

「Yes, she is an elven child blessed by the spirits to possess the Light attribute. Madam Lumia and Princess Mimir were trying desperately.」

Rosary nodded and answered Simon’s question.

「Is it too much of a stretch to claim that Iruma-dono is a citizen of Valkyra Kingdom?」

「That would be too unreasonable. Etoile-chan and the girls were born in the Sanctuary too.」

The reason Simon, Rosary, and the others were fixated with Etoile, Haruka, and Flora wasn’t because of their high capabilities. In the end, it was that they wanted a firm connection with the Sanctuary.

「Geez, it was only me in the beginning, but now not just Madam Rosary, even Madam Lumia and Lady Mimir were taking part.」

「Naturally so. No one is allowed to have an edge over the others.」

Having worked together in the Government building, Elizabeth and Rosary had a conversation from which you could tell how relaxed their relationship was.

「Still, am I the only one who wants him to have more children since this is the case?」

「No, His Majesty and I feel the same way. That having been said, it would be difficult to increase the number of his wives.」

To Simon and King Valkyra, Takumi should take in more wives than just the three he currently has. It would be even better if they were from houses with close ties to them.

「But from Iruma-dono’s position, aren’t three wives plenty?」

「…so we’re looking for good natured, extremely beautiful, and talented young women… it’s worth an attempt, I suppose.」

「Oh my, in that case, wouldn’t my daughter do?」

「Madam Elizabeth’s daughter, do you mean Lady Charlotte?」

「Indeed, she is working properly as an aide in Takumi-kun’s house. Moreover, I am not trying to be boastful because she is my daughter, but that girl is beautiful.」

When Margrave Volton and Prime Minister Simon discussed assigning a new wife to Takumi, Elizabeth recommended her own daughter Chalotte, who worked as an aide to Takumi in his home.

「…how old is Lady Charlotte?」

「She turned 18 years old this year. She isn’t too young, perfectly of age, don’t you think?」

「Elizabeth-san, didn’t you plan to have Charlotte marry in hopes of reviving the Vold Barony?」

「Madam Rosary, I am not fixated with the Vold Barony. I would be happy if it was revived, but to live in the Capital now, you understand, don’t you?」

Elizabeth had grown fond of living in the Sanctuary, so she had no inkling to return to her life in the Royal Capital, nor did she want to regain her own territory.

「Indeed. Chalotte would be close by, and the latest fashion trends come from Akane-chan, so we could have access to it first. I, too, have no desire to return to the Capital.」

「Oi, Rosary! Do you not intend to return anymore?!」

Rosary casually announced her intention to live permanently in the Sanctuary, bewildering Simon.

「After all, our children no longer require much care, and I have grown tired of tea parties and gatherings with other noblewomen in the Capital. Ever since you had become the Prime Minister, I had given it my all to collect information for you. Surely, that is no longer the case?」

「…perhaps it is time I retire and immigrate as well?」

「It’s wonderful, the Sanctuary~. The food is delicious, and entertainment is more plentiful as well. The concert hall and church are both splendid. I believe you would do well as a teacher at school too.」

「A school teacher, huh… it might be enjoyable to teach kids. Well, for now, I will discuss the matter of Iruma-dono’s daughters as well as introducing him to new wives with His Majesty.」

Godwin and Simon seriously began to consider having Takumi take in new wives.

Seeing this, Rosary and Elizabeth thought it best to discuss it with Takumi before talking to the King, but they did not say this to Simon nor Godwin.

They were convinced it would fail anyway.

Having grown closer to Takumi, both Elizabeth and Rosary knew how extremely shy and dense he was.

+++

# **654 - Old Men’s Foolish Errands**

With Rosary and Elizabeth’s help, Godwin and Simon learned of Etoile and the children’s aptitude for magic. They left after telling Takumi to consider engagements for his three daughters positively.

---

What was all that about? There’s no way I would have agreed to an engagement.

I felt relieved when Margrave Volton and Lord Simon left, but I don’t think that makes me a doting parent.

「Really, I apologize for this.」

「No, Madam Rosary. As a prime minister, Lord Simon has a job to do.」

「But to think that his job involves discussing your daughters’ engagements, it makes one wonder what a prime minister’s job truly entail.」

「Ha, haha.」

As always, Madam Elizabeth and Madam Rosary made themselves comfortable in my living room.

Madam Rosary apologized for Lord Simon’s suden visit, but I knew deep down that she and Madam Elizabeth were also eyeing my daughters.

「But Takumi-kun, I think proposals for engagements will start flooding in from now on.」

「Indeed, at this moment, only we know about it, but this is a matter that is bound to be discovered.」

Then, as Madam Rosary and Elizabeth were leaving, they casually dropped a troublesome statement.

I couldn’t help but let out a deep sigh.

---

Once they finished gathering information in the Sanctuary, as well as even managing to bring up engagement talks for even a moment, Godwin and Simon achieved their goals and headed home.

Godwin returned to Volton temporarily to deal with miscellaneous tasks, then would head to the Royal Capital. Simon returned straight to the Royal Capital.

Upon his return, Simon immediately had a private conversation with King Valkyra.

In their usual room, with the usual members, King Valkyra immediately asked Simon about Takumi’s daughters.

「So, how were Iruma-dono’s children? Was it as your wife stated?」

「Yes. It wasn’t only the elf Miss Etoile. Even the human daughter of Maria-dono could be an excellent mage, Miss Haruka had the aptitude for four elements. Lastly, despite being of a Beastkin race normally unsuited for magic, Miss Flora possessed the aptitude for three elements. It is certain that the children inherited Iruma-dono and and their mothers’ abilities.」

「Hou, that is impressive. However, if that information were to be leaked, many noble families would want to have Iruma-dono’s bloodline.」

「Those who were incessant about Iruma-dono’s commoner origins would likely not attempt contact to begin with.」

Both Simon and King Valkyra had no negative feelings towards Takumi for being a commoner even before he became the keeper of the Sanctuary,

They recognized him as someone who had contributed greatly towards the Kingdom’s development through his many inventions, and had witnessed his extraordinary talents firsthand.

While some nobles might be reluctant to marry their daughters to Takumi, there would be lesser reservations to having Etoile, Haruka, and Flora marry into their families. And it was likely that many would want them as concubines rather than legal wives.

「Well, those look down on Iruma-dono for being a commoner were only the Noblist faction.」

「The Royalist faction and Neutral faction are not as arrogant.」

In this world, Mages were largely utilized. In a world without firearms, they were a particularly effective means of powerful monsters, so it was practically a given.

And in general, excellent mages were mostly nobles.

That was because magic aptitude was often inherited.

Many noble families sought strong mages blood, keeping it within the family and connected.

Of course, there were times where someone with high magic capabilities suddenly appear from the commoners. It wasn’t rare for noble houses to compete for them.

Takumi, who was recreated and blessed by Goddess Norn, was a special case because of her influence, but that made him stand out more.

If they weren’t a member of the faction at odds with Margrave Volton and Earl Rockkford, they would have wanted to make a connection with him.

「Oh yes. I heard that there was also a school in the Sanctuary. What do you think of dispatching young women as teachers there?」

「The bar is set too high for civil servants, and their time with Iruma-dono is limited as well. It might be possible with teachers. In that case, they could sojourn to study music in the Sanctuary. The orchestral band there is special, after all.」

「Children of aristocracy have been tutored in education and music since youth. Let’s try that route.」

「Let’s continue vying for betrothals for Iruma-dono’s children, and offer mistresses and concubines to him.」

「Mhm, make sure this doesn’t leak it to the noblist faction.」

「Of course.」

King Valkyra known as the wise king, and Simon who had been supporting the country for many years were enticed by Takumi’s denseness.

Takumi was already blind to even the most transparent show of favor to the more proactive approach from the mermaid Fluna and Berkut of the Aligerous Tribe.

If even the women acquainting themselves with him could not make any progress, when would these two ever know.

+++

# **655 - Increasing Number of Applicants**

A little while after Margrave Volton and Prime Minister Simon returned, there was a gradual increase of new applicants wishing to immigrate.

Basically, I accepted everyone that Sylph and the Great Spirits approved of, but meeting the standards of those Great Spirits wasn’t easy.

Short term, temporary visits to the Sanctuary weren’t as high, but they would have to stay in the Annexed District.

Lord Simon stayed in Madam Rosary’s mansion, but Margrave Volton still stayed in the Lodge at Annexed District.

The Great Spirits and I were looking over the immigration applications.

「I wonder what this is all about. They are all young ladies of respectable families.」

「Takumi, in this world, the youth that have been educated are the children of nobles and wealthy merchants.」

「Indeed. It’s not unusual for workers and farmers to not be able to read.」

「Well, that’s how it is.」

Looking at the list, there were many hoping to become teachers and staff in the school in the Sanctuary. And so, it made sense that the children of nobles and merchants who had received proper education since childhood would apply.

「Moreover, the children of Valkyra Kingdom nobles also attend schools.」

「Oh Undine, isn’t it a place to network and form factions~?」

「Even so, you would need a certain level of knowledge to enroll.」

When Undine mentioned the school in the Royal Capital, Dryas pointed out that it wasn’t an establishment purely for the pursuit of knowledge.

There was a school in Valkyra Kingdom for the children of nobles and wealthy merchants.

In this world, it was a given for children not born to affluent households to be made to work since their youth. Attending school was enough to show one’s family background.

「If the child is exceptionally gifted, they can attend school on a scholarship.」

「They are exceptionally few though.」

To commoners here, literacy was only necessary for adventurers and traders. Even among the traders, only the wealthy could afford to enroll their children into school so they could maintain connections with nobles.

「Still, I’m definitely glad that people want to become teachers and staff for the school. But what is this music study abroad program?」

「Among the nobles, the concert hall and orchestral band here are famous. Innovative songs and instruments the world had never seen before have begun spreading to the capital, and there were some aspiring children who wish to learn from the source.」

I was honestly grateful that the school would have an increase in number of teachers and staff because of the personnel shortage. It didn’t necessarily mean that being accepted by the Great Spirits equaled excellence, but right now, we were so short on staff that we couldn’t be more particular. As long as they were kind-hearted, we accepted them.

There were also plenty of applicants besides the school teachers and staff, but they were people aspiring to join the orchestra, or learn from them.

These were 100% children of nobles.

Only the children of nobles learn music at such a young age.

「A school specializing in music is interesting, but that’s impossible right now.」

「Currently, everyone in the band is focused on their own work, after all.」

I do think it would be possible to establish a music-focused school at some point. Well, considering how we’re already struggling with the lack of personnel in a regular school, having teachers for music was simply unrealistic.

While looking at the list, I brought up the interviews.

Whether or not we accept them is another matter, but if we don’t at least conduct interviews, it could disgrace Lord Simon and Lord Godwin who sent the list.

「It’s fine if we do the interviews in the capital, right?」

「Indeed. Unlike with the civil servant, it would be difficult for them to come all the way here.」

When Undine said that, everyone else nodded.

When they were doing civil servant interviews, the rejected people could still find employment in Wedgefort and Valor, but it was a different story making nobles, especially the women, come to the Sanctuary for interviews.

「Still, why were there so few men? It’s a 9:1 ratio.」

「Fufu, Takumi-chan, you don’t need to know~ 」

「Eh, Dryas, you know why?」

As the list that was practically all women left me confounded, Dryas eluded to knowing the reason.

「Fufu, about that~」

「Okay, okay, there’s no one to be rejected from the document screening. Takumi, you can ask that prime minister to confirm the schedule.」

「W-wait, Sylph. Eh, does everyone know?」

I tried to stop people, but they just handed me the list and left in a hurry.

What was that about? It was frustrating, but Sylph and the others never say anything at such times.

+++

# **656 - More Ladies… And then**

I coordinated with Lord Simon on the schedule, then went to the Royal Capital to conduct interviews with people who wished to become school teachers and staff, as well as those who wished to study music with the orchestra.

As always, the interviews were conducted by Sophia, Akane, and I, along with four of the Great Spiritsー Undine, Sylph, Selene, and Nyx.

As written on the list Lord Simon had provided in advance, most applicants were young women.

Among them were a few individuals that had many years of being a private tutor under their belt, but they were the minority.

Such accomplished individuals who had also passed the Great Spirits’ screening were immediately considered teacher candidates.

Perhaps because Lord Simon had also investigated their family backgrounds and factions in advance, there were very few especially troublesome characters.

That said, there was no way we could approve everyone’s immigration.

According to Undine and Selene, even if the applicants themselves had no issues, there were cases where the problems were with their parents or noble sponsors.

During a break in interviews, I asked where they heard that about those people. Sylph and the others said that they did background checks of their circumstances. They entrusted it to their familial spirits though.

「What do you do with the applicants with troublesome parents or guardians?」

「If the applicant themself was not problematic, and if their parents or guardians weren’t planning anything too sinister, they may pass.」

「It would be wrong to reject someone simply because their parents or factions were problematic, no?」

「You’re right about that.」

It’s as Sylph and Undine had said. Even if the parents and guardians were plotting things, they were likely to be safe as long as they remained in the Sanctuary.

And so, the number of people aspiring to become school teachers and staff in the Sanctuary increased. Some had also been scouted by Madam Rosary, Madam Elizabeth, and Madam Lumia to become personnel for the government office.

We would need to build a housing complex for those coming to study with the orchestra, but it would take them some time to travel from the capital to the Sanctuary, so it could be done during that time.

For some reason, a few days after returning to the Sanctuary, Lord Simon sent a list.

「What’s this about? We just finished interviews a few days ago.」

「Let’s take a look inside first.」

「Y-yeah, you’re right.」

As Akane suggested, I took out the pile of documents containing the list from the box and scanned them.

「…let’s see, they want to hold another round of interviews.」

「Let’s see, …hmmm, there’s a lot of men this time.」

「Now that you mention it, there are.」

「Most are third sons or below. For matchmaking?」

「Matchmaking? What do you mean?」

「Well, the number of young women in the Sanctuary is increasing by a lot with the most recent interviews, right?」

「Yeah, it is.」

For some reason, majority of the people accepted during the interviews were young women. Thanks to that, the number of women increased significantly.

「Moreover, they’re all young women with an education and good upbringing.」

「Yeah, that’s true.」

「The clincher is that they’ve been authorized by the Great Spirits. For the third sons and lower who wouldn’t be succeeding their houses, this may be a chance to gain employment and a wife.」

「Ohh! So it’s killing two birds with one stone.」

I realized it when Akane mentioned it.

It’s not only this time, even my aides and those working in the government office, they had all been guaranteed a certain degree of character by the Great Spirits to some extent.

This time, we ended up with a lot of skilled women coming to the Sanctuary, but they were also excellent candidates.

「Then, I suppose I can’t refuse…」

「The people immigrating here have different objectives though.」

「What? The objectives of these guys?」

「No, I’m talking about these ones. But it’s fine if the men increase too, no? They probably won’t all be excellent individuals, but if they pass Sylph and the other’s selection process, then it’s fine even if they’re NEETs.」

「I’m not sure about NEETs, but they don’t need to be outstanding.」

The school and government office need skilled individuals, but there are other simpler jobs in the Sanctuary.

Then Akane suggested that we accept them so long as they weren’t inclined to commit crime.

「Well, it might be a problem if they cause trouble for other Sanctuary citizens, but in such cases, we could just exile them. NEETs rely on their parents, but it’s fine to accept them. Sylph and the others wouldn’t give their okay if those people are complete nuisances.」

「I’d prefer it if we can avoid NEETs, but some diversity could be necessary. Okay. I’ll contact Lord Simon about scheduling the interview.」

It would be problematic if only the number of young noblewomen increased once they start searching for future spouses, so it would be a good idea to balance it out by increasing the number of noblemen.

+++

# **657 - Harassment? No, A Spy?**

Because we did another round of interviews for the third sons onwards of nobles who were unable to participate in the women’s interviews, we ended up accepting around twenty men and several women that Sylph and the Great Spirits approved of.

And with that, the number of human men increased in the Sanctuary too. Until now, it’s only been a few cases such as with Vanga-san and some married couples who relocated to the Sanctuary.

And the first group of immigrants already arrived, but sure enough, or I suppose unsurprisingly, there were those who tried to sneak into the Sanctuary.

Apparently, the teachers and staff approved for immigration were unaware of it.

Some had even tried to rig the carriage in order to sneak in, but they were thrown out of the Sanctuary the moment they tried to pass through the gate.

「So, how many spies were there in the end?」

「Hmmm~ I dunno. I didn’t count them one by one.」

「There were that many?」

When I heard about it, I tried asking Sylph how many tried to sneak into the Sanctuary, but didn’t care to count.

「That mole? Spy? Do you know what happened to them?」

「Most of them had withdrawn to Wedgefort. A few of them returned to the Royal Capital.」

「Well, I guess they have to report their failure to infiltrate.」

Still, how foolish they were. There have been others who tried to infiltrate the Sanctuary using such methods before, which was why there hadn’t been any attempts recently.

「The immigrants this time are sons and daughters of nobles, so there are plenty of carriages to carry their luggage. Maybe they thought they could sneak in that way?」

「Exactly that. Why do women need that much luggage, I wonder. We ended up having to make their residence larger.」

We prepared spacious accommodation for them. It’s cheap, but they will be charged rent, of course.

「For a short exception, their parents were allowed into the annexed district. Of course, we didn’t let anyone harmful in, but for now, it’s fine.」

「…their parents have to accompany them this far?」

「It can’t be helped. There aren’t a lot of high nobility, but they are all pampered ladies raised by protective households.」

「Makes sense.」

Now that I think about it, if my daughters were to grow up and live in another city, I would also go with them.

「They’re from noble families. There are some cases where the boys were followed by their mothers out of concern.」

「Yeah, nope.」

So it seems there’s mama’s boys even in this world.

「Still, I wonder what they were planning to do after infiltrating the Sanctuary. I can’t think of anything meaningful though.」

「They’re likely after the materials of the Spirit Tree.」

「Ah, Sophia. Is Etoile sleeping?」

「Yes. She’s taking her afternoon nap.」

I couldn’t tell what those people who tried sneaking into the Sanctuary using rigged carriages were trying to do here. The one who answered me when I voiced that out was Sophia.

「So they’re after the materials of the Spirit Tree? Small amounts are being sold to Valkyra Kingdom and Lomaria Kingdom, aren’t they?」

「Man’s greed knows no bounds, Takumi.」

It was then that Undine and Selene appeared.

「What’s up, why are you guys together?」

「We were inspecting the cargo that entered the Annexed District by carriage.」

「The cargo?」

For Undine and Selene to inspect the cargo themselves, it must be a serious matter.

「I know the immigrating children aren’t the issue, but there are good-for-nothing people everywhere.」

「Did something happen, Selene?」

「There were several cursed items.」

「!? Cursed items!?」

「We’ve lifted the curse, you need not worry.」

My voice raised when I heard about the cursed items from Selene, but I was relieved to hear that she had dispelled the curse.

「But who brought such a thing…」

「Takumi-sama, there’s no point thinking about it. There are far too many like them.」

「That’s right. There are many different factions, such as the opposing factions between the immigrating children, so you don’t have to deal with each one.」

「…you have a point. If there’s no real harm in it then we can leave it as is?」

Neither people nor items that could harm us could be brought in, so I’ll just ignore it like they said.

It seems competition between nobles was common, and there were plenty of nobles who were jealous of the chosen individuals allowed entry to the Sanctuary because they themselves would never be able to.

In this way, I, too, must have been resented by the Noble Faction of Valkyra Kingdom. I suppose it wouldn’t be a mystery that they would take this chance to harass me.

The carriages filled with immigrating people will arrive one after the other, I wonder if they would need to help transporting their luggage

+++

# **658 - Like a Strange Butterfly**

All the teachers and staff of the school had arrived and entered their respective residences.

It also appeared as though the other students who came to study music with the orchestral bands had arrived.

As to be expected given how they were mostly nobles, the amount of luggage they had was immense. The residents of the Sanctuary also helped with the move.

During that, there was an eccentric man among the nobles that moved into the Sanctuary very quickly.

This time, it was mostly sons and daughters of barons and baronets who moved to the Sanctuary, but that man was the second son of an Earl family.

I thought he was someone who, by all rights, shouldn’t have come.

Normally, a second son had significance as insurance in case anything happened to the eldest son, and while it may sound wrong, he was a replacement child. Even if that hadn’t been the case, I’ve heard that second sons should have started a branch family.

I wonder if it was an oddball that moved to the Sanctuary. I did think that, but he really was a strange one.

It was when Sophia, Maria, Marnie, and I went on a walk with our children.

Etoile and the babies knew their grandmother Freesia-san, but for some reason, Madam Rosary and Madam Elizabeth were carrying them because they were taking a break at work.

It was at that time.

A blonde-haired blue-eyed man in his mid-twenties.

He wore frilly and flashy clothing that made it apparent that he was of noble birth.

The young man displayed his sparkly white teeth, knelt down in front of Sophia, and tried to take her hand to kiss it.

Unfortunately for him, Sophia left no gaps open, so the young man’s hand missed, grabbing only air.

「…mm, mmm, beautiful lady. I am Philip von Rosenmeyer. The second son of the Rosenmeyer Earldom. It must be fate that brought us together today. By all means, let us speak of our future together.」

「「「「「…」」」」」

Marnie, Maria, Madam Elizabeth, Madam Rosary, Freesia-san, and I were all at a loss for words at the young man’s abrupt actions.

「No, I am Takumi-sama’s spouse. I will not be whiling away with other men.」

「Ooh! My apologies. So you were this gentleman’s wife, I see. This Philip does not have a penchant for pursuing with another man’s wife.」

Sophia looked unfazed, quickly dealing with the young man named Philip.

Was there a Earl’s second son on the list?

I vaguely recall having met him during the interviews, but I don’t remember much else..

Philip-san stood up and apologized for his discourtesy, and in the next moment, his gaze was glued to Maria.

「Ohh! Miss red-haired Milady. Ahh! How could this be!? I must have been born to meet a lovely lady such as yourself!」

「I-I am also Takumi-sama’s wife!」

「Wha!? Oh my!」

Maria hid behind me as she spoke, then Philip-kun looked at me with wide eyes. Then his gaze moved past me and went towards Marnie.

As soon as he started eyeing her voraciously from the long rabbit ears on her head to the tip of her toes, he quickly moved in front of her and reached out to grab Marnie’s hands.

「Ahh! What magnificent style! You are overflowing with adult charm! I only have eyes for you now!」

「…I am also one of Takumi-sama’s wives. This body of mine is only for him.」

「Wha!? All three of these beautiful women are his wives…」

Philip looked at me with wide, surprsied eyes.

And as soon as I he came to me, he held both of my hands and shook them.

「Ahh! Are you a God?! May I call you Master?!」

「N-no, could you please stop?」

「Ooookay! I will try my best to amass a harem like Master!」

It didn’t seem like my words did not reach him.

Philip-san screamed “Uooo!” and began running.

「My my, that boy is the same as always.」

「He is a good boy, but a biiiit unusual.」

「Madam Rosary, Madam Elizabeth, do you know Philip-san?」

Madam Rosary and Madam Elizabeth who were carrying Haruka and Flora were seemed to know Philip-san..

「Yes, he is famous in the Royal Capital. The second son of the Earl Rosenmeyer is an excellent but disappointing young man.」

「I heard he was excellent in both academics and swordsmanship. …a shame, though.」

「I-is that so?」

Was he famous for being a disappointing? He seemed harmless, so maybe there’s no problem.

「Just as that boy said, he wouldn’t get involved with married women or someone’s lover, so I think it’s fine as long as you don’t listen to the rumors.」

「Indeed. If it weren’t for that one thing, he would have become popular.」

Freesia-san and the Madams were holding onto my daughters, but they must not have noticed that he tried to kiss my wives’ hands, so he really might actually have been a disappointment.

Still, he seemed like a guy that’s hard to dislike.

+++

# **659 - It Seems Quite The Unique Person Had Come**

A few days after meeting the unique young man known as Philip-san, I heard about the rumors circulating about him from Akane and Lulu-chan while we were playing with Flora in the living room.

「That Philip kid is amazing.」

「Regardless of their age, he would always talk to them nya.」

「Does anyone mind?」

「Lulu’s hand was almost kissed nya.」

「Of course, me too.」

「Sylph and the Great Spirits didn’t mind him, so we accepted him into the Sanctuary, but maybe I should have a talk with him.」

「He doesn’t seem to have any ill will, and he’s not too persistent, so I don’t think he’s that bad of a guy.」

「Just a bit disappointing nya.」

「「Disappointing, right?」」

Yes, he was, indeed, disappointing.

Philip had the typical foreigner look with his flowing blonde hair and blue eyes. If only he just shut his mouth, the women around him wouldn’t leave him be…

If only it weren’t for that behavior of his.

After dinner that day, I was relaxing at home and playing with Flora, Philip-san became the topic of conversation.

「That’s right. He kissed Laeva’s hand.」

「After that, he also took hold of my hand.」

While Charlotte was out shopping with Laeva, they had apparently encountered Philp-san.

「What’s amazing about that man is that he doesn’t discriminate between women.」

「Indeed. He kissed Martha-san’s hand and was beaten up by Vanga-san.」

「Uwaa, even Martha-san…」

Ever since Vanga-san and Martha-san started living in the Sanctuary, they’ve gotten considerably more youthful, but they were still well in their years to have a son already be an adult. From someone as young as Lulu-chan to even Martha-san, this man’s net is far too wide.

「It’s not just Martha-san, you know.」

It was then that Madam Elizabeth, Madam Rosary, Freesia-san, and Madam Lumia come in.

This is my house, but that was irrelevant to the women. They were truly such free-willed people.

「It wasn’t just Martha-san, meaning he talked to others as well?」

I’ve already given up on stopping them from coming to my house as they pleased, so we just continued the conversation.

「Evidently it is us, no?」

「Eh, Madam Elizabeth, Madam Rosary?」

「Lumia and I as well.」

「Ehh?! Mother-in-law and Madam Lumia too?!」

Since Philip spoke to Sophia, I knew it was possible that he would also approach Freesia-san and Madam Lumia. But Madam Elizabeth and Madam Rosary were significantly far in their years, though…

「My, is it truly that strange for me to be approached?」

「N-no, not at all. Madam Elizabeth, you’re still young, after all.」

「Oh dear, so are you saying that I am different?」

「N-no, Madam Rosary, you are also still young. Aha-, isn’t that obvious?」

Woah, that was dangerous. Talking about women’s age was taboo.

In reality, as humans, Madam Elizabeth and Madam Rosary looked younger than their actual age. Much like Vanga-san and Martha-san, this seemed to be strong shift after living in the Sanctuary.

As Elves, Freesia-san and Madam Lumia appeared youthful.

Still, while that may be the case for Madam Elizabeth and Madam Rosary, Madam Lumia was a different matter.

「What is Philip-san trying to do by talking up the Queen of Yggurle Kingdom?」

Aside from them, Phlip seemed to have flirted with Melty-san and her daughters, who were the mother and daughters who manage the orchard.

「I could understand it if it was only Melty.」

「Eh, there’s someone else besides Melty-san?」

Madam Lumia made a fed up gesture, stating that Philip-san made advances to others besides Melty-san. It made me wonder who she could be pertaining to.

「He even knelt down as he professed his love towards Melty’s daughter, Melanie.」

「…Philip-san…」

Perhaps I’m wrong to have been bit relieved that he hadn’t done so with Malorie-chan as well. But making advances towards Melanie-chan was already criminal enough.

「Hmm, perhaps we should tell him to focus only on adult women for now.」

「Indeed. We should make it known that married women are also off-limits.」

「Yeah, you’re right.」

「Fufu, it is no problem for widows such as Melty-san and myself. Well, Melty rejected him quite severely though.」

「I see~ understood. I will tell him to not stubbornly pursue people who aren’t interested.」

I respect Philip-san for his wide range of interests, but lolicons are unacceptable. When I said that I would give him a warning, Madam Rosary pointed out that it could pose issues to married women as well, and that I should tell him to avoid them as well.

Madam Elizabeth looked amused as she said laughingly said that widows were fine, though Melty-san flatly said no.

It’s only natural to ask someone who makes advances on minors to leave.

+++

# **660 - Is this on purpose?**

Thinking I should have a word with Philip-san, I went looking around for where he might be at.

That guy. Unlike the people who wanted to become teachers and staff at the school, or the students who want to study music here, he wanted to find work in the Sanctuary, but for now, hasn’t taken a single job.

Because of that, I had to search for him all over the place.

In the end, I found him without much trouble.

It looked like he was kneeling in front of a woman in the shopping district, whispering words of affection.

It was our maid, Sala.

Sala was already over 20 years old, so she was late to marry by this world’s standards, but according to Maribelle, she had promised marriage to a childhood friend, and he was supposed to come to Volton.

The childhood friend who would become her husband was planning to help manage and maintain the garden of our mansion in Volton.

At the moment, Sala was taking turns between working in our mansions in the Sanctuary and Volton, but Maribelle said that once she’s married, she would spend more time working at Volton.

Slap!

Ah, thought so.

Sala really hated that type, after all.

「What’s up, Sala?」

「Ah, Master, this man was being persistent in bothering me, I simply reacted. My apologies.」

「Ohh! Is that not Teacher?! Is this young lady also Teacher’s wife?!」

「No, Sala is our maid. Sala, you are free to go.」

「Well then, please excuse me, Master.」

Sala bowed to me and went into Papeck-san’s store. She must have some shopping she has to do.

「Phew, Philip-san.」

「Teacher, please just call me Philip!」

「Then, Philip. Sala has a partner she is to be wed to soon. I think you should stop approaching just anyone.」

「Ohh! That was wrong of me. When we meet again, I will apologize. Woah, Teacher, please excuse me. A beautiful flower beckons to me.」

「U-umm, wait, Philip.」

「Miss beautiful lady, would you care to have some tea and talk about our future togetherーー!?」

When Philip said that, she shrieked and ran away.

Yup. He never learns.

As I sighed and turned to go back home, I saw a trio of men approaching me from the other side.

Wondering if they had some business with me, I stopped walking as they were half running towards me and bowed deeply on their greeting.

「Well, well! If it isn’t Iruma-sama!」

「U-umm…」

「Ohh! How rude of me. This one is named Dan. Originally the third son of a baronial house, though this one had renounced this one’s family name, intending to offer my services for the good of the Sanctuary. As such, this one humbly ask for your favor!」

「T- this one? G-gozaru?」

The first one to introduce himself was a man with short, light brown hair and thick eyebrows calling himself Dan.

Rather than what he added to his introduction, I found his way of speaking to be incredibly curious.

As I stood there stunned, the second and third young men introduced themselves as well.

「It is an honor to meet you, Iruma-sama. I [Sesha – Samurai way of saying I] am your humble servant, Madd. Unworthy as I am, please treat me well.」

「Lastly is I, Bill. Though I was the fourth son of a baronet house, I will strive to become a Knight of the Sanctuary from the ground up, regardless of my family background. I humbly ask for your support.」

The second man to introduce himself was a largely built man with short blonde hair who called himself Madd. It was clear from his muscular build that he had undergone extensive training.

The third man who called himself Bill was a slender young man who had medium length brown hair tied back. He appeared thin, but it was evident that he was well-trained.

But more than anything, why were these three talking like they were samurai in some historical drama? These three were the first of this kind that I’ve seen since coming to this world, and I couldn’t help but bewildered.

Also, Bill-san said a word that caught my attention so I tried asking him about it.

「A-, yeah, nice to meet you. So Bill-san, what is a knight of the Sanctuary?」

「Please just call me Bill. A Knight of the Sanctuary is, quite literally, the spear and shield of Lord Iruma who safeguards the Sanctuary.」

「They protect the Spirit Tree, become the hands and legs of the Great Spirits, and ensure the safety of the Sanctuary citizens. Such are the roles of the Knights of the Sanctuary.」

「I-, I see…」

「Well then, as we must patrol the Sanctuary, we will take our leave.」

「「「Farewell!」」」

「…」

I could only gawk at the three men as they bowed deeply to me and went on their way.

Wait, I think we’re gathering way too many unique people.

Were they like this during the interview? No, they seemed normal, but were Sylph and the others just amused by them?

I should press them about this.

+++

# **661 - A Group of Eccentrics? No, It’s the Order of Knights.**

When I returned to the mansion, Sylph, Undine, and my family were having some tea.

「Oh perfect. Sylph, Undine, do you remember Dan-san, Madd-san, and Bill-san?」

「Pff, so you’ve met them.」

「If you’re reacting that way, then you know.」

「Of course, that was the purpose of the interviews, was it not? They’re quite eccentric, but upright children.」

「Indeed. That Philip kid wasn’t bad either, right?」

It seemed Sylph and Undine had a good grasp on things.

「They didn’t leave that much of an impression on me then though.」

「Of course not. When they’re in front all of us, they’re frozen solid from nerves.」

「Pff, and that’s what made their way of speaking quite proper.」

「Wha!? Is that so?」

According to Undine, those there behaved properly during the interviews because of how nervous they were. I thought it was odd to say that they behaved “properly” in that sense, but I suppose it couldn’t be helped that I hadn’t noticed.

And surprisingly, the slightly impassioned samurai trio were deemed acceptable.

「Takumi-sama, a knight order for the Sanctuary… wouldn’t that be wonderful?」

「Eh, Sophia, what’s up?」

For some reason, Sophia’s eyes were sparkling.

Oh yeah, Sophia was once part of the Chivalric Order of Yggurle Kingdom.

「Takumi-sama, please, by all means, permit the establishment of the Sanctuary Knight Order.」

「Uhh, Sophia, the Sanctuary is safe because there’s a barrier, you know? Would we even need a knight order? 」

「No, but it could happen that we would need to send reinforcements in case something were to happen to Valor and Wedgefort. Even with a barrier, there will be those who would attack. The citizens of the Sanctuary would feel safer if they knew there was not only golems, but also a knight order was present, wouldn’t they?」

Sophia was unusually talkative.

What she said also had sound logic.

Let’s consider the Sanctuary’s war potential.

Aside from the golems that were used during the war with Triaria Kingdom and the Divine Empire of Sydnia, our party was definitely our strongest force.

As for who would be next, I had to think about that.

Certainly, the five mermaids including Fluna were well-trained and well-equipped, but their main priority was ensuring the safety of the mermaids fishing.

Similarly, Wappa and the kid group had also been power leveled, but it would be wrong to count them as a fighting force.

Doganbo-san, Golan-san, the Dwarves, and the Evles also had some fighting potential, but, if say a war were to happen, I wouldn’t want to draft them as fighters.

「…you’re right, it’s just as you said. Maybe it’s okay to have one.」

「Thank you very much!」

「Y-yeah, calm down, Sophia.」

Sophia hugged me in delight.

It made me happy, but it was embarrassing to be watched like this by Sylph and Undine.

「Surely Father would be happy about this as well.」

「Dante-san would?」

「Yes. Father was originally member of the Chivalric Order. After receiving our territory, he seemed to have experienced a lot of hardships with agriculture.」

「I see. Maybe it would be a good idea to entrust it to him then.」

「Takumi-sama, let me be of service too!」

「Okay, okay. Please help too, Sophia.」

If Sophia wanted to do it, then I’ll leave it to her.

It may be a good for her to not only take care of Etoile, but also have a job that she likes.

「That’s perfect. There’s always some children that are too much for the school teachers and staff to handle.」

「No, you guys did the interviews.」

「My, we did not select the teachers and staff of the School. We simply screened if they had the qualifications to live in the Sanctuary.」

「She’s right, Takumi. Actually, some of them are even music students studying with the orchestral band this time. Aside from there, there are still some kids who are still figuring out what kind of work they want to do, no?」

「Does that include Dan-san and the others too?」

「It makes no difference, but you should stop adding -san. Takumi, you are the highest person in the Sanctuary. You musn’t lower yourself too much to people who have just immigrated. Moreover, those children are younger than you.」

「But they’re nobles. Philip-san is from an Earldom too, isn’t he?」

Sylph said that I should stop addressing people with “-san”. So I’m at the top of the Sanctuary, huh… she’s not wrong, but…

「Even if they’re an earl or a prince, they should understand that, here in the Sanctuary, you are practically the king, yes?」

「Understood. Dan-kun is fine, right? …but to think they’re younger than me.」

When the fact that they were actually younger shocked me, Sophia stood up and started moving immediately.

「Takumi-sama, I will post a sign to recruit members for the Sanctuary Knights.」

「Ah, yeah, I suppose you could put it up at the plaza in the Central District.」

「Yes, I’ll visit Laeva to ask her to build a notice board.」

Saying so, Sophia left for the workshop where Laeva was.

「Perfect timing. We would likely have no need for a Knight Order within the Sanctuary, but I believe it is essential to prepare for threats from the outside.」

「That’s true. I don’t want to think about it, but there’s always a possibility that something could happen that we can’t handle alone.」

When Triaria Kingdom and the Divine Empire of Sydnia invaded the Savage Lands, their goal had definitely been the Sanctuary. In which case, it wouldn’t be wrong to prepare for such a situation in case it were to happen again.

But, for the time being, I suppose it would just be those three…

+++

# **662 - Color Coding Seems To Be The Way**

Three pairs of sparkling eyes were staring, though they were the eyes of samurai-speaking trio.

Standing in front of them were Sophia and Dante-san wearing training clothes.

「…so only three of them had assembled, huh.」

「Father, it can’t be helped. The citizens who’ve been living in the Sanctuary have work to do.」

「Even if it is as you say, Sophia, three is far too little.」

「Father, more will join from here onwards.」

In contrast to Dan, Madd, and Bill whose eyes were sparkling, Dante-san who was excited to come to the assembly place after learning of the new knight order was dejected that only three people had shown up.

「Dante-dono! Though there may be only three of us, we shall always be the shield of the Sanctuary!」

「Indeed, we will! Inexperienced though we may be, our determination shan’t be bested by any other!」

「Please, we humbly ask for your guidance!」

「Ah, yeah…」

As expected, even Dante-san gave in to the pressure from the three.

Sophia was also brimming with motivation.

That was nice and all, but someone who was normally not in a place like this with a raised flag.

「Hey, I thought I should ask. What are you doing here, Salamander?」

「We’re founding the Sanctuary Knight Order, right? Then shouldn’t it have name colored names like Red Dragon, Black Dragon, and White Dragon?」

「Well, there are some countries that go by that naming sense. Others go by First, Second, etc.」

「Right? That’s why I brought the flag for the Fire Spirit Knights.」

「No, there’s a few things I’d like to comment on, but…」

Since it came about yesterday, it was inevitable that Salamander would have already have known about the knight order by today. After all, he was a Great Spirit. Still, for him to have even gotten Kaede to prepare a flag…

And so, when I looked at the flag Salamander was holding, it had the picture of a salamander on top of the Spirit Tree.

「Nice flag you have there, but are you really planning to split up the knight order when there’s only three members?」

「Yeah, right now, Sylph and Undine are placing an order for flags with Kaede.」

「Uhh, I could kinda see that from Sylph, but even Undine is?」

「Hm? Undine said that she already had those mermaids.」

「…so those five had already been dragged into this.」

Fluna and the others seem to have gotten caught by Undine. Hopefully it doesn’t interfere with their workk.

「Hey! You’re slowing down!」

「Don’t flap around when running!」

While I was chatting with Salamander, Undine and Dante-san had already begun training the samurai trio.

Right now, they seem to be running as part of their warm up.

「Then I will discuss the Fire Spirit Knights armor with Laeva.」

「Hold on, don’t ask Laeva for unreasonable things.」

「I know.」

After Salamander waved me off as he disappeared, I moved my gaze over to Sophia and theo thers.

Before I knew it, the number of people increased to six.

「Eh? They’re increasing?」

「Fufu, it’ll grow even more, you know?」

「Uwah! Don’t scare me like that, Sylph.」

I was surprised when Sylph suddenly appeared without a trace and talked to me.

Sylph enjoyed making her presence disappear to play tricks like this on me. She’s a Wind Spirit and is completely free-spirited, so I’ve just resigned myself to it.

「Sylph, are you doing the same as Salamander?」

「Yep, the Wind Spirit Knights.」

「Even if you split them half and half with Salamander, I don’t think three people would count as a knight squad.」

「Oh, my squad is only for the Elves.」

「Eh!? Only for the Elves?」

The number of recruits running with Sophia and Dante-san doubled to six before I knew it, but when I told Sylph that she would have to split them to 3-man squads with Salamander, she said that her knights would be limited to the Elves.

There was definitely a lot more Elves than Humans in the Sanctuary, but everyone had jobs, so I thought there weren’t any that could join the knights.

「I thought it was impossible because everyone was busy with work.」

「I know that much. That’s why I chose some promising children from Yggurle Kingdom and called them in.」

「Wha?! You’re inviting from Yggurle Kingdom!?」

「That’s right. So there’s no problem.」

I think that’s a LOT of problems. I’ll have to inform Madam Lumia and Mimir.

Still, the Sanctuary Knights seemed like a completely impulsive, poor idea.

I later heard that even Gnome started inviting individuals from Gnomstoll Kingdom.

There’s quite the distance from Gnomstoll Kingdom to the Sanctuary so it would take some them some time though.

Salamander, Sylph, Gnome, and Undine declared that they were founding their respective knight squads. A knight squad isn’t defined by its numbers though.

However, I would later come to realize that I had severely underestimated the influence of the Great Spirits.

+++

# **663 - Youths Gathering From All Around The Continent**

There was a time when I thought their antics had gone too far.

Thinking it was just a prolonged version of their usual games, I thought they would soon get bored and forget it.

Sylph and Salamander were excited to gather young talents to come to the Sanctuary to form the knight order, but I thought they wouldn’t be able to amass the numbers.

As for Fluna’s mermaid squad for Undine, they only had five members, so I thought their numbers would scale up to ten, but…

Sylph was talking excitedly with Salamander and Gnome.

「The Wind Spirit Knights will take this spot.」

「In that case, the Fire Spirit Knights will go here.」

「The Earth Spirit Knights will place its headquarters here.」

The three Great Spirits had spread out a map of the Sanctuary and were deciding on the locations of their respective headquarters.

「Taking the future into account, I’d like the building to be able to accommodate a hundred people.」

「Yeah. I have three people right now, but I expect promising individuals from all over the continent to come.」

「Same goes for me. Some dwarves aren’t suited to be blacksmiths. Among them, the young ones wishing to assist with the protection of the Sanctuary are making their way here.」

「…」

How did this come about? According to Sylph, at least twenty young elves were immigrating from Yggurle Kingdom.

Madam Lumia and Mimir-sama had no objections to Sylphs desires. Rather, they even said that Yggurle Kingdom wished to offer assistance. Of course, I politely declined.

And apparently, Salamander wasn’t recruiting youths from just Valkyra Kingdom, but also Lomaria Kingdom and Samandour Kingdom.

Even so, he’s said that it was a little over twenty people.

「There’s really not quite a lot of people capable of becoming part of the Sanctuary Knights. The Sanctuary isn’t a place that accepts everyone, after all.」

「I see.」

Incidentally, the headquarters of Undine’s Water Spirit Knights would be close to the sea. Well, actually, it’s more like it’s already been decided that I would be building it.

「Sophia and Dante really into the idea. Isn’t it about time you give in.」

「No, it’s not about giving in. I do think it’s necessary to have a means to defend ourselves. Whether a knight order is necessary or not is a different matter, but I respect everyone’s opinions on it.」

Still, I understand how Sylph was recruiting elves from Yggurle Kingdom, but how about the other countries? Valkyra Kingdom was one thing, but there’s also Lomaria Kingdom, Samandour Kingdom, and even Gnome’s choice of Gnomstoll Kingdom which is on the other end of the continent.

「Things like that… if an Earth Spirit finds a promising youth, obviously I would go there out scout them myself.」

「Ah, me too. Fire Spirits aren’t as spread out as Earth Spirits and Wind Spirits, but they’re able to find promising individuals too.」

「Haha, there’s no way they could refuse if a Great Spirit is scouting them.」

The Great Spirits sure were quick on their feet.

---

Somewhere in Samandour Kingdom, there was a young man holding a hoe, eagerly plowing the ground.

He was about to come of age next year.

The Samandour Kingdom, located in the southern region of the continent, had a warm climate, and the young man’s forehead was soaked in sweat from the farm work he had been doing.

This young man, or rather teenage boy to be more precise, was born as the third son to a farmer family.

His two older brothers would inherit the family’s fields, but the third son had none to take.

That’s why, once he reached adulthood, his only options were to work elsewhere or work under his brothers by tending to their land.

But if he were to farm for his brothers, he frankly wouldn’t be able to marry. And so, the only option the young man was really left with was to go elsewhere.

Many young people who became adventurers came from similar backgrounds, so the boy wasn’t particularly unfortunate.

He made his decision to leave when he was around ten years old, slowly making preparations once he realized that his place wasn’t at home.

That said, there wasn’t much that a ten year old third son of a farmer could do. He swung his sword as much as he could, and training his body as hard as possible.

And on that day, a turning point came to the boy.

Although he was a boy of a typical circumstance, he had a diligent and honest personality.

He didn’t possess any talent in combat, commerce, or academia, yet his sole trait as a sincere person, combined with the whim of a Great Spirit, had changed the boy’s fate.

「Ou! You there, boy.」

「Eh?」

A voice suddenly came from behind him. He stopped plowing the field and turned around, only to see a lad with red hair and red skin standing there.

However, even as a mere third son to a farming family, he inevitably realized that the lad in front of him was no ordinary being.

「Y- you’re a…」

「Ou, my name is Salamander. Well, I’m basically the Great Fire Spirit.」

「S-salamander-sama」

Startled by the sudden appearance of a Great Spirit, he dropped his hoe and prostrated himself before the great being.

Even if one wasn’t an elf or a dwarf, Spirits were still worshipped. This also applied to humans.

「You have quite a pretty color of your soul. Why not join my knight order in the sanctuary?」

「Salamander-sama’s knight order?」

「Yeah, I’m thinking of making the Fire Spirit Knights. I’ve come to scout for that for that order.」

「But I’m the third son of a farmer. A knight order is beyond my station.」

「Being a farmer’s third son or even a noble, it doesn’t matter. The knight order I’m making would be made up of people I deem acceptable. So, how about it? You want to go the Sanctuary?」

The boy may have been thrown off by the sudden proposition, but since he had already decided to leave home once he came of age anyway, so he accepted the invitation from the spirit he revered.

「V-very well. Please treat me well.」

「Ou, I’ll give you some money to cover your expenses. Be careful on your way to the Sanctuary.」

Saying so, Salamander handed the money over to the boy for his preparations and travel cost to the Sanctuary, then vanished without a trace.

It goes without saying that Takumi was later on extorted for money by the Great Spirits without any explanation for what it was to be used for.

+++

# **664 - Lining up at the Outskirts**

I see now that my prediction was too optimistic.

I ended up having to build the headquarters of three knight orders In the outskirts of the Central District of the Sanctuary.

These buildings would serve as both the headquarters, as well as the lodging for the knights, but it was a set of an administrative building, a male dormitory, and female dormitory. And I made three identical sets there, and one by the seaside totaling four sets.

I had to build a large shared training facility, along with indoor training grounds as well as outdoor training grounds.

It’s not that I was making light of Salamander or Gnome.

But I’ve only ever seen those two drinking or lazing around in the Sanctuary. I didn’t expect them to scout people themselves.

Because of that, I heard that, aside from Undine’s which mainly consisted of the Mermaids living in the Sanctuary, there were around thirty members gathered for Sylph’s, Salamander’s, and Gnome’s knight orders.

Thanks to that, I suddenly had to prepare buildings for the knights.

It would have been a piece of cake had it only been a matter of constructing the buildings, but they left everything, from interior design to furniture placements, and installation of magic devices, to me.

Well, I did like creating things, and it WAS my job, so I guess it’s fine.

Just as I had more or less finished constructing the buildings, I asked Sylph and Salamander a question that suddenly came to mind.

「Hey, don’t knights ride horses?」

「「…I forgot.」」

As I thought, they really didn’t think things through.

Returning to the mansion, we decided to talk to Sophia, who was overseeing the training of the samurai trio.

Even though they’re knights, it might not necessarily mean that they would be a cavalry, after all.

「Ah! …」

When I asked Sophia about the horse issue, she made a “woops” kind of face.

Yup, she forgot.

「So you were under the assumption it would be horse riders, didn’t you?」

「…Yes. Since they would be expected to patrol around the Sanctuary, I thought the cavalry would be essential.」

As I thought, Sophia had presumed that the knights would be on horseback. I suppose that’s normal.

However, Gnome said that his own order didn’t need it.

「Hmm, my knights won’t need horses. 」

「Eh, you don’t need it, Gnome?」

「Yeah, dwarven bodies are ill-suited for horses.」

「I see, I guess that’s true.」

「My knights order won’t need horses either. Our scope of activity will mainly be at sea. But we might want to tame some sea monsters.」

「That’s true, Undine’s wouldn’t need it either. Though I do think getting some riding practice wouldn’t hurt though.」

「That’s true. In actuality, the Mermangers can fight on land too.」
