Actually, in terms of strength, Fluna and the Mermangers are ahead, not just slightly, but overwhelmingly so. So it would be a waste to not have them practice horseback riding.

「Ah- oh yeah. Takumi, hand me the map of the Savage Lands.」

「Hm? A map? Give me a sec.」

As if remembering something, Sylph asked to me to take out the map of the Savage Lands.

The map wasn’t perfect, but we were able to make a somewhat accurate map with everyone’s help.

I took out a reserve copy of the map from my Item Box and laid it out on the table, then Sylph pointed towards a spot.

「Yeah, yeah, here, I think there are several herds of Battle Horses roaming the grasslands here and in the hilly areas.」

「Battle Horses, you say. Aren’t those monsters a rank higher than Demon Horses?」

Maybe she heard it from her familial spirits, or saw them herself, but Sylph said that herds of Battle Horses were there.

However, a Battle Horse was different from a Demon Horse, as it was a monster that was a bit more challenging to tame. Demon Horses were used to pull carriages even in Valkyra Kingdom, but there’s practically no one using Battle Horses.

「What are you saying? Takumi, didn’t you tame Tsubaki?」

「If you say that, I can’t refute it.」

Sure enough, it wouldn’t be an exaggeration to say that Tsubaki, after having evolved several times, was now basically like a dragon. Having been able to tame a creature like that just to pull carriages and be a saddle horse, the Battle Horse was just cute in comparison.

「Okay, fine. I am also interested in that Battle Horse, and if I have Kaede and Tsubaki with me, I’d have no problem herding them back.」

「We’ll leave it to you then.」

「Then I’ll build a stable for the Battle Horse near the headquarters for the Dwarves.」

「Gotcha, I’ll leave you guys to prepare for their arrival.」

「Selene and Dryas will help me out, so it’ll be fine.」

After we finished our discussion, I took Kaede and Tsubaki to the Savage Lands.

Gnome left to build the stable.

I wonder what kind of monster the Battle Horse is. I’m a bit excited.

+++

# **665 - Securing Horses**

I rode in tandem with Kaede on Tsubaki to the place that Sylph pointed on the map of the Savage Lands.

Kaede was in a really cheery mood behind me.

「I’m so excited to be out with Master!」

Kaede was over the moon the instant I said that she, Tsubaki, and I were going out.

Come to think of it, I haven’t been spending much time with her recently. That made me feel a tad guilty.

The location indicated on the map had a river running through the grasslands, with some small forests and gently-sloping hills.

「I see, it’s not only monsters, plenty of animals inhabit this area.」

「I can feel several presences, Master.」

『I can sense several presence nearby, Master.』

「Then as we planned, Kaede will capture them with her silk, and we’ll tame them if possible. Tsubaki’s here too, so we should manage somehow.」

「Kaaay!」

『Understood.』

In our party, Kaede and I, who excelled at searching for enemies, did our best to identify all Battle Horse presences.

We found the Battle Horses before long.

I’m not sure if a herd of five was small or big, but we need quite a lot of them, so I’ll try to tame them immediately.

The Battle Horse’s physique didn’t seem to be that different from a Demon Horse.

They were larger than normal horses, with thicker limbs. Despite that, they run faster than a Demon Horse, have plenty of stamina, and were tough.

As the name “Battle Horse” implied, they had wild and aggressive temperaments. Despite being a horse, they were also omnivores who ate the meat of small animals such as Horned Rabbits that they themselves hunted.

Their horse bodies commonly have a black base, with some identifying white marks on their forehead, or white tipped legs.

Their manes were long and neat.

Tsubaki accelerated and quickly approached.

The Battle Horses that noticed us tried to escape, but they couldn’t win against Tsubaki’s speed, and Kaede quickly caught them with her threads.

When we jumped off of Tsubaki, the horse that seemed to be the herd leader roared and snorted menacingly as it struggled unsuccessfully against Kaede’s threads.

It was when Tsubaki made a low and rumbly intimidating neigh that the Battle Horses stopped trying to break free from their bindings and fell silent.

「Thanks, Tsubaki.」

Tsubaki and Kaede were putting pressure on the Battle Horses.

Perhaps realizing that they couldn’t beat me, or that running away is useless, taming them went as smoothly as it could be.

「Okay, Kaede, you can undo your silk.」

「Roger!」

After Kaede released them, the Battle Horses slowly stood up and just waited for my instructions.

「Gather around me, we’re teleporting.」

**Bururu**

The Battle Horses surrounded me.

Kaede and I got on Tsubaki’s back, and I opened a gate to teleport us back to the Sanctuary. The Battle Horses followed after.

「Welcome back! As expected, I was right that they were there, wasn’t I?」

「Takumi-sama, these are amazing horses. I will take responsibility over these ones.」

「Ah, yeah, thanks.」

When we passed through the Gate, we were met by an overly excited Sylph and Sophia who was happy to see the Battle Horses, and led to the completed stable.

「Hey, Sophia. One of those is for me, right?」

「What are you saying, Father? One will not be allocated to you, as you are not even a member.」

「What are YOU saying? I AM a member of the Knight Order.」

Dante-san wanted a Battle Horse for himself, but was immediately shot down by Sophia.

「…are horses really that important to knights?」

「Who knows, I’m a Spirit. I haven’t a clue.」

「Suppose so. I wouldn’t either.」

After that, I went around the other places that Sylph pointed out on the map and caught more Battle Horses.

Eventually, I was able to capture forty Battle Horses, but Sophia and Dante-san said that it still wasn’t enough.

「Takumi-sama, if it is possible, please secure the same number of horses again.」

「…I can’t do that right away. Sylph and her familial spirits are still searching, so I will do it after that.」

I don’t know how many members the knight order will have, so increasing the amount of Battle Horses may turn out to be unnecessary, but Sophia and Dante-san thought otherwise.

With the help of the knight candidates and the children of the Sanctuary, Dante-san and Sophia happily took care of the Battle Horses.

If it’s to keep seeing Sophia look so happy, I should do my best and search for more.

+++

# **666 - Sea Beast Riders**

Once we secured enough Battle Horses to stop for now, Fluna came by as if waiting for that moment.

「Eh? Want to be a Beast Rider? You, Fluna?」

「Yes!」

「But you guys swim fast enough by yourselves, don’t you?」

「Is it not okay?」

With pleading, upturned eyes, I lost my chance to say no.

「…Sigh, if you say it like that, you have a monster you have your sites on, don’t you?」

「Yes!」

Knowing that I was giving the okay, Fluna grew spirited and answered eagerly.

Huh? Did Fluna just play me?

「So, what kind of monster is it?」

「Yes. It’s a cute little one that swims fast!」

「C-cute?」

「Yes!」

When I heard the details from Fluna, she said that when they were living in the coasts of Samandour Kingdom before they were sheltered in the Sanctuary, it didn’t attack the Mermaids and was rather on good terms with them even though it wasn’t a familiar.

「When we cured the monster child’s injuries, we became friends with monster parents.」

「Woah, so there’s monsters like that.」

「Yes! They’re awfully clever.」

The monster that Fluna and the others formed a relationship was likely a rare case.

Fundamentally, untamed monsters attack people indiscriminately.

But it is a fact that, on rare occasions, highly intelligent monsters and humans help each other out and become friends.

「Could it be, you want to go all the way to the coastal waters of Samandour Kingdom to meet it?」

「…is that a no?」

I assumed she was talking about the seas of the Sanctuary, but Fluna and the others wanted to look for them in the areas they lived in before.

Going by ship, it would still take several days on the Oceanius, but we can teleport there in an instant, so distance was a not an issue. I’ve already gone there once when we rescued Fluna and the mermaids.

「It’s only you going then, Fluna?」

「No, the five of us will come.」

「Ahh, so all members of the Mermangers.」

I wasn’t that much help in the water, so the full Mermanger squad coming was a wise choice.

In the end, I teleported to Samandour Kingdom with a fully-equipped Fluna, Lana, Mina, Shana, and Wistina.

It was the sea where Fluna and the Mermaids were exposed to threats of monsters and been in hiding.

Watching them from the beach, I saw the Mermangers go berserk against the sea monsters, perhaps taking all the frustration that had built up in their time here.

At first it was the large shark-like monsters that approached the mermaids like they were bait.

To the monster, the Mermaids were probably a delicious treat.

The mermaids disappeared from this area. As it’s been a while since the last time it feasted on one, the monster didn’t hesitate to attack when he saw a group of five mermaids.

Dobaaaannnn!!

「Insolent fish!」

A single strike… with a single strike from Fluna’s trident, she brought down the 8 meter long shark-like monster.

The blood of the slain shark flowed into the sea, and its scent attracted other monsters.

Fluna and the others were lying in wait with huge smiles on their faces.

After that, the rampage began.

Venting all of the frustration from the time they lived here trembling in fear, the five went absolutely wild.

I took some wood out from my Item Box and fashioned myself a boat and went around collecting the monsters they defeated.

Eventually, a large one appeared.

What made a large splash as it emerged from the water was Sea Serpent.

Seeing this, Fluna gave everyone orders.

「Kill it in a swift attack! Disperse!」

「「「「Understood!」」」」

The Mermangers dispersed to avoid the incoming opened jaws of the Sea Serpent, then instantly pivoted and attacked simultaneously with their tridents.

The coordinated, omnidirectional attack aimed at the neck had cut the Sea Serpent’s large head.

「Sea Serpents are no problem anymore, huh.」

The Sea Serpent, which had been their graduation test before, was now no different from a small fish to them.

Once I retrieved the Sea Serpent, I felt several presences approaching at high speeds.

「Ah, it’s come!」

Fluna yelled happily as I was being cautious.

Emerging from the depths was a slim plesiosaur-like monster with four small antlers horns.

「Have you been well!?」

「Uwaa, the little one has grown up!」

Fluna and the others were happy to be reunited with the plesiosaur.

I could tell that the plesiosaur was just as happy to see them again. It seems highly intelligent.

The name of the plesiosaur-like monster was Sea Dragon.

Smaller than a Sea Serpent, an adult Sea Dragon reaches only 8 meters overall, but in terms of monster ranks, it rose to that of a Sea Dragon.

Am I the only one who think it looks more charming than the face of a Sea Serpent?

The four antler tips were apparently its children.

Before I could even speak, the Sea Dragon family was safely tamed to Fluna and the Mermangers, and we teleported back to the Sanctuary.

+++

# **667 - Sophia becomes a Sergeant (Volume 12 END)**

Once we were done taming marine creatures at Fluna and the other’s request, we returned to the Sanctuary’s coast and left the rest to them, then headed to the three knight headquarters in the outskirts of the Central District.

In the spacious training grounds built on the outskirts, young men and women running in sync in a neat formation.

Overseeing them were Sophia and Dante-san.

Perhaps on a little field trip, Maria and Marnie had brought their daughters to watch. Freesia-san was also beside them, carrying Etoile.

「They’ve really grown in numbers.」

「Ah, Takumi-sama, you’ve returned.」

「Welcome home.」

「Wekom om.」

Watching them run in an orderly fashion, I made a comment about how I hadn’t realize their numbers had increased. Hearing this, Maria and Marnie turned around, and surprisingly, Flora imitated Marnie’s greeting.

That made me so happy I forgot what i was going to ask about.

I took turns holding and doting with Flora, Etoile, and Haruka.

When I was handing Flora to Marnie, Marnie asked if we were able to tame the sea creatures.

「So, were you able to grant Fluna-san and the other’s wish?」

「…here she is. About that. Yeah, we were able to tame them safely. I just watched though.」

「I see, what monster is it?」

「It’s apparently a type of Sea Dragon, similar to a Sea Serpent but with four fins, I guess? The Familiar Contract went without a hitch too, it seemed highly intelligent.」

「Is that so? I’ll have Fluna show it to me next time.」

Maria showed interest in the tamed monster.

I’m not sure if that could thing could be called a beast ride though.

「Are you out on a walk?」

「Yes. Flora has a lot of energy, after all.」

「Ai!」

「Haha, is that so? Did you play a lot?」

Flora tried very hard to speak, but of course, I still couldn’t understand her.

I once again turned my gaze towards the trainees running.

「…what a sergeant.」

「Sergeant?」

「No, it’s nothing. Just me mumbling.」

Seeing them run in orderly lines, I remembered scenes of military academy training in movies I’ve seen ages ago.

「They’re even singing while running…」

More so, Sophia was calling them “maggots”. Who did she get this from?

Leading the group were Dan, Madd, and Bill, the first three who wanted to become knights, and I noticed that behind them were individuals not of the noble class of Valkyra King, which included Elves, Humans, and Beastkin.

「Did the Elves increase considerably?」

「That’s right, Takumi-kun. As Sylph-sama wished for it, Lumia-sama and Mimir-sama actively promoted it.」

「…is it perhaps still increasing?」

「Yggurle Kingdom doesn’t have many places for young people to work as well.」

According to Freesia-san, Yggurle Kingdom had too many young elves looking for work.

Elves were naturally reclusive and don’t normally travel to other countries, so they had no choice but to search for work domestically. Moreover, Elves were long-living, so higher positions were limited and rarely had vacancies.

As a result, there were many Elves that were young NEETs.

「Then there’s the Sanctuary Knights. Sylph-sama, a Great Spirit, wished for it, and the workplace was on sacred land. You understand why the young, shut-in elves would jump at the opportunity, don’t you?」

「I understand, Yggurle Kingdom has a hard time too.」

I watched the running trainees again.

It was then that I noticed there weren’t any dwarves.

「Huh? There’s no dwarves.」

「Takumi-sama, Gnomstoll Kingdom is far from here.」

「And dwarves have short legs.」

「You have a point.」

Even though Gnome’s knights had yet to arrive, it still felt like there was a lot of people.

「…in that case, aren’t there too many?」

「Fufu, in the beginning, Salamander-sama’s troops were mainly the lesser noble sons.」

「Yes, and now they’ve scouted commoner Humans and Beastkin too, it seems.」

「Come to think of it, he’s here too. …that one, isn’t that Wappa?」

「Wappa-kun is amazing. Since Takumi-kun trained him, he’s much stronger than the other children here.」

I hadn’t noticed since he was in the group, but Wappa was running energetically.

Wappa wasn’t of age just yet, but perhaps because he was a Beastkin, he was growing quickly and had high physical capabilities.

Moreover, since he went through power leveling with us, his level was higher than everyone else here, and he had combat skills drilled into him.

「So Wappa’s going to join the knights.」

「He said he was going to protect his sister and the other children.」

「Ohh, then we have to cheer him on.」

I see, I thought he was still a child, but kids sure do grow fast.

As I was lost in thought watching Wappa run, someone tapped my shoulder.

「So you’re back.」

「Ah, Dante-san.」

「As you can see, their numbers have increased quite a bit.」

「Indeed so.」

「So, you know what that means?」

「Eh?」

「Equipment, please.」

「…yes.」

It seems we’ll have to make a large amount of armor and weapons from now on.

++++
